#/ /bhu su ku'i rnal 'byor pa 'bru'i sngags 'chang bsod nams chos 'phel gyis rgyal khams bskor ba'i rtogs brjod kyi phreng ba bzhad gad chen mo bzhugs/ /

/ /na mo gu ru buddha bo dhi satwa maNDa le bhyaH mkhyen rab chu gter gting mtha' zab yangs par/ /brtse ba'i mnga' bdag rgyud sde'i bcud kyis myos/ /nus pa'i dbang phyug skye
rgu'i gtsug gi rgyan/ /mtshungs med 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /blo chen rgyal ba ma lus 'dus pa'i dngos/ /snying po'i don kun gsal mdzad tshar pa rje/ /grangs
med gdul bya rgya mtsho'i mgon gcig pu/ /yongs 'dzin bla mas rtag tu byin gyis rlobs/ /'brel tshad don ldan padma'i sras kyi mchog /bka' gter gsar rnying dam chos du ma'i
mdzod/ /bod yul mun pa'i ljongs 'dir bstan pa yi/ /rgyal mtshan phyogs mthar bsgreng ba khyod la 'dud/ /rgyud sde'i bang mdzod rje btsun byang gling pa/ /mkhas btsun
bzang po'i khyu mchog grags thogs pa/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams dpal 'byor zhabs/ /'dren mchog dam pa gsum la

skyabs su mchi/ /rig gnas mthar phyin dge 'dun nyi ma dang / /'khrul med brgyud pa'i mnga' bdag e waM pa/ /yongs grags 'jam mgon bla ma nag po pa/ /'dzam gling bla ma gsum
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rmad byung thugs rje'i tsha zer gzi 'od 'bum/ /'gro kun mi shes ldongs pa'i sgrib las grol/ /rgya bod brgyud pa'i bla ma'i tshogs rnams la/ /sgo gsum
gus pas rtag tu phyag bgyid do/ /rgyud kun rtsa ba smin byed dbang bzhi'i lam/ /tshe gcig 'bras bu sngon du byed pa'i mchog /thabs mkhas dbang du brjod mdzad bla ma'i tshogs/
/'bad pas byang chub bar du 'dud do skyongs/ /he ru ka dpal bdag med lha mo'i tshogs/ /bde chen khro chags phag mos yongs 'khyud gsum/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs dang mi bskyod
rdo rje sogs/ /lhag pa'i lha mchog tshogs rnams snying dbus bzhugs/ /lhag pa'i lha mchog rab khros khro bo'i gar/ /dran pas snying gi gdung sel 'jam dpal dbyangs/ /rmad
byung dngos grub myur stsol yang

phur zhes/ /lhag pa'i lha tshogs khyod kyis ring du skyongs/ /yi dam tshogs kun khros pa'i mkha' dbyings las/ /rmad byung mthu stobs zer 'phreng bye ba brgyas/ /bdud dpung
mun pa mthar byed srung ma'i tshogs/ /bstan srung nyin mo'i mgon gyis ma gtong zhig /mdor na rtsa brgyud bla ma dkon mchog gsum/ /rab 'byams rgyal ba yi dam mkha' 'gror bcas/
/bstan srung nor lha gter bdag skyabs gnas rnams/ /dus kun byang chub bar du phyag 'tshal te/ /skyabs gnas sngon byon du ma'i rjes zhugs nas/ /sprang po'i rtogs brjod
sgro bkur spangs pa'i gtam/ /dad ldan gus pa'i zhal ngo ma bzlog par/ /ngal mdzem spangs te cung zad bri bar bgyid/ /bdag skyon sa chen rdul ltar yon tan ni/ /nyin mo'i
skar ma tsam du zad mod kyang / /skyon rnams rkun po'i nor bzhin rab sbas nas/ /yon tan gang yod lhug par bri bar bgyi/ /grub par gyur cig /de la gtsang stod g.yas ru myug
gi rgyal khab tu skye ba blangs nas yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po dang / ches mchog tu sku drin che ba'i dbang por gyur pa'i rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i dbang po yab sras gsum
gyi sku drin las rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che la mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang yid ches pa'i mthus/ ris med pa'i chos kyi rgya mtsho chen por 'jug pa'i sprang rgan rig pa
'dzin pa bsod nams chos 'phel zhes bgyi ba bdag gis lo bcu lon pa na grub pa mchog gi dbang po bsod nams dpal 'byor gyi zhabs las rab tu byung ba nas bzung deng gi bar
du bla ma dam pa'i sku drin las rnyed pa'i yon tan cung zad tsam zhig dad ldan gyi zhal

ngo ma zlog bar/ 'ga' zhig gi ngor che long tsam zhig smras pa ni/ e ma ho/ kho bo me mo phag lor skyes pa nas bzung / da lta bdun cu don bdun gyi bar gyi dga' ba dang / skyo
ba dang / btang snyoms la sdod pa'i bar gyi gleng mo brjod na/ dga' bar bsam na ci bya la 'das/ skyo bar bsams na snying chu mig ngar zags/ btang snyoms la bsams na dgod
bro/ de yang res 'ga' ni rgyal khams chu bzhin du myul/ res 'ga' ni zhag zla lo sbrel nas nyal/ res 'ga' ni gzhan phan du ming btags pa'i 'di yin med pa'i zar zir dang
za 'chag kho nar lus/ da bsam rgyu ni rang dbang thob pa'i gnas shig tu rang sems las med du gcig pur gnas te/ 'chi ba'i grogs po mdza' bshes kho sgug snyam kyang/ dad ldan
gyi zhing sa la byin rlabs skyon bral gyi sa bon btab/ snying po 'bras bu don du 'gyur la re 'di ltar ro/ /sngon rabs byon pa'i skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi mdzad par/
'das ma 'ongs da ltar gyi mdzad tshul brjod du ma mchis pa zhig yod bzhin gda' ste/ bdag lta bu'i blun po la ni/ 'das ma 'ongs gnyis ni gang 'dra yin dang ci 'drar 'gyur
zhu tshod things pa ye med/ da lta'i gnas tshul/ rang gi spyod pa zhi drag ci byed thams cad kyi sngon du gyur pa 'di ka ma gtogs/ gzhan ma yi ge'i rigs su bkod rgyu ye
med/ 'on kyang gang smras kun shugs che ba dang / gang byung sba gsang med par thams cad kyi sngon du smras gtong ba bdag rang gi srol rang byung bcos su med pa yin zhing
/ don la mthar thug chos kyi blo phugs sprang la gtad yod pas/

sprang po rgyal khams myul ba'i bde sdug gi gtam smra ba'i kha sus kyang 'gegs par mi nus pas/ de brjod pa la dga' ba yod na'ang yod mi dga' ba yod na'ang yod/ blang dor dang
bral ba'i btang snyoms pa yod na'ang legs mod/ de la phyi ltar na rgyal khams kyi sprang po phyi nang gi skye bo kun gyi blun po'i ngos 'dzin rang yang de'i khur bzhes
la gnas pa'i ser gzugs/ nang ltar na sde snod gsum dang / rgyud sde gsar rnying ma lus pa'i bang mdzod/ bstan pa rin po che spyi dang bye brag rnams srid mthar rgyas par
byed pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa'i dpa' bo/ gsang ba ltar na rje btsun rdo rje 'chang rtsod dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa gnas gsar chos rje zhes grags pa/ don la 'jam pa'i dbyangs
dang gnyis su med pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs kyi padmo las skyes te/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i phyi nang gi gdams pa rgya
mtsho lta bu dang / dpal ldan sa skya pa'i rje btsun gong ma yab sras rnams kyi snyan dang zhal nas brgyud pa'i bstan pa rin po che'i yang snying nged rang dpal kha'u brag
rdzong pa'i snyan brgyud slob bshad thun mong ma yin pa'i bstan pa dri ma med pa gsang chen zab mo'i gdams pa zab pa las ches zab pa'i snyan brgyud med du mi rung ba'i
sbas don yid bzhin nor bu rnams kyi kha lo sgyur ba'i rgyal tshab/ ris med phyogs 'dzin dang bral ba'i a wa dhU tI' pa'i btsun pa bhu su ku'i ngo mtshar gyi gtam gleng
ba la gsum ste/ rigs rus cho 'brang dang ldan pa'i sgo nas chos sku skye ba med pa la skye ba'i cho 'phrul bstan tshul/ 'khor ba 'di tsher dong du nyal ba ltar gang du'ang
bde ba'i go skabs mi 'dug

pa nas/ thar pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa rgyal ba'i bstan pa la rab tu byung tshul/ bstan pa rin po che la thos bsam sgom gsum gyi sgo nas srid mthar rgyas par byas tshul lo/
/dang po rang gi yong khyer 'di ga las med kyang gong ma tsho'i zhabs 'dren du 'gro ba las mi 'dug na'ang / thog mar rigs yod tsam brjod pa kun gyi bya srol la 'dug pas/
de yang bdag tsho bstan pa snga dar gyi dus/ bod kyi rus tshan mi'u gdung drug gi dmu las gyes pa'i 'bru zhes pa las chad/ khams su chags te rigs brgyud spel ba re dang
/ gzhan gtso cher sgrub pa snying por lhur byed pa 'ba' zhig byung 'dug /de nas re zhig na chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i phyag phyir 'brangs nas bod la byon/
'phags pa rin po che'i nang blon la nye ba zhig byung / lugs gnyis kyi mkhyen rab mkha' dang mnyam pa zhig byung 'dug pas/ 'phags pa'i dngul gyi dam kha dang / 'bru lung
pa tshang ma 'jags so gnang / dgon kha bzhi sogs 'debs pa mdzad/ de nas 'jig rten gyi thugs 'gel sras sku mched gsum byung ba'i chung ba la gnang / gzhan gnyis la dgon pa
rnams phog ste 'khor slob rnams la sgrub pa snying por byed dgos tshul gyi bslab bya gnang / khong rang 'di snang gi bya ba ngan pa thams cad bzhi mdo'i rtswa ltar dor/
byang gi gnam mtsho phyug mo'i do ri se mo bya ba kha yar yod pa'i dbus mar zas ngan ngon tsam la brten lo brgyad sgrub pa kho na la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ spyir srid pa bde
'gro dang gsung gleng mdzad cing / bla ma 'dod lha dang bcas pa zhal mngon sum du gzigs

khyad par dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams dbang phyug ma nyid kyis/ khyod kyi mi brgyud chos brgyud dang bcas pa'i srung ma ngas byed do/ /zhes zhal gyis bzhes 'dug pa nas/ da
lta bdag lta bu'i rjes su 'brangs nas lugs gnyis kyi dpal rgyun gong 'phel du rgyas pa'i 'phrin las yang dag mdzad pa 'di yin/ de nas slar 'bru dgon par phebs 'ja' lus rdo
rje'i sku brnyes nas phung po lhag ma med pa'i chos kyi sku skye ba de nyid la brnyes so/ /de'i rjes su sku mched tshang mas sgrub pa kho na lhur mdzad/ de'i nang nas kyang
sku che bas rgyal khang rang du sku rim phug pa kho na mdzad/ 'bru dgon pa nas zhabs sa la ma reg par bya ltar yar phebs mar phebs gnang / thang cig tsam na chos sdings
dgon pa'i la kha de na pha bong chen po zhig 'dug pa de byis pa rnams kyis yur ba'i 'dam la rtsed mo byas pa ltar brdzis nas da lta'i bar du yang zhabs rjes legs dod
kyi dpe thub pa 'jog pa gnang 'dug pa dang / des mtshon pa'i grub pa'i mtshan ma bsam pa'i ra ba las 'das/ gzhan yang rgyal khang gi mgon khang / chos rgyal 'phags pa nas
bzung dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rim pas ye shes pa yang yang du spyan drangs pa'i me tog gi char bab pa'i mgon khang du rgyun gyi thugs dam bskang gso sogs la
bzhugs skabs/ rgyal mkhar rtse nas dmag dpung stobs shin tu che bas rgyal khang yang 'chor la nye bar thug /gzhan rang phyogs nas thabs byed mi ni ci yang med/ mgon khang
nas rje nyid kyi thugs dam mtshan ltas sogs kyis dgongs/ dmag bzlog la dmigs pa'i gtor

ma zhig 'phang ba gnang 'dug pas/ rdo rje chos skyong rnams kyi mthu stobs nus pa gcig tu dril ba'i gnam lcags thog gi 'phang gtor zur brgyad pa de nyid/ 'byung bzhi sogs gang
la'ang ltos pa gang la yod/ rdo rje pha lam lta bu yang rdul du rlog pa'i nus pas/ gzhan rnga sil sogs kyi ban ling yang gang la dgos su 'dug /ting nge 'dzin rdo rje
lta bu kho na'i ngang nas rtag gtor de mgon khang gi skar khung la gtad de 'phangs pas/ pha tshad de na brag rol pha bong sral le yod ba de'i gseb tu thogs med du thim nas
da lta'i bar du'ang brag de la gtor ma'i shul gsal po kun gyis gzigs par yod cing / pha rol gyi dmag dpung de nyid rang phyogs nas sor rdo chung ngu gcig 'debs mkhan med
par/ mtshan sgang de nyid la gar thegs med par song nas yul phyogs de nyid bde zhing skyid pa'i nyi ma shar ba yin te/ dam pa 'di kho na'i sku drin du 'khum mo/ /rdo rje
thog chen phyi rol gzugs su shar/ /grub pa'i nus pa gnam lcags me dpung bzhin/ /bden pas ting 'dzin mthu yis gzi 'od kyis/ /btson rar chud pa'i skye bo phal cher spar/
/de nas thog gnyis tsam song 'dug ste/ de rnams kyis kyang sgrub pa kho na lhur len zhing nyan bshad sgom pa sogs du ma nas ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa rab 'byams shig 'dug
ste yi ges 'jigs pa dang kun gyi rna bar mi 'dzul bas re zhig zom me bzhag /de'i rjes su shangs kyi dpal sna nang so'i sras mo khab tu bzhes pa gnang ba'i sras su bdag gi
pha de nyid sku 'khrungs/ 'di ni byis pa'i dus nyid na rgan po'i

spyod pas dus 'da' zhing skye bo thams cad zil gyis gnon nus pa la sogs pa'i dpa' sgam can zhig yin la/ sku mched gsum byon pa'i che ba yin pas rab tu byung / thugs sbyong
sogs la gser mdog can du phebs/ chos rje bdud 'dul ba dang / lha dbang pa gnyis kyi sgrub tshul kho na la dgon pa gong 'og tu bzhugs pa gnang / yi dam chos skyong sogs kyi
bsnyen sgrub mtshan ma ma thob bar du gnang zhing / 'phrin las bskang bshags bskul sogs mdzad pa na mar me dang sha chen gyi spos dud dang bshug pa'i brgyangs glu sogs
gzhan rkyen la ma bltos par mngon sum du mthong ba sogs brjod du mi ldang ba byung 'dug /sku bgres pa gser mdog can du dgung lo bcu gsum pa la phebs/ sde snod gsum sogs la
sbyangs pa phul du phyin pa mdzad de skyes thob de nyid la ston grags che ba'i tshad thub pa zhig byung / shangs kyi g.yang lung pa tshang ma la ser bsrungs kyi zhal bkod
gnang bzhin par 'dug pas/ 'bru pa rang gi zhal ngo phebs phyin srung yul de la lo dgra drug gi gnod pa yong ma myong 'dug cing / skabs shig sku mched tsho sku phras pa
nas/ a ne yin pa'i btsun ma zhig gis mdzad/ de ma bzhugs pa dang gser mdog can nas thugs sbyong mdzad bzhin par dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi pa la g.yang du ser bsrung la
phebs/ phyi rol gyi lha srin sogs dregs byed thams cad zil gyis gnon nus pa zhig byung 'dug pas sdigs mdzub gtad pa'am/ dmigs rim btang ba'am/ phus btab pa tsam gyis bsrung
khongs la yong ba lta ci/ de skor gyi yul phyogs

gzhan rnams la yang lo legs kyi 'bru tshogs gong 'phel kho na byung / de skabs shangs kyi nang so g.yang chen pa'i bu mo bud med kyi skyon kun spangs pa de nyid shangs kyi
'ba' rar rab tu byung / ser bsrung la bzhugs dus/ pha mes brgyud pa'i srung ma des bdag lta bu yong ba'i rten 'brel yin nam gang ltar khong gi blo sgul/ chos rje kun dga'
rin chen pa la dad pa dang spro ba tshad med byung 'dug pas/ btsun ma des bsnyen bkur tshad med byas/ lhag par 'o skol gyi 'dren pa yang dag zhus/ slar gser mdog can la
phebs myug pa rab 'byams pa/ gnas kyi slob dpon ston pa bzang ba dang btsun pa'i tshad thub pa zhig yod pa des khyod la g.yang du khams dngas po dang skyid po e byung gsung
gin 'dug pas/ khams dngas po dang skyid po rang byung lhag par g.yang chen pa'i btsun mas 'o skol sogs kyi ster sbyin mang po byung zhus pas/ a li a li chos rje la 'o
skol 'dren don ye med do gsung byung bas/ ngo shin tu tsha ba ngo lpags da lta zhus 'gro ba snyam byed pa byung gsung / de lta bu'i mdzad pa ni kha phyir ltas rnams kyis
bsams na cir 'gyur mi shes/ nang don legs skyes ma'i bu mos/ bcom ldan 'das la ba mchog stong gi 'o skol btus nas zhus pas sku lus gser gyi bstan pa phyis pa ltar song zhes
pa dang / yang dbang bzhi'i skabs su gsang dbang gi sta gon gyi dong du yang byed pa ltar/ de dus gsang dbang zhig thob pa ka 'dra/ gang ltar nyer bzhi pa la gong du smos
pa ltar yon tan du ma dang ldan pa'i g.yang chen pa'i bu mo chos 'dzom rgyal mo zhes pa rdo rje btsun

mo'i rnam par sprul pa de nyid khab tu bzhes pa gnang ba'i sras su bdag spun gsum byung ba'i che ba bdag nyid yin pas/ skyon med rdo rje theg pa'i dal 'byor gyi lus 'di nyid
thob par gyur to/ /rdo rje'i lus bzang skyon med gru gzings 'di/ /ded dpon mkhas pa brtson 'grus lcag gis bskul/ /rab med gya gyu 'khor ba'i mtsho las sgrol/ /zag med bde
chen nor bu'i gling du phyin/ /mtha' yas tshogs gnyis dpal las 'khrungs pa'i sku/ /bgrang yas 'gro kun phan bde bskrun slad du/ /bsam yas gdul bya'i bung ba skyong ba'i
phyir/ /dpag yas nyams dga'i skyed tshal nga re skyid/ /de yang ma ma de nyid kyi dri ma med pa'i mngal du bdag bltams pa nas bzung / yum la sku lus bzhin mdog sngar bas
dang ba dang sku sngar bas yang zhing / bde ba'i tshad thub pa zhig dang / thugs dam 'jam sdud bzang gsum/ bla ma mchod chog /gtor ma brgya rtsa/ rdzogs chen gyi smon lam
stobs chen/ smon lam bzhi skor/ le bdun gsol 'debs la sogs pa'i thugs dam 'chag med mdzad pa shin tu spro zhing bogs kyang che ba gegs kyi rnam pa skad cig tsam yang med
par zla dgu ngo bcu hril rdzogs pa dang / yab kun dga' rin chen grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po nyer lnga pa'i dus me mo phag lo btsas pa yin zhing / ma ma nyid la
btsas ma thag pa'i dus ltas khyad par can mang po byung tshul bdag rang lo bcu tsam 'gro dus bka' lung gnang gin 'dug ste/ tshang ma dran par yang mi 'dug /dran tshad bris
kyang sgro bkur che bas bzhag /gang ltar btsas ma thag hri AHdang / oM oM zer ba

dang / hU~M la sogs pas rang babs su 'dren pa zhig byung 'dug /byis pa gso bla zhing skyed che ba g.yur rdzi zhing gang gi yang 'tshe ba dang bral ba zhig byung 'dug /de nas
cher skyes lo yang drug tsam lon 'bri klog sogs lnga drug dus thebs ma chag tsam 'di shes pa yin/ bdun pa'i dus drin khyer thabs med pa'i ma ma de nyid kyis zhal span gnang
/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gong ma rnams kyi bstod pa yongs grags 'di rnams dang gzhan gong bstod kha yar dang 'jam sdud/ smon lam bzhi skor/ sher snying / phyag 'tshal
nyer gcig sgrol gsol dang bcas pa kha yar la sbyangs pa byas/ ming lhun grub tshe brtan rdo rje zer bas/ chos rje tshe brtan rdo rje'i drung zhes mi rnams kyis yang 'bod/
nga rang yang de ga'i khur bzhes byed/ bla tshul zhig de dus nas byed pa'i rtsis byed/ byis pa yin kyang bdag bla ma yin zer dang dod byed pa zhig yod/ mgon po'i bskang
ba nag po mchod rten/ bstod 'bum rnying ma rnams dang / kun rig /tshe dpag med lha dgu'i cho ga /rab gnas don gsal sogs bla chung la dgos pa'i chog sgrigs lag len sogs
tshig don phra rags kun la sbyangs pa byas lag len byas pas skye ba mang po nas sbyangs pa yin pa 'dra zer mi byung gzhan lag len mdzad pa 'dra mthong bas a ma a ma snyam
pa mang po gda'/ lo bcur slebs nas da bdag nyid rab tu byung ste tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa zhig byed pas gnang 'tshal zhus pas/ yab yum gnyis kyis yang gnang / de lo byed
pa'i rtsis byas kyang bdud dbang 'dras khyer cung ma grub bo/ /rgyal ba'i bstan la lhag bsam dad mod kyang / /snyigs dus bdud

dbang ches pas lo ru 'gyangs/ /'on kyang 'khrul med 'khon ston sa skya pa'i/ /rjes su 'jug 'dod dal 'byor lus 'di rnyed/ /gnyis pa rgyal ba'i bstan pa la rab tu byung tshul
la gsum ste/ so so thar pa'i sgor zhugs te sde snod gsum la sbyangs tshul/ rdo rje theg pa spyi dang bye brag gi rgyud sde mtha' dag la nyan bshad sgom sgrub byas tshul/
byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas ma gyur 'gro ba'i don rab 'byams bsgrubs tshul lo/ /dang po bcu gcig pa la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dpal 'byor zhes btsun pa dang grub pa mchog
gi dbang po/ chos brgyad 'dir snang gi nyes pas nam yang gos ma myong ba'i dpa' bo de nyid kyi drung du lam log pa las khyad par du bya ba sangs rgyas la skyabs su 'gro
ba'i thog mar dge bsnyen gyi brtul zhugs nos/ de nas bshad pa'i rtsa bzhi la sogs pa'i bsrung sdom phra zhing phra ba kun la spangs blangs ngo lkog med par byas/ dam
pa de'i gsung nas lung bstan lta bur dgos/ khyed bsod nams chen po yod chos tshul zin la sgrub pa 'phel ba gyis/ bstan pa la phyogs 'dzin ma mdzad gang mos la nyams len mdzod/
sngags pa yin pas sgrub pa mthar phyin pa'i sngags 'dren dgos gsungs nas/ ming bsod nams chos 'phel gyis gsungs/ mdor na mkhar mthon po'i ba gam 'dogs pa'i thog mar
gnas de'i 'gram gzhi 'bru ba bzhin du rtsa ba'i gzhi 'di legs par bcas pa'o/ /des mdzad pa'i tshe dpag med grub rgyal lugs kyi dbang chog /sman bla'i mdo chog /bsngo ba
sogs bla chung la dgos pa'i slob gnyer phran bu byas/ bcu gnyis pa phyag khyer thal rtsed kho nas

g.yengs/ bcu gsum pa la gang la'ang 'jigs pa med pa'i ham can zhig yin pas/ rin spungs nas karma pa mi bskyod rdo rje spyan drangs myug tu phebs/ rgyal khang la phreng sdem
gcig rim gnyis rim yod pa'ang ma 'dzems par thal mar phyin seng sbubs kyi logs shig tu bsdad pas 'brel tshad don ldan de dang sbyin bdag des gtsos pa'i dpon che chung sogs
kyi 'bras bu don ldan du 'gyur la re brgya 'bul sogs bsnyen bkur mang po gda'/ khong tsho'i lto za ba'i cha rkyen du 'phral gyi snyan brjod tsam la mkha' 'gro'i dbu skra'am
seng sbu las grub pa yin zer ba'i zhwa de brgya 'bul re la yud tsam bzhes pa thang bcu gsum mthong / de mthong grol yin zer ba dang mi bskyod rdo rje de nyid skyes
chen tshad mar grub pa yin pas ma dad cing ma gus pa ci yang ma byas/ gang ltar zhwa de mthong grol yin na bdag kyang lan bcu gsum grol rigs par gda' ste/ rang nyid dug gsum
gyi bag chags ches pas lan nam snyam/ de nas 'phags pa rin po che nas bzung yongs 'dzin du mas bdag gir mdzad cing zhabs kyis bcags pa dang / bstan pa snga dar gyi gtsug
lag lcog ro klu sbubs kyi lha khang / myug chos sde'i bla mar bkod pa'i bka' lung phebs/ na so dang shes yong ci yang med pas lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas chos sde mi zin tshul
nan gyis zhus kyang ma grol/ yab yum gyi bka' yang phebs pa dang bstun/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dpal 'byor gyi sku drin las/ dge bsnyen gyi brtul zhugs 'chang ba'i rdo
rje 'dzin par khas blangs/ yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi zhabs stegs seng ge'i khri la 'khod/

lugs gnyis kyi phra rags ci grub byas byis pa ham can zhig bdog pas gang yong ba shog snyam pa'i thag chod 'di ga gdong 'ded byed pa ma gtogs chos brgyad dang 'brel ba'i legs
legs de tsam nas mi shes pa lags so/ /snga dar bstan pa'i me ro gnas pa'i sa/ /skyes chen du mas byin rlabs seng khri la/ /byis pa 'jigs med lo ni bcu gsum pa/ /lugs gnyis
khrims kyi rgyal pos bka' stsal bskos/ /dge mtshan du ma 'byung ba'i rten 'brel bsgrigs/ /sku drin dran kyang khyer ba'i thabs ma mchis/ /'brel tshad mthong bas grol
ba'i karma pa/ /'khrul zad slu med skyabs mgon khyod gcig po/ /las bde sdug 'khor lo rgyun bskor 'di/ /khyed ye shes ral gris myur du chod/ /rta gos sbyin bdag gis bteg
pa'i bla gzugs kyi zol zog /'khor mang 'dus pa yi dbus na ches mtho yi mu cor/ /lan brgyar yang yang du sgrog pa mgal bsdum gyi gad brgyangs/ /lad mo 'di la phyogs bcur bzhugs
pa'i rgyal ba sras bcas khrel min nam/ /'jam dbyangs dpa' bo bsod nams dpal 'byor zhabs/ /khyod kyi drin las log pa'i lam las thar/ /lam gyi rtsa ba dge bsnyen sdom
pas phyug /bdag gi de ring rin chen nor bu rnyed/ /de nas bcu bzhi pa nas bzung bcu bdun gyi bar gdan sa'i khur byas bsdad/ drin gyis lan brgyar bskyangs pa'i pha ma yab
yum gyi zhabs tog lhod med byed rtsis byas/ 'on kyang sre ba se ba cung zad kyang byung ngo / /bco brgyad pa la bdag tsho rang gi sbyin bdag yin pa'i sgo mdun 'og pa zhes
pa'i zhal ngo zhig rab tu byung / de nyid bzod pa'i gos dang tshul

khrims kyi rgyan gyis rnam par mdzes pa mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i bang mdzod rdo rje 'dzin pa'i mnga' bdag chen po de nyid kyi stag lung sna dkar gyi mkhan po gnang / mtshan paN
chen grags pa thogs med ces pa'i zhabs drung du bdag gis sleb/ gzhi sngon ma'i steng du/ gnyis pa dge tshul gyi bslab pa 'dul ba nas gsungs pa'i gsol bzhi'i cho ga'i sgo
nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa thob/ de nas gsungs pa'i rags rdog bcu sogs bsrung sdom phra zhing phra ba rnams la nyes bcas phra mo tsam gyis ma gos shing theg chen gyi byang
chub sems dpar byas/ gnas der dam pa de'i drung du lo gsum bsdad/ dbu ma rtsa 'grel/ karma sha tam/ mngon pa rtsa 'grel/ bshad mdzod chen mo/ /phar phyin rtsa 'grel/ byams
chos sde lnga/ bstan pa rin po che lhag ma ma lus pa'i phung po bstan bcos sdom gsum rab dbye la sogs pa phal cher blo la zin/ tshig rkyang ma lus pa zin yang zin/ go
don mtha' gcod pa rnams dam pa de'i gsung zer phra mo 'dzin blo byas kyang / dpag par dka' ba'i gsung gi zur tsam yin te nam mkha'i khams las byis pa'i 'dom gyis gzhal
ba dang mtshungs so/ /mdor na pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhung lugs la thos bsam sbyang ba byas blo kha yang spro snyam pa byung / de nas nyer gsum pa la shangs rnam gling du
dam pa de'i zhabs phyir phyin/ sangs rgyas bstan pa'i spyi'i sbyin bdag rin spungs nas kyis zhal bkod gnang / dgon gsar zhig 'debs pa mdzad pa'i gnas ming la thub bstan
gser mdog lhun por gsol/ der lo gsum sde snod kyi bshad gra thag chod pa zhig

byung / dgon pa de gnyis su dam pa de nyid kyi sku drin la pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhung lugs la thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs phal cher chod/ nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal mchog rab
las mtho ba su'i rtsar yang dpa' zhum mi dgos tsam zhig bdog /da lta ni dgon pa de la lugs gnyis khrims kyi bya bas bor ba'i karma dgon gsar zhes grag go /de nas dam pa
de nyid chos grwa chen po gser mdog can du shangs pa gra tshang gi slob dpon la phebs/ zhabs phyir bdag gis kyang phyin/ lo lnga tsam bsdad/ po ti phyi ma rnams la sbyangs
pa mthar phyin pa byas/ dge 'dun brgya phrag bdun tsam gyi dbus su skyes thob de nyid la ston grags che ba'i tshad thub pa zhig byung ngo / /mtha' yas srid mtsho'i sdug
bsngal skyob pa'i phyir/ /rig grol ldan pa brgya phrag bdun gyi khrod/ /phar tshad 'dul sde la sogs sbyang tshul byas/ /nor mchog byang sems sdom pas rgyud las phyug /mkhas
pa'i dbang po grags pa thogs med zhabs/ /bcu phrag gcig dang bse ru lo grangs bsten/ /khyod kyi drin las phung khams nyon mongs lcags/ /gser 'gyur rtsi yi rin chen rol
par bsgyur/ /dal 'byor don yod yin snyam mi mtsher gda'/ /de nas gsum pa dge slong ni nyer brgyad pa la paN chen chos kyi rgyal po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i
blo'i zhabs khri la mngon par mtho ba'i gdan sa brgyad pa 'bum rab 'byams pa don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos te/ gnas brtan 'dul ba 'dzin pa dge 'dun nyi ma bstan pa'i rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang pos mkhan po dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po grags pa thogs med kyis las slob

'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po don yod rdo rjes gsang ston dang grib tshod kha skong sogs dge 'dun bcu phrag gcig gi dbus su bkra shis pa'i gtsug lag khang dpal ldan bkra shis brtsegs
par bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po thob/ de nas gsungs pa'i srung sdom nyis brgya lnga bcu sogs la mig gi 'bras bu'am/ khog pa'i snying khrag ltar gces
pa bsrungs/ nyes bcas cung zad tsam gyis ma gos par gnod ba med pas/ dkon mchog zhabs drung du mi mtsher tsam 'di yin/ de nas mdo phyogs kyi slob gnyer yang zur gyis bzhag
/sngar sbyangs rnams yid la gcags nas 'phral du 'bel gtam byed dgos byung yang / mkhas pa'i snyan grags 'brug stong ldir ba ltar yod pa rnams kyi rtsar dpa' zhum mi dgos
tsam 'di yin/ 'on kyang 'phral gyi 'bel gtam gleng mo tsam las pham pa bzhi dang bcas pa'i bslab pa la skyon gyur byung na mi rung snyam spam me ba byas/ gang ltar sum
ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa'i dngos po rgyud la ldan pas bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi dge bshes su byas so/ /'khor ba'i khyim kun bzhi mdo'i rtswa ltar rgyab tu bor nas sras bcas
rgyal ba'i yon tan rjes su dran/ /dran pa'i mod la shAkya'i bstan la rab zhugs bslab gsum skyon med tshul khrims rgyan gyis mdzes/ /mdzes shing mdo rgyud dri med ma lus kun
gyis gser snod gdams ngag nor bu'i dpal gyis gang / /gang yang paN grub du ma'i zhal bcud ngoms pa med par bod yul 'gyur ba'i dam chos ma lus legs par spro/ /legs tshogs
ma 'dres phyi nang rten 'brel kun/ /thog mar

'dzoms pa grags pa thogs med kyi/ /drin las ma nor sku bzhi'i rgyal srid che/ /bdag nyid bsod nams bgo skal ldan pas thob/ /'dul 'dzin dam pa dge 'dun nyi ma yi/ /zhabs pad
dri med dge slong sdom pa la/ /nyis brgya lnga bcu'i spang bya de bor ba/ /dri ma kun dang bral ba'i lam gzhi yin/ /gnyis pa rdo rje theg pa spyi dang bye brag gi las la
nyan bshad sgom sgrub byas tshul la brgyad de/ yongs 'dzin dam pa bcu phrag gsum dang zung gnyis bsten tshul/ phung khams skye mched ma smin pa smin par byed pa'i yi dam
chos skyong mkha' 'gro nor lha dang bcas pa'i dbang lung rjes gnang gi chu bo nos tshul/ bskyed rdzogs zung 'jug gi nyams len gzhi lam 'bras gsum gtan la 'bebs pa'i 'khrid
tshul rgya mtsho ltar nos nas bsnyen sgrub las/ mtha' sbyin sreg gis bskang ste lhag pa'i lha mchog du ma'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi mtshan ma mngon du gyur pa'i grub
pa'i mtshan ma shar tshul/ 'gro ba lha mir bcas pa'i phyag dang mchod pa smon lam gyi rten du sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs tshul/ mgon med srid mtshor 'khyams pa'i nyam
thag gi 'gro ba mtha' dag gi don rtse gcig tu byas tshul/ brkam chags can gyi rtag 'dzin mtha' dag bzlog pa dang tshe sgrub kyi mchog gyur sbyin pa'i phar phyin bskyangs
tshul/ bstan pa rin po che spyi dang bye brag srid mtha'i bar du rgyas par mdzad pa'i bshes gnyen gyi tshogs bskrun tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ rtsod dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis
pa gangs can ljongs su rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i mnga' bdag mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan

pa'i rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs kyi 'phrin las kyi kha lo pa mkhas pa dang grub pa rig pa 'dzin pa du ma'i khri la zhabs
kyi padma ngal gso ba'i tshar chen rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mdo sngags rgyud sde gsar rnying gi bka' srol chu bo'i rgyun bzhin mi 'chad par sgrog pa'i sngags
'chang ayon sku dngos mnga' ris rigs 'dzin chen po/ dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i rigs bdag mkhas btsun grub pa'i dpa' bo byang gling 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin po che/ mdo sngags
rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son cing tshul khrims kyi phung pos rgyud yongs su mdzes pa 'phags nor bdun gyis phyug pa'i dge 'dun nyi ma/ bsams bzhin du snyigs dus kyi 'gro ba
rnams 'dul ba'i ched du byon pa nag po spyod pa'i sku'i skye ba 'jam mgon bla ma dam pa/ rgyal ba thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje 'chang gi gdan sa bdun pa bla ma gsum gyi
thugs kyi sras mchog ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ rigs gnas mthar phyin 'dul 'dzin kun gyi gtsug rgyan paN grub grags pa thogs med/ grub pa yongs kyi 'khor lo sgyur ba'i
dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dpal 'byor/ brtul zhugs kyi sgo nas phyi nang gi mi dang mi min kun la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes pa'i dbang phyug dam pa ngor chen
dkon mchog dpal ldan/ dri med 'khon gyi rigs su sku 'khrungs nas snyigs dus kyi dmu rgod ma rungs pa'i 'gro mgon bdag chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ gzhal du med pa'i yon
tan rin po che'i phung po la dbang 'byor ba'i mkhas btsun

don yod rdo rje/ mdo rgyud rgya mtsho lta bu'i pha rol tu son pa'i rig 'dzin grub mchog kun dga' mchog ldan/ shes bya'i mkha' la mkhyen rab kyi gzi 'od 'bum phrag 'gyed par
nus pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'dar skyid gshongs pa blo gros rnam rgyal/ /'jam dpal gshin rjes rjes su bzung ba'i brag dkar chu bzang pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ grub thob
thang stong rgyal po'i gdung gso ba bstan 'dzin nyi ma bzang po/ rgyal ba gnyis pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi rgyal tshab bo dong mkhan rin po che bslab gsum dbang phyug
/bka' brgyud bstan pa'i sgron me 'brug pa gcung rin po che/ 'khrul zhig grub pa'i dbang po ra sa 'dzin gyi gdan sa pa bstan pa bzang po/ lung rigs rgya mtsho'i mthar son
zhing nyan grol gyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mnga' bdag rong pa dge slong chos bzang po/ sngags 'chang grub pa'i mnga' bdag zhabs drung mkhyen brtse'i drung gi
khu bo rje nam mkha' rgyal ba/ shangs ri bo bde chen ba bla ma rnal 'byor pa/ myug pa chos rje sbrum phu ba/ gzhan yang chung ngu'i dus bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / tshe dbang
dang / byin rlabs zab mo 'dra thob pa'i bla ma bdun dang bcas bsten nas mdo rgyud bstan bcos sogs gsang sngags gsar rnying bod yul du 'gyur ro cog gi dam chos mtha' dag
la phyi nang gi sgro 'dogs legs par chod pa'o/ /skyes chen rnams kyi tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho la/ /blo mig ldong yang bdud rtsi'i chu thigs 'thung / /nyams myong rlan
gyis sbyar ba'i 'bras bu smin/ /skal bzang snyan brgyud bdud rtsi 'thung 'dod rnams/ /rings par

tshur shog chos kyi bgo skal long / /rtogs 'dod don gnyer rtog ge'i rig pa sbyong / /pho sgrob phyogs lhung de rnams gnyid byos shig /gnyis pa phung khams skye mched ma smin
pa smin par byed pa'i dbang lung rjes gnang thob tshul la gnyis te/ sngags gsar ma dang rnying ma'o/ /dang po la/ rnam grangs kyi sgo nas brjod na/ bstan pa rin po che'i
lus yongs su rdzogs pa dpal ldan sa skya pa nas brgyud pa dang / byang chub sems kyi rlan gyis 'gro rgyun thar lam du khrid par mdzad pa jo bo dpal ldan a ti sha nas brgyud
pa dang / sgrub brgyud chu bo'i rgyun ltar las 'ongs pa mar pa mi la nas brgyud pa dang / 'od gsal chos sku'i dbyings las gzugs sku thig ler bzhengs pa mkhas grub khyung
po nas brgyud pa dang / rje btsun dbyangs can lha mos rjes su bskyangs pa'i paN chen bo dong pa nas brgyud pa dang / rgyal ba'i lung bstan karma rabs bdun nas brgyud
pa'i dbang dang / gnyis pa la yang bka' ma dang gter ma gnyis yod pa las/ de rnams la'ang pha rgyud ma rgyud gnyis med rgyud de/ rgyud sde 'og ma sogs bsam gyis mi khyab
pa 'dug pa rnams so sor bkod na mangs pas 'jigs te 'dir rtogs sla ba'i phyir phyogs gcig tu brjod na/ rang lo rtsa dgu pa nas lo bzhi'i bar chos gra de nyid du dam pa gnyis
kyi drung dang myug sogs su dge sbyor gang 'phel dang snang zos gang bde byas bsdad/ rang lo so gsum pa lug lo zla ba bzhi pa'i gnam gang la drin khyer thabs ma mchis
pa'i paN chen chos kyi rgyal po grags pa thogs

med chos dbyings su gzims/ rgyal ba'i zhing khams su chos kyi nyi ma med pas gdul bya'i tshogs mun rum du gyur to/ /'on kyang ye shes kyi zer la rgyun 'chad med pas gsol ba
'debs pa dga' ba snyam/ lag yod kyi rab byung chas nas bzung bdog bcas kyi dngos po thams cad dus gcig tu spungs nas kun tu bzang po'i mchod sprin ltar byas te/ dge 'dun
tshogs pa la phul mang ja dang / rna dkar du gdung mchod pa rnams la ja sbrel sogs gang bstab kyi gsol ba btab/ de nas dam pa nyid ma bzhugs pa dang gang la'ang snying po
mi 'dug pa nas sgrub pa snying por byed snyam myug la log /de lo zhabs drung mkhyen brtse'i drung dpal zha lu gser bkang gi gdan sar phebs/ de nas yab sras lhan cig tu
myug la phebs pa'i bsu ba ser sbrengs dpag tu med pas spyan drangs pa'i phyag phyir phyin/ de snga yan du thos pa'i dbang lung rjes gnang sogs kyang so sor thob skabs dang
bstun nas bkod na mangs pas 'jigs nas 'dir phyogs gcig tu brjod pa la/ de lo dpal sbug rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod du/ zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga la gsung ngag rin
po che 'dzugs pa gnang / zhabs drung mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gis dbu mdzad bdag lta bus tha shal byas pa'i skal ba bzang po'i mched po bco brgyad kyis zla ba bdun gyi
bar la gnad du dril nas zhus pa'i thog mar/ snang ba gsum gyi 'khrid/ de grol ma thag maNDal tshom bu lnga pa la brten pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa/ brgyud pa gnyis
ldan gyi phyag len cig tu byas pa/ de rjes slob ma rjes 'dzin/ kye rdo rje man ngag lugs kyi rgyu dus

kyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang chu chen mo las bshad pa ltar slob ma dbang bskur ba'i dbang stegs thun mong ma yin pa slob bshad kyi dbang / bar du lam gyi dbang /
tha ma 'bras bu la mtshams sbyor ba'i dbang ste yab bka' dang / rdo rje bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du rgyu dus kyi dbang / gsang dbang gi lam
bdag byin rlabs kyi 'khrid kyi thog mar nang gi bdag med ma gtum mo'i drod bskyed pa'i slad du bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor chen po byin rlabs kyi
brgyud pa ma nyams pa ste yum bka' dang / lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi 'khrid phyi nang gi byin rlabs/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi byin rlabs thun mong dang thun mong
ma yin pa/ brda ston gsal ba'i byin rlabs/ bla ma rin 'byung gi byin rlabs/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi byin rlabs dang / de dag gi rgyab
rten zab cing rgya che ba rgya bod kyi rgyud rgya gzhung bstan bcos rnams kyi lung / tshad ma rnam bzhi'i skabs so sor thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa/ bod yul gyi mkhas
pa dang grub pa'i skyes chen rnams kyi bzhed lugs tha dad du/ glegs bam che 'bring chung gsum bcu gnyis kyi lung brgyud pa 'di dang 'di nas brgyud sogs thob cing / 'di
thos phyin lam zab zab gzhan la yid smon med pa'i bzhed cig gda'/ de nas rang lo so bzhi pa nas bzung dus gsum gyi rgyal ba kun gyi spyi mes gsang chen dam pa chos kyi 'byung
gnas mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i glegs bam rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bstan pa'i rgyal

mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs drung du kye rdo rje bka' babs rnam pa bzhi'i dbang / rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' 'grel chen ku mu tas gtsos pa'i yi ge mang po'i lung / rdzong lugs
kyi gur rigs bsdus man ngag lugs kyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa dang bcas pa thob cing nyams su myong ba'o/ /de nas rang lo so lnga pa la paN grub chen po a bha yas
bkral ba'i sta gon gcig gis chog pa'i dbang gi grangs zhe gnyis dang kr-i ya sa munytsa nas kha bskang ste dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum ste rdo rje 'phreng ba
rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi bcu zhe lnga tshig don lag len dang bcas pa/ bde mchog lo nag dril gsum rdul mtshon la brten pa'i dbang / bde mchog dkar po'i byin
rlabs/ bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sbyangs pa'i yon tan/ sdom pa 'byung ba/ mai tri bcu gsum ma ste yab bka' dang / phag mo so bdun ma/ bcu gsum ma/ dgu ma ste yum
bka' dang / dpyal a mo ghas mdzad pa'i byin rlabs sgrub thabs sogs yi ge mang po'i lung / nag po gzhung drug /bsdu ba gsum pa/ sman lngar grags pa/ sa skya pa'i nag 'bum
dang bcas pa'i rgya bod kyi yi ge mtha' yas pa'i lung / gsang sngags rgyud sde mtha' dag gi yang snying ches shin tu zab pa/ bde chen ral pa gcig pa bcom ldan 'das dpal bde
ba chen po lha nyi shu lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang chog bsres pa'i dbang rgyas pa dang / cho ga'i lugs so sor byas pa'i dbang bzhi re re la yang dbang bzhi
sbyar ba'i rgyas pa dang / yab gtsor byas kyi ye shes 'pho ba'i byin rlabs rgyas

pa/ yum gtsor byas kyi bsdus pa/ de dag gi rgyud rgya gzhung ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i bka' srung / gshin rje kA la dang bi kA la ste gshin rje
dmar nag gi rjes gnang / de'i man ngag rgya mtsho lta bu'i lung / man ngag thams cad rdzogs pa'i mthar rdo rje slob dpon bdag po chen po'i dbang rgyas pa/ mdor na bdag
gi yongs 'dzin dam pa dpal padma rgyal po rdo rje ye shes rtsal gyis dka' ba du ma khyad du bsad de rgyal khams chu bzhin du myul nas btsal ba'i gdams pa zab mo/ /dbang po
rab 'bring tha gsum/ tshe gcig la 'tshang rgya ba'i lam zab mo 'di nyid zhal shes phra rags dang bcas te/ bdag la gcig tu gdams pa nyams su myong ba yin no/ /tshad med
slu ba med pa'i skyabs mgon des/ /chos dbyings thugs kyi bang mdzod sgo phye nas/ /mthar byed gdul bya'i re ba 'gengs pa'i phyir/ /bdud rtsi lta bu'i chos de kho bos rnyed/
/byang phyogs bod kyi yul gru gang nas kyang / /'di blug gser snod gtsang ma ma rnyed pas/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba sras bcas bzod par bzhes/ /mi smra snying nas nyams len
dag la 'bung / /gzhan yang rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i zhabs drung du rang lo so drug pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa dang / 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / spyan ras gzigs
gsum ras bris la brten pa'i dbang dang / zab cing rgya che ba'i yi ge ma tshang ba med pa'i lung / dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rA 'bro rnam pa gnyis kyi dbang rdul tshon
la brten pa byis 'jug dbang bdun/ bdag po chen po'i dbang dang bcas pa/ de'i bsdus rgyud

'grel pa dri med 'od sogs dang / rgyud de nyid kyi 'grel pa'am TI ka dpal ldan bla mas mdzad pa'i glegs bam bzhi/ sems 'grel skor gsum sogs rgya bod kyi gsung rab mang po'i
lung / gshin rje gshed kyi skor la dgra gdong 'jigs gsum la bcu gsum re re'i rdul tshon la brten pa'i dbang bzhi zab mo re dang / 'jigs byed ro langs brgyad kyis bskor ba/
dpa' bo gcig pa phyag mtshan gyis bskor ba dang / zhang skyo gnyis kyi lha bcu bdun ma dang / 'jam dpal zhi khro zhe dgu ma'i rdul tshon la brten pa'i dbang bzhi dang
/ gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma/ lnga ma/ dgu ma dang bcas pa'i dbang dang / de rnams kyi rgyud rgya gzhung bstan bcos rgya bod kyi yi ge mtha' yas pa'i lung / rgyud rgyal rtog
pa bdun pa'i 'grel pa zab mo bzhi tsam dang / 'bri gung dpal 'dzin gyi gsung rab pod kha yongs rdzogs shig dang / gzhan yang shin tu spros pa med pa'i 'od gsal 'char
ba'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi byin rlabs/ gshin rje mthar byed dmar po rnal 'byor bzhi'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi lha mo 'od 'dzin ma dkar mo'i byin rlabs/ 'khrul 'khor gyi byin

dkyil gyi steng nas rdul tshon la brten pa'i dbang dang / dpal phyag na rdo rje lha dgu'i dbang rdul tshon la

bcos mang po'i lung / 'khor lo chen po'i rtsa rgyud bshad rgyud/ de dag gi dgongs 'grel/ 'grel pa rdo rje'i myu gu sogs gsung rab ji snyed pa'i lung / gzhan yang phyag

po/ /rab 'byams rgyal ba yi dkyil 'khor/ /grangs med thos pa 'di bsams tshe/ /lan brgyar thal sbyar gyi 'dab 'phreng / /bcu gsum sa lam gyi go 'phang / /ma reg bar du rang

tshogs yi ge mang po'i lung / rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras kyi thugs dam gyi snying po dmar mo skor gsum la paN grub chen po nA ro ta pas bkral ba'i nA ro mkha' spyod

dang /

pa'i lung / rje btsun sa skya pa'i bka' srung dpal dur khrod bdag po yab yum gyi rjes gnang / bka' srung dbang po dkar bdud lcam dral gyi rjes gnang / dur khrod bdag po'i
rgyud gsang ba snying gi 'khor lo le'u brgyad pa/ paNDi ta bai ro tsa na rakShi ta las brgyud pa 'dzim lo tsA ba'i 'gyur ba sogs rgya bod kyi yig sna bcu drug gi lung

srid gi zur bka'/ bran bdud kyi rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa bka' gtad dang bcas pa/ lha brgyad/ lha dgu/ lha bcu gnyis ma rnams kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i

'jigs byed khrag 'thung dud pa'i sol ba can gyi rjes gnang thun mong dang thun mong min pa/ gsang sgrub kyi rjes gnang nan chags mar grags pa/ gyi ljang lugs mgon po bcu

ba/ /khyod kyi mchog dang thun mong sgrub pa'i lha/ /grangs med cig tu bdag la legs par gdams/ /rgya bod rgyud dang rgya gzhung bstan bcos tshogs/ /yan lag bcu gnyis la
sogs shing rta'i lam/ /bod yul 'gyur ba'i dam chos ji snyed pa/ /zas gtsang sras kyi rgyal tshab mkhyen brtse'i dbang / /'gran zla bral ba de yis bdag la stsal/ /skal bar
bzang snyam dad pa'i blo gros rgyas/ /gzhan yang grub brnyes 'dod rgur stsol ba de nyid kyi drung du rang lo bzhi bcu pa la/ chos skyong ba'i srung ma rnam thos bu zhes
grags pa'i bka' gter gsar rnying dang 'brel ba'i gdams pa du ma zhig nos pa'i thog mar gnyen po'i lha dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po'i rjes gnang / de'i rgyud rdo rje
sa 'og le'u gsum pa zang dkar gyi 'gyur sogs rgya gzhung bstan bcos sna bcu gsum/ zang dkar gyi stum ston la stod du gnang bas de nas brgyud pa'i stod lugs sam/ bya sder
lugs su grags pa'i rnam sras ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang / de'i gtam rgyud gar mkhan mchog gi brtag pa phyi ma las byung ba rnam sras

skye brgyud sogs rgyud dang rgya gzhung nyer gsum/ yon po jo ston la gnang ba'i smad lugs su grags pa'i rgyal po chen po ngal gsos po bde byed 'khor dang bcas pa dang / drag
byed klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes gnang chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i yi ge'i steng nas thob cing / man ngag snying dang 'dra ba'i gdams pa zhal shes dang bcas pa sna
so gnyis/ spos sgang pa rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i sna bcu gcig /gzhan yang skyor mo lung pa'i lugs sam phyag len ltar yang thob/ 'brom sde nyi ma'i lugs su
grags pa'i ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang / lha dgu'i sgrub thabs rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum shin tu bsdus pa sogs nor du sgrub pa yig sna brgyad/ sri'u gso ba'i yig sna bzhi
dbang sdud gsum/ nad zhi ba bgegs las rgyal ba gnyis bsad pa'i yi ge lnga/ phyir 'jug las byang / lo rgyus sogs rgyal chen gsang sgrub ljang ser be con ma'i rjes gnang
/ man ngag mgul khug sro ma can dang / dgon pa ba'i be bum se khab ma/ 'phags pa klu sgrub zhabs kyis sprang po nyi ma dngos su bsgral ba'i chos skyong rgyal po chen po rta
sngon bdud mo bzhi bskor/ nang ma mo ltar sgrub pa lha dgu'i rjes gnang / bai shra ma Na kha rag khram thogs nag pa'i rgyud le'u so lnga pa las gsungs pa'i drag byed seng
zhon klu brgyad kyis bskor ba'i rjes gnang / kha rag khram thogs nag po'i rgyud sogs tsho lnga/ gsang ba gshin rje ltar sgrub pa mdung dmar can lha bcu gsum gyi rjes
gnang / de'i sgrub thabs dang rjes gnang gi yi ge rnying pa/ rnam sras yang gsang srin po bzhi bskor gyi rjes gnang / de'i sgrub yig /shu raM ga wa rma'i

lugs kyi rnam sras mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha bco lnga'i rjes gnang / de'i sgrub thabs sogs yi ge drug las mkhan dang bcas pa'i mdung dmar can gyi rjes gnang /
de'i rjes gnang gi yi ge sgrub yig sogs/ mgon po gar mkhan mchog ljang gu/ zhal gcig phyag bco brgyad pa 'brug zhon gyi rjes gnang / rnam sras gar mkhan mchog dmar smug zhal
gsum phyag drug pa lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang / rnam sras dkar po lha dgu'i tshe dbang / de dag gi sgrub skor las tshogs dang bcas pa/ ayon chos kyi rgyal po'i gdams pa
zhang lha bzang klu dpal gyi bha dha hor bcom pa'i rnam sras zhi drag gnyis las/ rnam sras ljang ser ram sprin gseb mar grags pa'i ser chen lha dgu'i rjes gnang / man ngag
la lo rgyus sogs yig sna bcu bzhi/ drag po yang gsang mdung dmar can phyag mtshan bzhi pa gtso 'khor gyi rjes gnang / gnod sbyin dbyug to can gyi rgyud le'u bdun pa sogs
yi ge nyi shu rtsa gnyis/ yon tan rin po che 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u bcu gnyis pa sogs rgyal po kun skyong gis mdzad pa'i yi ge lnga/ rnam sras seng ge bu bdun gyi skor
la/ drag po phyi sgrub drag sngags kyi rgyud sogs yi ge lnga/ 'khor gyi skor la/ rta bdag brgyad kyi sgos sgrub sogs yi ge bcu/ gzhan yang yig sna zab mo bcu gsum/ cho
ga lag len gyi skor la/ zhi drag spel ma'i sgrub thabs sogs yi ge bcu bzhi/ tshig don lag len phyag 'khrid dang bcas pa legs par thob cing sbyangs so/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i
gdams skor ji snyed dang / /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i rgyal srid ma lus pa/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i 'phrin las khyod gcig pu/ /mkhyen dang

brtse bas bdag la bstan bsam gdams/ /khyod mnyes bgyid pa'i bya ba gzhan don dang / /bstan dang 'gro la phan pa lhur len las/ /rkyen ngan rdzu 'phrul che yang dbang mi 'chor/
/bde sdug 'byor rgud nad gdon gtses kyang rung / /ma rungs las ngan du mas mnar kyang rung / /khyod mnyes sgrub pa nam yang mi gtong bas/ /'dir snang tshe dang bsod nams
dge sbyor la/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i 'tshe las skyab tu gsol/ /nam zhig sgyu lus bor bar gyur pa na/ /sa lam bar chad ma lus zhi nas ni/ /gang du 'tshang rgyas zhing khams
der bgrod nas/ /zhal mthong gsung gi bdud rtsi 'thung bar shog /byang phyogs 'di na dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /rgyud sde bzhi sogs chos phung brgyad khri'i mtsho/ /rang
blo ngom pa lam bzang chu thigs 'thung / /gzhan yang bod yul 'gyur ba'i srung ma'i tshogs/ /dbang 'khrid rjes gnang byin rlabs ma lus pa/ /tshe rabs kun tu khyed kyis rjes
bzung nas/ /lam gyi 'khrul pa zad par byin gyis rlobs/ /mi zad 'dod rgu sbyin phyir ne'u le/ /rin chen lnga 'dus brgyud pa las byon pa'i/ /snyan grags 'byor pa'i rgyal
'bangs dbang bsdud phyir/ /rnam thos bu dang lag pa'i 'dab 'phreng sbrel/ /nam mkha'i mdzod la 'gran zla med do snyam/ /bdun ldan nor la dbang sgyur rin chen sems/ /mdza'
med dbrog tu med pa'i bzhad cig gda'/ /dga' dga' 'dra na kun kyang 'di ltar mdzod/ /mi dga' na ni sdug rtsir phung rtsir mdzod/ /gzhan yang yongs 'dzin dam pa byang gling
rin po che/ /paN chen grags pa thogs med/ grub mchog bsod nams dpal 'byor/ 'dul 'dzin dge 'dun nyi ma/

ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ ngor chen dkon mchog dpal ldan/ bdag chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun kun dga' mchog ldan/ rgyal tshab bslab gsum dbang phyug rnams la
kye rdo rje'i rgyu lam gyi dbang / rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dbang / tshe dpag med lha dgu /mgon po lcam dral/ mkha' 'gro lha brgyad/ 'chi med rnga sgra/ sa phur/ kun rig /rdo
dbyings/ dpal rtse gnyis/ byin rlabs thugs dbang / phyag na rdo rje 'byung 'dul/ tshe dbang sogs de rnams kyi 'phral dgos kyi yig cha so so'i lung dang bcas pa/ de thams
cad kyang tshig dang don du bsdebs nas lag len tshun brgyud pa 'di dang 'di nas brgyud sogs ma 'khrul ba byas/ gzhan yang yongs 'dzin rnams kyi drung du tshe dbang gi
rnam grangs du ma zhig dang / lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor sogs dbang lung rjes gnang mang dag thob mod/ phal che ba gong du brjod pas yid ches pa'i gnas su 'tshal/ de thams
cad kyang thob blo dang go yul tsam ma yin pa khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang nas rtsa ba'i bla ma 'di zhes brgyud pa ma nyams shing ma 'dres la yongs su rdzogs pa 'di rnams
nyung ngu'i tshul gyis bkod pa lags/ thob tshad bris kyang sgyid lug pa las mi gda'o/ /bdag chen rdo rje 'chang kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po/
sku drin mtshungs med mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rnams kyi bka' 'bum/ mtshan brjod gra tog gser gsum sogs mdo mang po'i lung / paN chen shAkya mchog ldan/ kun mkhyen bu
rin po che/ bo dong phyogs las rnam rgyal/ byang chub sems dpa' rgyal sras rin po che/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po yab sras kyi bka' 'bum cha ram pa'i lung / bka'

gdams glegs bam/ thub pa dgongs gsal sogs sa skya bka' 'bum cha ram/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog gi bka' 'bum sogs mtha' yas pa zhig nos pa yin no/ /pha mtha' med kyang nam
mkha'i khams la byis pas gzhal/ /rtogs pa med kyang chos kyi mtsho las sprang pos brgal/ /myong ba med kyang thar pa'i mkhar las btsan sa 'dzin/ /'gro rgyu med kyang 'og
min la sogs chos nyid thim/ /rnam dpyod blo gros ldan pa'i mig bral yang / /dran pa'i bsam pas thub pa'i bstan la bya ra sgrim/ /rgyal sras spyod pa lhag bsam byang chub
sems nyid la/ /rtag tu bslab dang gong 'phel smon par gyur/ /gnyis pa rnying ma ba'i dbang lung rjes gnang la/ /rnam grangs kyi sgo nas brjod na/ bka' ma dang gter mar
bcas pa 'dug pa phyogs gcig tu brjod na/ kun bzang gnyis pa rigs 'dzin chen po'i zhabs drung du bka' brgyad/ bka' ma rdzong 'phreng ma dang / sde snod gsum dang / rgyud
sde bzhi sogs mtha' dag gi don mdo dbang zab mo dang / de nas rang lo zhe gcig pa la/ ayon sku dngos mkhyen brtse'i zhabs drung du/ mkha' la rigs 'dzin gyi gral ma zhig /sa
la dkyil 'khor gyi bkrag ma nyams/ bar du dam rdzas kyi dri ma yal ba'i gsang chen/ mnga' bdag nyang gis srin mo sbar rjes nas spyan drangs pa'i bka' brgyad bde gshegs
'dus pa/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug gis gnam skas kyi klu bdud nag po'i lto nas spyan drangs pa'i gsang ba yongs rdzogs/ rigs 'dzin dngos grub rgyal mtshan gyis dug sbrul
dpung 'dra'i dbus mchod mdzod nas spyan drangs pa'i

rang byung rang shar ste bka' brgya gtso bo sde gsum rdul tshon la brten nas/ kun bzang gnyis pa'i drung du/ sngon du rtsa dbang gis rgyud smin pa de rnams la/ gsang ba yongs
rdzogs sgrub dbang shin tu rgyas pa bdud rtsi sman sgrub bcas pa lan mang du thob cing / gzhan lo tsA dang gter kha mi gcig pa kha yar du bzhugs pa'i zab pa skor dgu sogs
bka' brgyad kyi dbang rgyas 'bring mi gcig pa bcu gsum tsam thob cing / bde 'dus gsang ba yongs rdzogs rang byung rang shar rnams kyi pod kha yongs rdzogs re re/ ayon
gnyis pa'i drung du lho byang gi gter kha du ma zhig thob pa la/ rdo rje drag po rtsal gyi byin rlabs thugs dbang / rdo rje drag po rtsal lha nyi shu rtsa drug gi dbang
rgyas 'bring gnyis/ rdo rje drag po rtsal sgrub sde brgyad kyis bskor ba'i bum dbang rgyas pa/ rdo rje phag mo khros ma nag mo'i dbang / ka dag lhun grub rig pa'i rtsal dbang
zab mo/ /bla ma yum chen gyi gtor ma'i dbang bzhi/ bla ma rigs 'dzin gdung sgrub kyi rtsa ba'i dbang rnam pa nyi shu pa dang / sgrub dbang rgyas pa/ gtor dbang thob
mchog blo bde dang bcas pa/ kun bzang gnyis pa'i drung du/ lho gter mkha' 'gro chen mo/ /'jam dpal nA ga raksha phag mo dbu bcad ma/ yang gsang rdo rje phag mo khros ma nag
mo zhal gnyis ma lha lnga'i dbang dang bcas pa/ ayon gnyis pa'i drung du thugs rje chen po lha lnga'i dbang / lha lcam padma gsal gyi skyes mtha' sprul sku padma gling
pas sman brag nas spyan drangs pa'i zab chos bla ma nor bu rgya mtsho'i dbang rnams sgrub chen mtshan nyid rdzogs pa'i sgo nas rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor so sor thob pa
la/ thog mar sta gon dbang chog

rdo rje'i go khrab kyi sgo nas rig 'dzin lha lnga'i/ rdo rje rnam 'joms dkar po lha bco lnga'i/ gu ru'i rtsa dbang bla ma gsang 'dus kyi/ bla ma'i gtor dbang rab 'byams/ gu
ru sku lnga'i tshe dbang / rigs 'dzin yang gsang bla med lha lnga'i/ phyag rdor dkar po yang gsang lha nyer gcig gi /phag mo yang gsang bla med kyi/ drag po yang gsang bla
med lha lnga'i/ yang gsang nor bu sgrol gsal/ rta mgrin yang gsang bla med kyi/ rnam thos bu dmar po'i/ mgon po sde brgyad kyi dbang rnams dang / mnyam med sprul sku klong
chen rab 'byams pas mdzad pa'i rdzogs chen mkha' 'gro yang tig skor la/ dpal rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dbang / lho gser mdzod nas byon pa'i dpal rdo rje gzhon nu che mchog
gi /sprul sku ratna gling pas ma dang lha mo brag nas spyan drangs pa'i dpal rdo rje gzhon nu'i/ chos rgyal ratna gling pas gnam skas brag nas spyan drangs pa'i 'jigs byed
me'i spu gri lha lnga'i/ de nyid kyi tshe sgrub g.yang zhag 'khyil pa'i/ chos dbang gnam skas nas spyan drangs pa'i dpal rdo rje gzhon nu 'bar ba'i dbang / de rnams rdul
tshon la brten pa'i dbang bzhi kho na dang / sgrub pa bka' brgyad 'dus pa'i yang snying / rta mgrin yang gsang/ 'chi med tshe'i rdzong chung gi tshe dbang / ging lnga
gza' gdong gi srog dbang / lha lcam padma gsal gyi skye mtha' sprul sku tshul khrims rdo rjes dgas lung khra mo brag nas spyan drangs pa'i rdzogs chen mkha' 'gro yang tig
rgyal ba rigs lnga'i dbang zab pa las ches zab pa bka' gter gnyis 'dus 'jam dpal gshin rje sgrom bu mar grags pa'i rgya zhang khrom gyis

spyan drangs pa'i gshin rje 'joms byed 'bar ba lha bzhi bcu rtsa gcig gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i dbang / gshin rje gshed dmar po'i
tshe dbang / bka' ma yang dbang brgyud man ngag de mtshungs dang bcas pa lus pa med par khong du chud/ rang bzhin rdzogs pa chen po yang tig sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi
rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang gsung rab mtha' dag gi lung / sna nam pa chen po rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi skye mtha' sprul sku rdo rje gro lod rtsal gyi bsam yas rnam
snang thugs sgrom nas spyan drangs pa'i zab chos/ bla ma bka' brgyad yongs 'dus kyi/ bla ma zhi ba'i skor rigs 'dzin rtsa ba'i dbang rnam pa nyi shus byang chub pa dang /
sgrub dbang rgyas pa dang bcas pa rdul tshon la brten pa dang / nyang ral gyis srin mo spar rjes nas kha byang dang lhan cig tu spyan drangs pa'i/ gu ru rnam pa bcu gnyis
kyi dbang / bka' brgyad yongs 'dus kyi nang tshan ayon tshe dpag med zhal gsum phyag drug pa yum lha mo so gcig gis bskor ba'i dbang rdul tshon la brten pa dang / drag
po dmar chen dbu dgu phyag bco brgyad pa'i smin byed dbang gsang ba ye shes rang gsal gyi dbang / rtsa ba'i bde chen rol pa sgrub pa rgyas pa lha dbang bcas pa rin chen bdun/
'phrin las bzhi ste phan pa'i dbang gsum/ nus pa'i dbang / rigs brgyud spel ba'i dbang / gsang ba'i dbang / shes rab ye shes kyi dbang / dbang bzhi pa rnams sgrub chen
rgyas par gnang ba'i sgo nas thob/ bka' 'dus kyi nang tshan tshe bdag 'od kyi thig le'i skor la/ bcom ldan 'das 'jam dpal gshin rje gshed phyag rgya chen po zil gyis gnon
pa'i 'jam dpal zhi khro'i

dbang / khro rgyal mi g.yo ba sngon po zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha lnga'i dbang / mkha' lding khra bo zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i dbang / gu ru sku lnga 'chi med tshe'i dbang
/ zab chos padma snying tig gsang ba'i dbang / zab chos kun bzang snying tig dam pa rigs brgya'i dbang / zab chos mkha' 'gro snying tig dbang lnga rdzogs de nyid nyi shu
pa/ thugs gter nas byon pa'i gu ru zhal gsum phyag drug ba lha zhe gcig gi dbang rdul tshon dang / thugs sgrub gsang ba 'dus pa bla ma rdo rje 'chang lha nyi shu rtsa drug
gi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa dang / sbas yul 'bras mo gshongs kyi lha ri rin cen snying po'i 'ja' 'od phug pa nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe sgrub thabs bdud rtsi 'khyil
pa/ mgon po tshe dpag med lha nyer lnga'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du rtsa ba brgyud pa'i dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs dang / bkra shis dag pa'i rdzas la brten nas tshe sgrub
pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por sgrub chen mtshan nyid tshang ba'i sgo nas sgrub dbang rgyas pa/ bcud len gyi dbang dang bcas pas rgyud yang dag par smin par byas/ gzhan yang
rang lo zhe gcig pa la/ mnga' bdag nyang gis srin mo sbar rjes nas spyan drangs pa'i drag po dmar chen me'i spu gri can gyi rtsa ba don gyi dbang dang yan lag 'phrin las
kyi dbang bzhi rdzogs pa dang / sprul sku padma gling pas skur rjes rdo rje'i gur nas spyan drangs pa'i drag po dmar chen zhal gsum phyag drug pa lha nyer gsum gyi dbang
rdul tshon dang / byang gter gyi dbus mdzod nas byon pa'i tshe sgrub lcags sdong ma'i dbang / mgon po tshe dpag med dkar po 'chi med 'od snang ma lha bcu gsum gyi dbang
/ mtshams med lnga sbyong na rag dong sprugs bka'

gter gnyis la/ zhi khro rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor gnyis/ padma brgya ldan gyi dkyil 'khor brgyad de ras bris kyi dkyil 'khor chen po bcur/ rgya gzigs ston pa'i yi ge'i steng nas
smin rgyas su ma tshang ba med par stsal zhing khong du chud/ sprul sku chen po sangs rgyas gling pas gye re bye ma dkar po'i chu rong nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe sgrub
nyi ma kha sbyor/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dmar po zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa yum lha mo'i lnga'i dkyil 'khor du tshe dbang zab mo/ /padma gling pas lho brag sman mdo nas spyan
drangs pa'i tshe dpag med lha nyer brgyad kyi dbang / skur rjes rdo rje gur nas spyan drangs pa'i tshe sgrub rdo rje 'phreng ba'i dbang / padma las 'brel rtsal gyis
spyan drangs pa'i rta mgrin gyi dbang / chos dbang gis gnam skas nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po 'khor ba dong sprugs/ rje btsun karma pa'i khyad chos thugs rje chen
po rgyal ba rgya mtsho lha bcu bdun gyi rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i zhing bkod pa'i gtor dbang / tshe dbang / rgyal sras rdo rje gling pas mon bum thang chu mu nas spyan drangs
pa'i thugs rje chen po rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i sprul sku sangs rgyas gling pas phug ri phug mo che nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po nor bu lugs kyi/ rgya ston padma
dbang phyug gis gangs bar phug mo che nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po yid bzhin nor bu'i/ chos dbang gis lho brag mkha' chu nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen
po yang snying 'dus pa'i skye bdun sgrub chen dang rjes su 'brel ba'i rtsa sgrub kyi dbang ma bu tshang ba skye ba bdun pa'i dbang dang bcas pa/ thugs rje chen po bcu
gcig zhal lha so bdun gyi dbang rdul tshon la brten pa dang / phyag mtshan zhe gnyis kyi rjes gnang / sprul sku bya mang pos lha mtsho srin mtsho nas spyan drangs pa'i kun
bzang thugs gter gyi dbang lung rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ grub chen mi tra dzu gi lha lnga'i byin rlabs/ dpal mgon ma ning dregs pa'i srog

dbang / bod khams skyong ba'i bstan ma bcu gnyis kyi srog dbang / gnod sbyin zangs kyi beg tse can gyi rjes gnang / chos dbang gi dzambha la dmar po zhal gcig phyag gnyis kyi
rjes gnang / nyang ral gyi gter kha nas byon pa'i zhang blon gyi gtor dbang / gra pa mngon shes kyis bsam yas ga ba bum pa can nas spyan drangs pa'i zhang blon rdo rje
bdud 'dul/ phyi sgrub ber nag lha lnga'i rjes su gnang ba dang / nang sgrub lha dgu'i rjes gnang / dzambha la dmar po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i rjes gnang / byang gter gyi
bka' srung / e ka dza Ti dang / dur khrod ma gsum/ re ma ti/ dbang gi ma bdun/ bstan ma bcu gnyis/ rdo rje legs pa/ gnyan chen thang lha/ lcags mdzod kyi bka' srung byang
btsan pa rnams kyi bka' gtad kyi rjes gnang re re/ bstan srung yongs rdzogs kyi dbang / byang gter gyi dpal mgon stag zhon nag po'i rjes gnang / dpal mgon ma ning / tshar
chen chos rje nas brgyud pa'i dbang rjes gnang / zang zang lha brag gi gter kha gnod sbyin nor lha yongs rdzogs kyi dbang rjes gnang yongs rdzogs/ byang chub sems dpa'
zla rgyal gyi zhal gzigs rta mgrin nag po'i rjes gnang / nub zangs mdzod kyi dbang sdud lha chen 'khor bcas kyi phyi nang gsang ba'i rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa/ 'jam
dpal nA ga raksha'i gter kha mi gcig pa gsum gyi dbang lung gdams ngag dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang / de mtshungs bka' ma dang bcas pa'i rjes gnang zab mo lnga tsam dang /
chos rgyal ratna gling pa'i chos skyong dam can sde bdun gyi dbang lung rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ gnam skas kyi gter bdag mkha' ri klu bdud smyon

bka'i bka' gtad/ bum thang gi bka' srung drag po gsum sgril gyi bka' gtad/ dug sprul spungs 'dra'i gnas bdag klu rgyal 'chi med nye ba'i dbang po'i bka' gtad dang bcas pa/
de dag gter kha so so'i shog ser bu yang bu dang bcas pa'i sgrub thabs las tshogs ji snyed pa dang / padma bka' chems/ padma thang yig mi 'dra ba bcu gcig tsam dang / ma
Ni bka' 'bum/ rnying ma'i rgyud 'bum/ gshin rje gshed/ 'char ka tshe bdag dang bcas pa'i dbang lung rjes gnang yongs rdzogs sngags bsdebs dang bcas legs par sbyangs shing
khong du chud/ mdor na lam 'di'i phyogs la yang pha rigs 'dzin chen po dang rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi sku drin las ding sang gi ming btags kyi sngags pa chu
rdo dang 'dra ba rnams dang cung mi 'dra ba zhig bdog /gzhan yang rang lo zhe gnyis pa la/ sde srid bkra shis stobs rgyal drung gis sde par bdag rdzong star gyis gsung
pa'i phyag dam dang / ngos rang la yang phyag dam phebs pa'i nang na/ 'dir 'brel tshad don ldan dpal padma rgyal po rdo rje ye shes rtsal/ mnga' ris rigs 'dzin chen po spyan
drangs te gsang chen dang chos kyi sgo mo phye ste/ tshe gcig la kun tu bzang po'i go 'phang mngon du byed pa'i thabs theg pa yongs rdzogs kyi nyams len thos pas grol
ba'i sgrub pa chen po bka' brgyad kyi skor sogs gsol ba 'debs rgyu yin pas/ de bar gyi phyag g.yog dang chos nyan pa la shog gsung byung bas/ sa dang po'i rtogs pa mngon
du gyur pa lta bu'i spro ba nyi ma shar ba ltar byas/ de 'phral chas nas gnas gsar nas kyi na bza' dngos gtsang ba rnam grangs gnyis kyis gtsos pa'i 'bul

ba 'dra dang bcas ras 'dzims kyi la mo la byas yongs/ gter ston nyid lho nas tshur phebs pa'i lam bar du zhabs rjes zin la res nyin mtshan dal med yongs kyang cung ma zin/
'dar stod grang mo che'i mdun sar cung zad ngal gsos/ rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po tshar pa rje'i rin thang med pa'i sku gdung rin po che la lus 'di zhing gi rdul snyed du
sprul nas phyag 'bul byas/ de nas shar mar phyin sngags rnying ma'i chos grwa rgyun mi 'chad sgrog pa dgon phug pa'i mdun sar tsha ba byas/ de nub klu lung du bsdad/ sang
snga bar phyin te sdod kyi phug po cher mjal/ 'bul rgyu rnams phul bas na bza' rnams de 'phral bzhes thugs dgyes dgyes kyi zhal ta mang dag gnang / bla ma drag po'i byin
rlabs thugs dbang bka' drin stsal/ de nas rgyal po'i pho brang du phebs 'jig rten gyi 'dod rgu ni lha'i dpal la 'gran bsdo ba tsam 'dug /bka' brgyad bde 'dus/ gsang ba
yongs rdzogs/ rang byung rang shar te sgrub pa chen po gsum sbrel mar gnang / pha padma rgyal pos gtso bum bzungs thag /bdag gis yang dag /sde srid sku mched kyis 'jam dpal
dang / rta mgrin sogs kyi bum pa so so'i bzungs thag 'dzin pa'i skal ba bzang po'i dpon slob rnams kyis zla ba gsum gyi bar la sgrub pa mdzad/ sgrub dbang mdzad dus gtso
bum dang yang dag gi bum pa ma gtogs/ gzhan ma bum pa thams cad chu dang dbyer med du 'khyags nas bum chu gnang rgyu mi 'dug /gter kha de gsum gyi shog ser las ji ltar
byon pa'i yi ge rnams kyi lung / sgrub chen de gsum gyis gtsos/ kun bzang thugs gter/ byang gter gyi mdzod lnga'i

chos tshan so so/ mngal skyes nor bu'i bang mdzod/ gtan khrims/ dus khrims/ gsang sngags lam rim/ chos dbang gi ma ning / byang gter gyi stag zhon/ gza' mchog chen po/ bstan
srung yongs rdzogs sogs/ zla ba bdun gyi bar la nyin mtshan khor yug tu dbang lung rjes gnang sogs chos kyi sbyin pa thang mar brdal te chos 'dod kyi re ba mthar phyin
par mdzad/ bstan pa rin po che srid mtha'i bar du rgyas par mdzad pa ni bstan pa stobs kyis rgyas par mdzad pa'i sde srid kyi bka' drin dang / 'brel tshad don ldan padma
rgyal po'i zhal 'od gsung gi bdud rtsis blo gros kyi bum pa khengs te padma 'od kyi gzhal yas la thal mar phyin chog pa ni padma rgyal po yab sras kyi sku drin yin pas bde
na kun kyang 'di bzhin mdzad par zhu zhig /sku gsum sras gcig rgyal ba'i kha lo pa/ /chos sku gnyis pa tshul gzugs padma zhes/ /khyod nyid cig shos rigs 'dzin mtshan 'chang
ba/ /bdag gi 'dren pa bka' gter du ma'i mdzod/ /rgya bod gter gnas chen po thams cad kyi/ /mchog thun sgrub pa'i chos mdzod khyod gcig pu/ /gangs can bod kyi gdul bya'i
skyabs mgon de'i/ /gsung gi gsang ba ches gsang 'di thos pas/ /srid zhi mnyam nyid rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor nga / /sngags pa tshogs pa'i khrod na mi mtsher gda'/ /de nas
rang lo zhe gsum pa khyi lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bcu la bkra bzang la phebs/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa rgyas par gnang / de nas bkra bzang sgrub chen gyis bzhengs pa'i bla
brang 'du khang sbrags pa der zhabs drung sku mtshams zhag bdun mdzad/ bdag gis kyang mkha' 'gro spyi'i yum chen e ka dza Ti'i gtor khang gi mdun du bla ma drag po dbu dgu
pa'i bsnyen

pa zhag bdun byas/ zhag bzhi song ba'i tho rengs kyi dus rmi lam na/ mi dkar po snum la brjid pa zhig gis ayon nyid dpal chen rdo rje gzhon nu'i skur bzhengs pa'i skabs kyi
dam rdzas kyi dkyil 'khor dang bcas pa bkrag ma nyams pa/ chos nor gyi gter gnas mang po dang bcas pa bstan/ khyed rang gi 'dren pa nyid kyi chos nor gyi las 'phro 'di rnams
yin zhes gsal por bstan/ mthar dri bzang gis yid brnangs pa tsam byas 'ja' tshon khra shig ge ba'i ngang nas yal ba ltar byas gnyid sad byung bas dri bzang mngon sum
du'ang thul gyin gda'/ gang ltar de grol nas bar skol la phebs/ padma 'od kyi gzhal yas na rdo rje gzhon nu dang / bla ma drag po mthing kha/ gzhan yang tshe dpag med sogs
yi dam chos skyong dbyer med kyi sku 'dra 'dug gsung / phyag 'khrid gnang bdag gis kyang bla mas ston pa gnang ba ltar rang byon de rnams rgyan tshun chad ma 'dres pa
mthong ngo shes pa gda'/ de nas skor ba mdzad rlung gsang du phebs/ gsol ja'i bzhugs gral rgyas par gnang / de nas gral gyes gzhan ma kun bsangs/ bdag la sdod gsung pa nas
phyag phyir bsdad/ rlung gsang la phyag rkyong ba gnang song bas rdza'i ga'u chung ngu zhig bzhes sku 'phrag la 'jug pa mdzad song / ji ltar lags zhus pas/ khyod la yun
du ma song bar bstan a gsung / yin pa gsang rab tu dam par dgos rgyu la/ dus kun log pa kho na sgrub pa'i phyag g.yog ngan pa zhig yod pa des/ sku rgyab la spyan drangs/
sku 'phrag na yod pa kun la bsgrags/ des rkyen byas gter bdag khros nas chibs pa bzang po zhig

'phral du shi /de 'phral 'gro gsung nas mi bzhugs pa'i grabs mdzad/ bdag gis 'di ltar mi mdzad pa dgos zhus mtshams sbyor lhag bsam rnam par dag pas phul/ gzhan sbyin bdag
gnas gsar ba dang 'bri gung pa bya yul ba/ snye mo ba sogs dga' mo los yin/ de tsho'i dngos las byang pa'i mtshan dga' bas gdan chags sa gnang dgos nan zhus phul/ sde srid
sku mched drung du'ang phul/ so so nas dges dges ci yang gnang / mchod yon legs tshogs kyi dpe thub pa tsam byung / de nas gong du nged rang dpon slob kyi mthun grub spyan
drangs pa'i spyan ras gzigs thugs sgrub skye bdun sogs kyi dbang rjes gnang lung / klu 'bum nA ga raksha/ dbang sdud lha chen/ dzambha la pho dgu mo dgu'i dbang rjes
gnang lung dang bcas pa sogs zab gter du ma'i bdag por gyur pa lags so/ /gzhan yang rnying ma'i rgyud 'bum sogs bka' gter gyi chos sgo brgyad khri zhig thob mod/ phal che
ba ming rkyang tsam min pa nyams len dang spel ba'i gnas dang bral bas thang chad dang 'dra snyam bsams bzhin thang chad pa las mi 'dug go /snyigs dus 'gro rgyun nyam thag
nga ro 'bod/ /'di 'dra'i dus na padmA ka ra khyod/ /thugs rjes yal bar btang ba ma legs mod/ /las ngan 'khor ba'i lcags skud mdud med kyi/ /grangs med bsdams pa 'di dag
gzigs lags sam/ /myur du dpal ri 'od kyi mkha' dbyings nas/ /byin rlabs mkha' 'gro'i chu 'dzin gsar pa yi/ /'chi med bdud rtsi thugs rje'i char rgyun gyis/ /'khor ba'i
khyim kun 'khrud par byin gyis rlobs/ /steng 'og bar dag ma rungs 'byung pos gang / /dmu rgod rgyal 'dre the rang

tsha rag gtong / /chos byed phal la chos brgyad 'gong po zhugs/ /de dus dus 'dir rig 'dzin 'khor tshogs dang / /zhi khro rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus pa/ /rnam sprul sprul
pa bye ba bsam yas kun/ /ra mda' zla med 'bod do thugs rjes gzigs/ /byang phyogs mun pa'i ljongs 'dir chos nor gyi/ /dpag med gter gyi sgo mo da phye zhig /las can 'brel
ba'i pho mo ji snyed pa/ /stobs chen myur du byon la bdud rigs choms/ /bdag gi smon pa 'di dag 'grub gyur cig /gsum pa 'khrid tshul rgya mtsho lta bu nos nas bsnyen sgrub
las mtha' sbyin sreg gis bskang ba la'ang / gsar ma dang / rnying ma rnams rim pas bkod na/ dang po ni rang lo nyer bzhi pa mdo phyogs kyi slob gnyer byed bzhin pa la sngon
du dbang gi smin pa grub zin nas/ 'bru dgon par sngar nas myong ba ni ci yang med/ ham pa byas mtshams shig byas de yang sku gsum gyi lha las gzhan pa med pas de'i nang
nas thugs kyi lha dpal phyag na rdo rje/ de yang che ba brgyad kyi nang nas 'khor lo chen po dbang gis che ba'i gzhi'i bsnyen pa byas dus/ zhag kha yar zhig song ba na
nub cig rmi lam mngon sum rang zer rgyu med pa'i za zi zhig la/ zla bo zhig na nas 'chi la thug pa'i nyams shar/ dkar po nyams de dngas nas bsams rtse na nga rang gi khong
pa'i nang na yar rgyug pa btsugs pa 'dra ba'i zug gzer ni bzod blags med pa lus ni ya yo mi thub pa tsam 'dug /ci 'drar 'gyur ram snyam pa ma gtogs thabs sogs ni gang
yang med/ drin khyer thabs med pa'i pha ma gnyis zas ni ci za ci 'thung bsnams nas zo 'thung gsungs kyang na ba'i gnas tshul ni zhu ma nus/ zas

de rnams sbas nas bzhag /zos tshul zhus/ de nub nas bzung zhag lnga thugs dam ma chag tsam ma gtogs mang po ye ma thub/ yab kyi bka' lung la khyod mtshan nyid bar song bas
mi nus pa 7yod pa nam/ bzhin mdog ye mi 'dug blo lhod byas kha 'don byed dgos gsung / mtshan nyid pra bcal kho na'i dbang gis gnad dang myong ba dmigs pa sogs ni ci yang
med/ da ngas skye ba grangs med cig blangs yod kyang don med kho na ma gtogs chos byed gsha' ma zhig ma byung 'dug /da lan gcig po chos byed pa'i khung byas pa 'di la da
lta shi na rang legs snyam dga' tshor tshad med rang byung / de lta bu'i rbad kham thag chod byas pa'i nub mo rmi lam na sgra zhig lhang lhang 'dug /rlung lta bu yin nam
snyam pa'i de bas gsang ba'i sgra'i gdangs la khyod nad 'di las grol ba yod do zer ba thang gsum byung / gnyid kyi rnam pa cung zad byung ba de sad pa na/ e bden nam snyam
langs pas zug gzer yod pa rnams ni byung ba'i rjes gang yang med par gar song khung med du song 'dug /mngon sum ma yin nam snyam tsa na khams dngas pa rig pa bde ba thugs
dam la spro ba nyi ma shar ba lta bu byung / bsnyen pa'i thog ma 'khor chen lha bcu gsum la zla ba drug gi bar la bgegs kyi rnam pa tsam yang med par bdud dang bar chad
kyi rgol ba las rgyal ba'i thog ma 'di nyid yin no/ /de'i dus dgun shin tu grang ba'i skabs yin kyang mchod pa'i yon chab rnams res 'ga' cung zad 'khyags/ res 'ga' dbyar
dus ltar sdod pa ma gtogs ye nas mi 'khyag /dam rdzas kyi gtor ma rnams kyang dri ma phun sum tshogs pa dang / dpal ldan lha mo nyid la gtang rag

gi gtor ma bcugs pa mngon sum du blangs pa dang / yab nyid sku'i mdangs baiDUrYa dngas ba'i mdog lta bur mthong zhing mdor na des mtshon pa'i bsnyen rtags phran bu byung ba
rnams ni brjed par thal lo/ /de grol 'phral dgon pa der myug gi chen po rnams kyis gtsos pa'i mi grangs brgya lhag cig la tshe dbang grub rgyal ma zhag tu sgrubs pa'i de
nub sir ri zhes pa'i sgra dang thig pa'i skad cig 'dug gang yin nam snyam ba ma gtogs shes rgyu ma byung / sang ltas pas tshe chang gi snod nyung ngu ma song ba'i khar de
ltar khol zhing lud nas nyal sa tshe chus khengs nas 'dug mod/ tshe dbang rgyas par byas dbang re bskur bas tshe'i bar chad kun bsal nas phyi nang gi bgegs thams cad grol
'gro ba 'di de dus nas bzung da lta'i bar du yod kyang kun gyis go bar mi gda'/ de nas sde pa'i bka' lung la khyed mtshams grol 'dug pas che ba brgyad kyi nang nas rdo
rje rnam 'joms khrus kyis che ba'i steng nas yul phyogs 'di nyid kyi lha mi kun la khrus gsol zhig byed dgos phebs pas de ltar byas/ brgyas pa rgyud sde nas gsungs pa ltar
yid ches nges byas/ bum pa sku bzhi ye shes lnga'i bdag nyid chos sku'i dung chos/ chos dbyings ye shes kyi mchod yon phul ma thag /bum pa de nyid mchu dang kha nas khrus
chab chil chil lud byung bas/ zla bo kho na re chu blug drags pa yin pa 'dra zer/ de gar gda' byas/ rgyal po yul phyogs lha mi kun gyi ma rig pa'i bag chags dri ma drug
dang bcas pa bsal zhing dag par byas so/ /mtha' yas gdul bya gzhal yas nam mkha'i khams kun tshad med skyong ba mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug khyod las gzhan/ /grub pa'i
dbang po

dpag med dngos grub 'byung ba'i sgo gcig bsod nams dpal 'byor khyod kyi da dung skyongs/ /gnas lnga mthar phyin mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan grags pa thogs med drin las phyi nang
bdud las rgyal/ /da ni gang ltar byas kyang dam pa rnam gsum drin las da lta'i dus na sprang po bsod nams chos 'phel skyid/ /rang lo so gsum pa lug lo shangs yul skyid pa'i
bya 'dab g.yas ru smyug gi yang dben dpal sbug rnam par grol ba'i ri khrod du zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga la gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad tshugs te/ rje btsun
rin po che mkhyen brtse'i zhabs drung gis dbu mdzad skal pa bzang po'i mched po bco brgyad kyis bla ma bdun gyi bar la gnad du bsnun nas gzhi bsnyen byed lugs la nyi ma
lnga tsam gyi bar la nan tan chen pos dpyis phyin pa blo yul du nges par byas te zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes gsum la grol/ de nub rang la 'di snang gi bya ba thams cad chu
shing gi sdong po ltar du 'dug pa rgyab tu bor nas/ gzhi bsnyen gyi mtshams la rang gi bsam gtan khang bur bcad rgya shin tu dam par byas nas zla ba bdun gyi khongs su bogs
'byin pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dang bcas/ yongs 'dzin rdo rje 'chang tshar chen chos rje'i drin las bgegs med du mthar phyin/ de'i dus zla ba gnyis song ba'i cho 'phrul
chen po'i tshes lnga'i nyi ma shar lhod tsam la gnyid du srib tsam song 'dug pa'i rmi lam na/ sngar mjal ba ni lta ci smos mtshan thos pa tsam min pa mig gis mthong yang
ye ma myong ba'i bla ma cung zad bgres nyams pa sku'i zil lta bar mi bzod pa dbu gtsug dbu lo dang bral ba/ lha rdzas kyi chos gos rnam pa gsum dang ldan pa zhal khro
'dzum dgyes

pa'i bzhed sgra dal gyis 'byin pa/ spyan 'bras zlum zhing brjid pa zhi ba'i nyams can gru gsum cung zad yod pa phyag gnyis lung bstan pa'i phyag rgya ltar mdzad pa gar dgu'i
nyams dang ldan pa zhig byon byung nas khyed skal ba bzang yongs 'dzin dam pa brgyud pa 'khrul pa'i dri ma dang bral ba de dang mjal/ lam tshang la ma nor ba mkha' 'gro'i
zhal rlang ma yal ba 'di lta bu thob phyin chad snying nas nyams len la 'bungs mdzod gsungs dbugs dbyung / da khyed rang 'di lta bu'i gdams pas yongs 'dzin brgyud bcas
la nam yang slu ba med pas dus kun tu 'du 'dzi dang / grub mtha' gzhan gyi dbang du ma song bar zhes na gsol ba thob mdzod gsung lung bstan/ des nas nam zhig bstan pa dang
snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa rin po che'i bdag po khyed rang byed dgos pa yong bas 'khur bzhes dang dga' ba khyad par can sgoms mdzod gsung gzengs bstod/ phyag gis byil byil
mdzad nas nga yang khyed rang dang nam yang 'bral ba med do gsung byung ba dang snyam du gnyid sad pa na/ e ma chos kun rmi lam sgyu mar snang ba bden par 'dug /de lta
bu'i bla ma dang dngos su mjal na ci ma rung snyam mchi mas mdun ngos bangs pa tsam nang du shor/ bsams tsa na blo bde ba'i tshad thub pa rig pa 'ur langs te dga' ba dang
spro ba yid dngas pa thun bzhi'i dge sbyor la dang ba'i dad pa nyi ma shar ba ltar byung / de lta bu'i tshul lan cig ma yin par phebs byung bas dad pa dbrog tu med par
byung / phyis bsams tsa na khyab bdag he ru ka dang dbyer med pa tshar chen rdo rje 'chang gi yongs 'dzin kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma blo ldan

shes rab kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por gda' bas/ brgyud 'dzin kun la ye shes kyi gzigs pa dam pa rgyun chad med par yod 'dug pas/ bdag kyang bsod nams che snyam pa'i
dga' spro tshad med byung / bdag gi spyil bu de snga gong rje rab brtan pa'i bzhugs yul yin pas khong gnas rnying rgyal po de la gsol mchod gnang gin yod 'dug pas/ de'i
nang la rgyal po de khor re 'gro ba zhig gzigs pa dang / lhag par bdag la thugs rje'i gzigs pa mi lhod par gnang gin yod gda' bas/ zla ba de kha'i nang du rje btsun chos
kyi rgyal po bka' drin mtshungs med tshar pa rjes myug nas phyag dam bdud rtsi ril bu'i thum pa gsol ras 'dra dang bcas phebs byung ba'i nang na/ khyod kyi sgrub khang der
gnas rnying rgyal po 'di 'phral 'phral 'gro ba zhig 'dug pas bar chad dam 'tshub kyi rnam pa bzhin mi yong 'dug gam/ ngas kyang dmigs pa sogs gang yod byed kyin yod/ lar
rdo ring rin po che la rang re'i brgyud 'dzin kun la gnod pa mi byed pa'i srog snying phul nas dam bcas 'dug pas/ 'o skol rnams la 'di gcig pu'i bka' drin kyang bsam pa'i
ra ba las 'das/ gang ltar de la dmigs pa'i gtor ma 'dra dang / dge sbyor 'bung bskyed de byed pa dang lhag par lam zab mo nyid la nan tan gyi rtag tu gsol ba thob/ gegs
sel bogs 'don gyi skyel so 'di gcig pu yin no gsung ba zhig phebs byung bas/ sku'i zil dang gsung bag phebs la blo yul du babs pa de dran/ dngos su mjal ba lta bu'i dad
pa'i dga' bas snying rtsa zhu ba'i chu'i dngas ma ni 'dren byed kyi bu ga g.yos te 'khur tshos 'dzin ma'i khyon la ri gzar gyi 'bab

chu ltar shugs drag rba rlabs dang bcas 'bab pa zhig byung / 'on kyang gsol 'debs kyi tshig 'ar ma 'ur ma byas/ mdor na yab sras de gnyis kyi thugs rje las/ lam 'di lta bu'i
nyams len gyi bgrod pa zin/ gang byas tshabs su 'gro ba dang ci byed chos su 'gyur zhing gzhan phan du 'gyur ba/ bla ma dang yi dam tha mi dad du 'grub pa sogs ni cung
ma yin nam/ gang ltar de gnyis la tha dad yod pa ni ma shes/ rgyud nas zla drug sgom pa'i sbyor ba zhes pa rdzogs ldan la dgongs sam snyam/ snyigs ma lnga'i dus 'dir de nyid
bzhi 'gyur gsungs pas/ sku mthong gsung thos ni lta ci rmi lam du rgyud nas gsung ba'i bsnyen rtags phran bu byung kyang thams cad bris pa la yid ches chung bas thang
cig phaT/ he ru ka dpal bdag med lha dgu'i tshogs/ /tshogs drug yul snang khyod kyi rol par shar/ /dag bya dag byed 'khor 'das zung 'jug tu/ /rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor nga rang
zhe blo bde/ /bskal bzang thog ma'i sangs rgyas kun tu bzang / /chos dbyings gsung gi nyi ma gzi 'od 'bum/ /blo ldan shes rab rgyas pa'i pad tshal du/ /lhungs ma thag
tu kun dga'i yal 'dab rgod/ /brjid pa'i sku dang 'dzum pa'i zhal bzang ni/ /mthong thos dran pas srid zhi'i dpal 'byor rnams/ /dge mtshan srid mthar rgyas mdzad rdo ring
pa/ /sras kyi dpa' bo 'phrin las kha lo sgyur/ /stong nyid smra ba'i khyu mchog tshar pa rje/ /zab dang rgya che'i snyan brgyud snying po ni/ /rang sems chos sku'i 'bras
bu 'di na'o/ /de nas zla ba dgu pa'i nang du shangs yul skyid pa'i bya 'dab smyug rgyal khang du sleb/

zhabs drung rje'i bka' lung la khyod sleb pa legs/ shangs la chu bzlog cig la 'gro dgos pa 'dug /chu des rang phyogs la gnod tshabs chen po yong shas yod 'dug pas/ rdzas 'di
rnams do nub nas sgrub pa gyis gsung / gzims chung du zhag bdun sgrub pa byas/ de nas shangs kyi lung pa'i dkyil rgyal ba skyed pa'i yum mchog 'di nyid kyi 'khrungs yul
g.yang chen du phyin/ chu de'i rtsar phyin pas rba rlabs gnam la snyog pa 'dra ba/ mthong ba tsam gyis lta bar mi bzod pa rig gzar gyi rbab lta bur byas/ rang phyogs la
kha bltas nas chu rags chen po zhig 'dug pa de nyid 'phred gtubs su 'phral du byed pa 'dra ba zhig 'dug /e ma 'di lta bu bsgyur ba'i nus pa'i ci yod 'byung ba la kha lo gang
'gro snyam pa'i dogs pa byung / 'on kyang dpa' zhum pas mi 'ong bla ma dam pa'i thugs rje dang lha nag po chen po khyed kyi mthu stobs la rag snyam/ blo la the tshom
'khu khrid med par thag bcad/ rdzas de rnams chu de'i gdung la btsugs/ rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i bskyed chog rgyas par byas/ gtor bsngo dang chu'i gnod pa drag po mi 'byung
ba'i 'phrin las rgyas par bcol/ ya nga bag tsha med par blo bde 'bol rang byas te nub g.yang chen du bsdad/ sang snga bar ltas pas gnam lcags kyi thog ltar drag po'i chu
de/ rang phyogs sgang du lang / de nub 'phreng gcod byas nub rang la bltas nas 'gyur 'dug pas/ ya mtshan che/ nga rang la gdeng thob pa ni ye med/ bla ma la blo khel ba'i
thugs rje myur la stobs che ba de tsug tu gda'o/ /g.yang pa chos rje bsod nams chos 'phel pas mthu rtsal lag yod 'di gar 'dug zer ha

las byed pa dang dad gus byed pa mang du byung / gzhan yang rang lo sum cu rtsa bdun pa la dam chos mtha' dag gi bang mdzod bod yul gyi bde skyid ma lus pa'i sgo gcig po mkhyen
brtse'i zhabs drung du/ mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i glegs bam gcig po gsung ngag rin po che tshogs bshad lan gnyis dang / slob bshad lan cig dang bcas pa rgyas par thob de
yang slob bshad kyi go don zur pa tsam ni/ bla ma rab kyi zhal las blangs/ /zhes pa ltar yongs 'dzin mtshan nyid tshang ba'i sku gsung thugs mnyes par bya ba'i zhal sgo
las 'byung gi /yig nag mtha' dag ltas pas don de nyid rtags pa'i thabs bral te/ tshad ma snyan brgyud bzhi'i spros pa bcad/ /ces dang / rgyu lam 'bras gsum dbyer med don
smra ba/ /gsungs pas theg chen thun mong ba'i nyams len snang ba gsum nas/ dang po rgyu'i dbang nyid 'khrid du byas/ de'i rgyun skyong ba slob bu rjes bzung nas tha mal rnam
rtog sbyongs pa bskyed rim gyis ngo sprod kyi tshul dang / bar du lam gyi dbang nyid 'khrid dang / de'i rgyun skyong ba gya nom lha zhen sbyong ba rdzogs rim nyid ngo
sprod dang / tha ma 'bras bu la mtshams sbyor ba gong ma gsum gyi dbang 'khrid dang / de'i lta ba ngo bo nyid gsum gyi rgyun skyong ba sgo gsum la ye shes skye ba'i rnam
rtog sbyong ba gong ma gsum gyi 'khrid nyid ngo sprod kyi tshul du byed pas na/ rgyu mtshan de'i phyir mgo bshad thabs nas mjug bkra shis yan la rgyud thams cad kyi snying
po rin cen snang ba'i don nyid gtan la phab cing 'gros de nyid sbyar bas na/ dbyer med don smra ba de la slob bshad kyi chos

zhes sa skya gong ma nas da lta'i bar du skal ba can re re la bzhugs pa 'di lags/ las sla dang tshod yod dang / mgyogs chas dang spom yor dang / zol zog gi lugs thams cad spangs
nas ma bsres pas na de skad ces bya ste/ de lta bu'i sbas don snyan brgyud 'ba' zhig tu bzhugs te skal ba bzang po'i slob bu gcig brgyud kho nar bzhugs pa lags so/
/ma skyes rgyud la yod pa'i sa bon la/ /dbang bzhi'i man ngag chu lud mtshams sbyar bas/ /skyon dang bral ba nyams myong myu gu rgyas/ /bde chen lo tog 'bras bu ye shes smin/
/'khrul med rgyud rgyal ke la sha nyid la/ /log tog sprin gyis ma sgrib tsha zer dran/ /mos gus byang chub sems kyi chu klung las/ /'ongs pa'i bka' babs bzhi sogs zab
mo'i don/ /da lta sprang btsun smyon pa'i nyams len yin/ /snyan brgyud sbas don gzhan gyis ma thos pas/ deng gi dus na zab don 'di nyid la/ /rtog ge'i gzo 'dod yod kyang
don ma rtogs/ /thun mong gdams pas blo gros ngoms par mdzod/ /gzhan yang rang lo nyer bzhi pa la 'dul 'dzin dbang po dge 'dun nyi ma'i drung du gsung ngag rin po che tshogs
bshad lan gcig dang / tshar chen yab sras kyi drung du slob bshad lan gnyis dang tshogs bshad lan gnyis lam 'di'i phyogs la dam pa gsum gyi drin las lam skor phyi ma
dang bcas pa lan lnga thos shing sbyangs pas rang rgyud kun gzhi'i phung khams rin cen rol par byas te zhi dul 'bras bu phyug cing su la'ang re ba dang / smon mi dgos pa
chos 'di'i bdag po las ches lhag pa zhig lags so/ /byang phyogs kha ba'i

ljongs kyi mun rum na/ /bstan dang 'gro drug don mdzad sa skya pa/ /zhal 'od dngas pa'i mkha' la tsha zer gyi/ /yul gru ma lus blo gsal padma rgyas/ /dri bsung phyogs brgyar
rgod cing bung ba'i tshogs/ snyan brgyud sbrang rtsi'i bcud kyis myos pa rnams/ /'bras bu glu dbyangs sprin gyi rnga bsang ltar/ /phyogs bcur sgrog pa'i dpa' bo'i tshogs
