rnams rgyal/ /gzhan yang bde mchog lo nag dril gsum gyi 'khrid/ nag po rim bzhi/ bsdu ba gsum pa/ rim lnga dmar 'khrid/ dpyid kyi thig le'i 'khrid/ bde mchog dkar po'i
tshe 'khrid/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi grol byed kyi lam rje btsun yum gyi rtsa dbu ma'i 'khrid thun mong ma yin pa lus dkyil/ 'pho ba/ bsam mi khyab thun mong ma yin pa/ rje
btsun yab dang thun mong ba'i rtsa dbu ma'i 'khrid/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rim lnga'i 'khrid/ rdo rje nag po gur gyi mgon po'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi brag rdzong ma'i
nyams 'khrid/ nang 'khrid thun mong ba yar klungs pa'i zin bris gzhir bzhag la zhal shes cung zad dang / chos nyid bde chen gyi mgon po rang zhal lta ba'i sbas don sa skya
tshad kyi rna bar ma grags pa'i zhal ngo brgyud 'dzin thun mong ma yin pa chig brgyud du bzhugs pa'i gsang 'khrid zab mo dang bcas 'khrid tshul lnga'i sgo nas nyams 'khrid
du thob/ mdor na srung ma'i dbang po 'di'i skor la yongs 'dzin dam pa rnam bzhi'i zhal sgo las thob pa dang / lhag par 'gran zla kun bral mkhyen brtse'i zhal sgo nas
thos pas bstan srung 'di nyid kyi chos tshul ji snyed thob pa yin no/ /phyi nang rten 'brel lus la rab bsgrigs nas/ /rdo

rje lus kyi rang zhal sngon du byas/ /byang phyogs srung ma'i gtso bo rdo rje gur/ /phyi nang gsang gsum gdod ma'i rgyud skor bcas/ /ma lus rigs brgya'i ngo bo rdo rje 'dzin/
/paN grub mkhyen brtse'i thugs kyi sgo phye nas/ /bgegs med dgyes pa'i dngos grub dbyar mtsho ltar/ /rba rlabs phyogs bcur bskyod pa'i chu klung las/ /sa skya'i gdung
brgyud zhal bcud snying po ni/ /rtag tu 'bras bu khur 'dzin kha'u pa/ /bdag gi yongs 'dzin rnam gnyis zhal 'od las/ /da lta bdag gi blo yi bum pa las/ /gzhan du yod med gzu
bos bya ra mdzod/ /ma thos gsang chen gzhan na yod gyur na/ /myur du zhabs rdul mchod nas gus pas len/ /bod kyi yul gru gang na yod kyang rung / /bdag la myur du ston
nam brda thong zhig /de nas rang lo so bzhi pa la sprel lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu la/ zhabs drung rin po ches kye rdor gzhi bsnyen mdzad/ bdag gis sngar gyi bsam gtan
khang bu der dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i gzhi bsnyen zla ba drug byas/ gnad dang dmigs pa byed lugs sogs la bslab bya yang phebs pa'i tshul snying du bcangs nas nyams su
blangs pa'i zla ba gcig dang zhag bcu bzhi song ba'i nyi ma rtse shar la gnyid du song ba'i rmi lam na/ a tsa ra brjid che la snum bag dang ldan pa brgyad lag pa sbrel
nas gar sna tshogs byed cing dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur mang du ston/ thams cad lag pas bdag gi 'phreng ba mgo bo la bzhag /ske la sgor/ 'dzum pa'i zur gyis gcig gis gcig la blta
zhing kun gyi 'dzum pas bdag la ltas nas/ par pir gyi gleng mo mang dag byed kyin 'dug kyang gam la cher ma zin/ de lta

bu'i tshul gyi lan ma kha yar byung / gnyid sad pa na bsams na chos nyid bde chen gyi mgon po mkha' 'gro lha brgyad kyi rnam par 'dug pas rmi lam ngan pa rang ni min pa 'dra/
gang ltar mgon po sogs mngon sum mthong zer ba du ma yod gin gda' ste de dag gis lam 'di phyogs la ma bsgrubs kyang 'grub pa'i gang zag du ma zhig yong gin yod 'dug pas
de 'dra yin nam/ 'di tshos ni lo zla zhag ci bsgrubs kyang de 'dra'i na ma bral/ rnam 'phrul tsam rmi lam du byung ba la dga' bar zad do/ /khyab bdag he ru ka nyid du ma'i
gar/ /mgon po'i tshul 'dzin bskal bzang bstan pa skyong / /rnam 'phrul ji lta ji snyed dgyes pa'i tshul/ /mngon sum gsal bar mdzad 'di nyams re dga'/ /de nas zla ba bzhi
song ba'i bya lo cho 'phrul chen mo'i tshe bcu bzhi'i snga thun gyi nyi ma dro phyed tsam la gnyid kyi rnam pa yod tsam byung ba'i rmi lam du bdag gi sgrub khang nas
rgyal chen bzhi sogs so so nas dmag rigs du ma go mtshon dpag tu med pa gyon nas/ so so nas ru shangs kyi rnam pa dpag med byas te thon song / 'phred lam bde mo zhig yod
pa de la byas/ myug chos sde'i rgyab ri dga' ldan rtse mo zer ba zhig yod pa de'i rtse tshun chad dmag snum la dpung che ba des khrig de khengs 'dug /co sgra byas te g.yas
su lan gsum bskor nas/ dug gsum gyi dgra las rnam par rgyal ba'i rtags su lha rgyal gyi sgra 'brug ltar dus gcig tu ldir ba lta bu dang / dar 'phyar kha dog sna tshogs
kyis nyi ma bsgrib thub pa lta bu dang / dung gi sgra sogs rol mos sa gzhi g.yo nus pa tsam 'dug /de thams cad la yang de 'dra'i sprul pa nyi zer gyi rdul ltar 'phros/ mthar

stong gsum thams cad mer gyis khengs 'dug /de nas gcig la gcig thim rang zer rgyu ni mi 'dug /mtha' nas me long la has btab pa bzhin rim pas 'dus/ mthar 'od zer sngon po baiDUrYa
dngas pa'i mdog lta bu nyi ma 'bum gyi gzi 'od ltar 'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba zhig byas song / de nyid rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i drung mdun gyi nam mkha' sku mtheb
sor gyi tshad tsam mtshan dang dpe byad kyis spras pa lta bas chog mi shes pa lta bu zhig byon byung bas de'i thugs khar sim de thim song / de nyid kyang 'od zer sngon
po'i rang bzhin du gyur nas rang la thim song / yang de 'dra ba'i sprul pa byed pa'i khung la gnyid sad byung bas/ ya mtshan che dgod bro lar chos 'di'i bzhugs tshul la/
srung ba yang dag bzlog pa yin/ /bzlog pa yang dag bsad pa yin/ /zhes pa ltar srung ba grub pa tsam ni yin pa 'dra/ gang ltar rmi lam la nges pa med/ 'on kyang srung bzlog
bsad mnan thams cad dus gcig tu grub ste sprul pa spro ba dang yang sprul spro ba sogs 'di'i gzhung nas bshad pa'i bsnyen sgrub kyi rtags rab 'bring tha gsum cha tshang
ba tsam byung / 'grel pa gur rgyan du gsungs pa'i 'bum phrag drug cu rtsa bzhi dag bcad khor yug tu byas nas song zhing / de nas gzung da lta don lnga'i bar du thugs dam
'chag med kyi khungs byas/ ma hA kA la 'bum phrag brgyad brgya dang bdun cu kha yar song 'dug cing / shA sa nas gtsos pa'i srung ma 'di'i skor la bod rbad bsad gsum gyi
sngags rnams 'bum phrag phyogs kyi bsgyur ba tsam song / mdor na yul gzhan g.yeng bas bzlas par yod pa nas 'bras bu yang de mtshungs shig yod dam bsam/ gang ltar

chos mthun gyi bzhed dgu mtha' dag lhug par stsal bas thun mong gi dngos grub sna re tsam du zad do/ /rdo rje'i chos skyong phyi rol grags pa'i gzugs/ /rgyud gsum rang sems
gcig nyid kho na la/ /srung dang bzlog pa la sogs med mod kyang / /ma rtogs 'khrul pa'i snang ngor phyi rol shor/ /rtogs na de dang de 'dra'i dgos pa shar/ /kun gyis ma
go lkugs pa'i tshul du bzhugs/ /dpa' bo gur mgon nag po de nyid dang / /khyab bdag he ru ka dpal gang de la/ /tha dad mi 'dug gdod nas gcig nyid do/ /de nas zhabs drung yang
sku mtshams grol byung / bdag gis kyang grol te gzims chung du gtang rag gi bskang gso dpon slob stabs gcig tu zhag gsum sbrel cig byas/ de grub 'phral dpon slob rnams
zha lu la phebs thog rgyal nas zhal ngos bsu ba gnang / bsam rtser rin spungs zhal ngo dang mjal phrad dgyes dgyes gnang 'dug /bdag gis dpal sbug tu bsdad khyod rang sgrol
dkar la tshe bsnyen cig gis gsung ba nas zla ba phyed gnyis tsam byas pa'i khongs su bogs 'byin pa'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg dang bcas gegs med du grol/ gzhan yang 'di'i
sbyin sreg sde pa'i sku rim sogs rang gi bar chad zhi ba'i sbyin sreg brgya lhag pa song zhing / de bar la bsnyen rtags sam gang yin kyang zhag bcu drug song ba'i rmi lam
du/ thang yangs po 'jam la dkar ba'i sa gzhi la byang sems chos sku'i mchod rten/ sku gzugs kyi tsha tsha khri khrag du ma 'dug /de rnams la kunda ltar dkar ba'i na bza'
gsol ba gral la rim par bsgrigs zin pa de la mchod pa sna tshogs 'bul/ 'di

thams cad nga rang gi lha yin zer yid dga' dga' byed pa'i rnam pa byung ba dang gnyid sad/ bsam na de dus kyi dge mtshan du ma des lo brgya 'tsho ba'i rten 'brel mang po go
lags so/ /drug sgrags ldan pa rdo rje'i gur chen nang / /phyi rol mtshan mas ma gos kha ba'i mdog /lo brgya'i bar chad tshe sbyin ma des bsal/ /'chi ba'i grong khyer bdud
kyi g.yul las rgyal/ /de nas bya lo'i ston dus rang lo so lnga pa la rwa khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud thun mong ma yin pa'i nyams khrid zab mo dang rgya ston gyi mdzad
pa'i zin bris/ jo gdan yon lhun gyis mdzad pa'i zin bris/ rgyal khams lo tsA ba ma Ni kas mdzad pa'i zin bris/ tsha ba rong pa shAkya rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i zin bris/
de rnams kyi steng nas 'khrid tshul zab mo re re dang / gzhan yang mtshan mo rgyu ba/ mtshan ma gyen bsgreng / rwa rtse'i rnal 'byor/ 'chi kha ma'i rnal 'byor sogs 'khrid
tshul du ma zhig thob cing rgyud thog nyams len la yang dag par sbyar/ de grol 'phral zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bco lnga la sngar gyi bsam gtan khang bu de nyid du rdo rje
'jigs byed kyi bsnyen pa mthar phyin par byas pa'i zhag bcu song ba'i srod thun gyi sgang la dngos su gzhogs g.yas na mar gzugs mi mngon pa'i gcan gzan sems can ma rung
pa zhig yar rgyug mar rgyug byed pa'i mdun pa shar cing / de la bred dngangs shin tu che ba rig pa mnan pas mi non pa sha rnams kyang g.ya' khyug khyug byed pa/ da ltar
rang had de langs na snyam pa'i zil bun ne ba had had dran pa 'tshor snyam byed pa zhig byung / dge sbyor tshan bskyed nas gang yong ba shog da lta rang za na yang zo

snyam pa byas bsdad/ rgyud nas 'jigs pa chen po 'ong zhes pa'ang cha 'dra tsam yin pa 'dra/ de nas srib tsam nas 'thung dkar de nyid mdun na yod pa gzugs mi mngon pa rkog rkog
zhes pa'i skad cig 'dug /'phral bltas pas dkar yol shubs bcas o dkar bas khyer 'gro'i 'dug pas raksha 'jigs su rung ba de skyon pas bzhag song / gzhan yang yi dam 'di
nyid la bsnyen pa thengs ma bzhi byas pa nas bzung da lta yan la 'di nyid kyi snying po 'bum phrag lnga brgya dang nyi shu kha 'thor song zhing / rtsa sngags nye snying
sogs la des mtshon pa'i 'bum phrag brgyad cu lhag pa song / gzhan yang yi dam 'di nyid kyi dkyil 'khor la sgrub cing mchod pa dang / 'jug cing dbang blang ba stong phrag
gcig dang bdun brgya kha yar song zhing / bogs 'byin zhi ba'i sbyin sreg zla ba bzhi sbrel ba dang gzhan yang skabs su ji snyed cig song / thams cad tshul bzhin du bris na
sngags par zhal gyis bzhes pa rnams kyi sngags grangs las mi nyung tsam song bas kun rdzob tu gyur dogs nas ma bris so/ /dang po'i mgon po gur gum gzhon nu'i sku/ /khyod
nyid dus 'dir srin po'i cha lugs kyis/ /bstan dang gdul bya'i snying la bde ba ster/ /khro rgyal zhal dgu pa des da dung skyongs/ /so ma pU ri mkha' 'gro'i pho brang nas/
/ral gri'i phyag mtshan rol pa'i rdo rje yi/ /'bum phrag bcud phyungs mkha' 'gro'i snying khrag 'di/ /bod yul bsgyur nas 'jam dpal rwa lo sogs/ /'khrul med brgyud pa'i
zhal 'od las 'ongs pa'i/ /mdo rgyud nang tshang ma lus hrul por ston/ /tshe gcig bcu gsum

sa de e ma ho/ /gzhan yang dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po dpal ldan chos skyong birWa pa'i thugs bcud skal ldan dbang po rab tshe gcig la sangs rgyas thob pa'i thabs gshin rje
gshed dmar po shin tu spros pa med pa'i de kho na nyid kyi 'khrid zab mo yang thob/ de nas khyi lo rang lo so drug pa la/ bstan pa rin po che'i spyi'i sbyin bdag rin spungs
nas gos sku zhing khams rgya mtsho'i rab gnas la zhabs drung yang phebs dgos gsung ba'i snyan gsan byung ba nas zhal bzhes mdzad/ bu rin po ches mdzad pa'i dus 'khor
mngon dkyil rab gnas sogs zhal spen gnang nas/ sa gar/ mchod gar tshun chad la bdag lta bus tha shal byas pa'i bskal pa bzang po'i mched po brgyad cu tsam la nyin mtshan
khor yug tu slob sbyangs bka' drin bskyangs nas khong du chud/ rang lo so bdun pa phag la rin spungs nas spyan 'dren gyi bsu ba bzabs mar bcas te gdan 'dren pa'i phyags
phyir phyin/ rab tu gnas bya'i lha tshogs rigs ldan yin pa dang / de mtshungs dus 'khor gyi steng nas phyi nang gi rten 'brel legs tshogs kun bsgrigs nas rgyas par gnang
ba'i khur bzhes mdzad/ de ltar cho ga rgyas par bsgrubs/ me tog 'thor bar rje btsun dam pa byams chen na phebs 'dug pa gdan drangs/ kye rdor gyi steng nas phyag nas khyug
tsam zhig gnang song / rten 'brel dang legs tshogs kyi rgyun thams cad ni la kha'i spang rtsi rlung gis bdas pa ltar song / rab ston gyi sha sna ni srin po'i pho brang ltar
'dug /gzhan yang bza' btung gi bye brag brjod kyis mi lang ba tsam

'dug mod/ de grol nas byams chen du rje dam pa'i drung du rdog dkyil bdun sogs gsan par phebs pa'i phyag phyir khor tsam phyin/ de nas nub chos lung brgyud nas dpal sbug ri
khrod du dge sbyor gang 'phel gyi rnal 'byor skyid pa'i rang ngo shes pa zhig byas so/ /e ma ya mtshan ltad mo ngo mtshar can/ /snyan pa'i ba dan 'brug sgra stong dang mtshungs/
/don gyi gtso bo nam mkha'i mtha' las bskrad/ /'bras bu lo tog mi zad rlung gis khur/ /grags 'dod rlung gis btegs pa'i gshog brgyang gis/ /ches mtho'i dbus na thun
mong bsil g.yab mdzad/ /mthar thug lam gyi skyel so gcig pu pa/ /lam zab bla mar snying nas 'dud do kye/ /de nas rang lo so brgyad pa byi lo gling log bde 'khrugs skabs
gnas gsar nas kyi phyag tu bo dong byung / gzims khang sogs kyi phyag nas kyi phyags phyir khor tsam phyin/ phar lam khro phu'i lha khang steng shod khyad 'phags bcu gsum
sogs gnas mjal yid ches par byas/ spyi sgos kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam rgya cher byas/ rim par myug tu phebs zhal ngo rnams la sku 'brum bzhes/ de 'dra'i sku rim
sogs kyi ban ling la rtse rang du bsdad/ bsnyel gzhi rnams rim pas dngas/ zhabs drung tsho slar bo dong la phebs song / bdag gi sngar gyi bsam gtan/ khang bu nyid du mtshams
bcad rgya shin tu dam par byas bsdad pa'i dus snga ma bo dong la khor tsam yongs pa'i skabs su gnas mjal sogs byed pa ni ma byung / de'i dus kyi rmi lam na bo dong du
sleb nas kun ra chen po zhig 'dug pa de na gzhan

skye bo'i rgyu 'grul dang 'du 'tshogs sogs ni ye mi 'dug /khyams stod de na khri dpang mtho dman mnyam po byas pa'i khri du ma zhig dang / gzhan khor yug tu gdan bkod khad
de byas pa zhig 'dug /de na dkon gnyer yin zer ba'i ban btsun mdog smug po brjid chags pa zhig 'dug pas/ khyed rang khri 'di 'dra zhig la myur du 'god rgyu yin zer/ he he
bdag la 'di 'dra gang nas yong byas pas/ de 'dra ma zer byed dgos pa yod de khyed rang gnas mjal 'di tsho yang mdzod zer/ gnas de'i phug na sgo legs po zhig 'dug pa phye
byung / bdag gis kyang phyin bshags na sa la pus mo nub pa tsam 'dug /phyag 'tshal ba bzhin ni ma byung snga ma mthong tsa na bu mo gos dkar khra gyon pa 'dra 'dra lnga
'dug /slar de rnams gar song ni ma shes/ sku rang gang na yod byas pas ma gzigs lags sam/ 'di na lags zer ba ltar bltas pas gtso bo'i sman sku bstan byung bas baiDUrYa dngas
pa'i mdog 'dra ba dre'u zhon pa be con thod khrag thogs pa 'dra 'dra lnga 'dug /dkon gnyer khong gi rten bshad kyi rnam pa zhig byed kyin 'dug kyang cung mi mthun pa
gda'/ de nas gnyid sad tsa na ci yin nam bsam pa ma gtogs kha rog bsdad/ de grol nas slar drung la 'di 'dra byung tshul zhus pas khyod kyis dmag zor ma mthong 'dug pa rgod
bro gsung dgyes dgyes ci yang gnang / rmi lam dang mngon sum gyi khyad ma gtogs rigs lnga char de kho nar gda' gsung / slar de lo gnas gsar gyi phyag tu po dong byung /
bdag kyang zhabs drung phyag phyir yong dgos shar/ de nas bla ma thugs rje can de'i phyi nang

gi rten 'brel legs tshogs mang po dang bcas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal sras rin po ches byin gyis rlabs pa'i khri chen po gsum gyi nang nas rta ra bla brang
zhes phyi nang stong nyid du yod pa de nyid byed dgos pa byung zhing / de nyid zhabs stegs seng ge'i khri la ci yang mi shes bzhin du sdod dgos pa byung ste/ bsams na
sngon gyi rmi lam kho yang bden pa e yin/ lar rmi lam 'khrul pa las ma 'das mod/ phyis gnas mjal byas pas gtsang khang de na sngon gyi nas sogs ni yod pa tsam las mi 'dug
/gang ltar lha de yang dre'u zhon pa zhig las mi gda'/ phyis rjes gnang sogs chos skor gyi gsol ba btab kyang ye ma byung / khyed rang gis mthong ba tsam gyis mi chog gam
gsung ba des chog pa yin nam bskang gso sogs byed pa ni ye ma byung / sngon gyi lha des sngon du lung bstan stsal/ /mngon sum gsal nas mngon du gyur pa 'di/ /dngos kun
gsal gzigs dngos byon bla ma des/ /dngos por dril nas dngos grub ya mtshan gnang / /yang bsnyen pa de nyid kyi zhag kha yar song ba'i rmi lam na/ zhabs drung chibs pa zhel
le ba zhig la chibs na bza' hrul le ba bzhes/ zhal cung zad nongs pa tsam mdzad nas phebs byung / bdag gis phyag 'bul byin rlabs zhus/ sku rdab yong ba 'dra zer ba zhus
pas cang mi gsung bar phebs song / gnyid sad byung bas sku dog chen po 'dug pas zhe blo ma bde ba'i mthar thug pas ji ltar drag snyam pa ci bya la 'das/ da gzhan thabs gang
byas kyang bzhugs pa'i

tshan min pa 'dug /rje btsun rigs 'dzin chen pos gdan bzhugs kyi gsol 'debs shig byung na sku dog las grol ba 'dug snyam/ rmi lam gyi gnas tshul sde par zhus pas/ rje'i drung
gi mtshan rtags dga' mo mang 'dug pas/ chu bo ri la 'phral du pho nya btang ji ltar zhus pa ltar/ yi dam mang po la sbyar ba'i gsol 'debs shig gnang byung bas sku tshe'i
bar chad bdud sde las de nyid du grol ba yin no/ /rmi lam la nges pa ci yang med pas dga' bar zad do/ /de nas glang lo so dgu pa la sde pa'i sku rim la myug gi rtser bzlog
chen bzhi'i nang nas/ kha 'bar ma zla ba sbrel nas nyin re la tshar gnyis re 'chag med btang / de grol ba dang sde pa'i thab chen po dong la 'degs pa gnang / zhabs drung
yang phebs bdag la yang 'gro gsung ba'i bka' bkod byung / nan gyis zhu grol zhus kyang ma gnang bar phyag phyir yongs/ de lo 'bri gung zur pas spyan drangs pa'i gshin
rje gshed du ba dum bu la brten pa'i dmag bzlog byed dgos pa 'dug pas byed mi chos rje bsod nams chos 'phel gyis gsung ba dang / de'i bca' gzhi sogs kho rang gis shes kyin
yod gsung ba'i phyag dam zhabs drung gis bsam rtse nas phebs/ de 'phral bcas gzhi rnams gang rtsol byas zhag bdun mtshams bcad rgya shin tu dam pa zhig byas dgug gzhug
dang sngags rtse gcig tu 'dren pa'i dus zhag bzhi song ba'i srod la gnyid du srib tsam song ba'i rmi lam na tshag tshag ces pa'i sgra zhig 'dug /de'i rkyen gyis gnyid sad/
yang dngos su tshag sgra shin tu che ba byung bas zla bo la thog 'di ji ltar

byas pa yong ngam byas pas/ gdung 'bred gtubs su chag byung bas nyan ka btsugs nas bsdad/ mal da lta spos pa drag zer ba mang po byung / thog rdib nas shi yang de spos na de
'dra las skyag 'byung chung ba med snyam de ga mnan nas bsdad/ de'i sang nyin snga thun gyi dus su sla nga sha gsar pa'i 'bus khrig gang 'dug /ji lta bu yin nam mig 'khrul
ba ni min nam/ khyi thod ni skam po yin/ gzhan ma rdzas rnams la de 'dra byung dogs med 'dug snyam spyi mong gi yog thos khyi thod phyin kha log tu dkrugs skor ba nang
skor byas/ da 'bu 'di rnams ma bsal na ni 'chi ba 'dug /bsal na ni sku rim gyi rtags bzang ngan ji ltar yin mi shes pa 'dug /gang ltar sla nga dug shing gi mes dal bus
bsregs/ mig btsum ste bla ma'i thugs dang sems can rnams kyi shes pa rang sems gsum dbyer med du bsres nas stong nyid du zim me lhod de bzhag pas/ de'i ngang nas 'bu rnams
ni 'ja' yal ba ltar song nas ci yang mi 'dug /me gtong ba'i zla bo de na re de lta bu'i cho 'phrul ni shin tu bred/ 'a rdzi zer lta mi nus par bros song / de nas mis ma
mngon par sa mtshams su sbas pas pha rol gyi dpung yan lag bzhi pa'i tshogs de ni char med kyi 'brug bzhin du rang dngas su song / rang phyogs bde skyid kyi bsgo skal thob
pa de yang 'di lta bus sbyor ba'i stobs nus su mchis/ de nas zla phyed tsam na tho rengs kyi dus gnyid du song ba'i rmi lam na/ bo dong e'i rdzong nang nas bud med gzhon
nu mdzes shing brjid pa rgyan dpag tu med pas brgyan pa/ phyag

na mdung dar sna lnga du ma thogs pa zhig 'thon nas lcags ri'i rtse na tshur khor re 'khor ba dang lha rgyal gyi sgra tshangs pa'i gdan man chad mgul nus pa dang / dar 'phyar
gyis nyi ma 'grib 'gro ba tsam byed kyin 'dug pa'i ngang nas gnyid sad/ bsams na dpal ldan dmag zor rgyal mo dgyes pa'i tshul gyis g.yul las rgyal ba'i rtags yin par go
/de nas zhabs drung yang phebs byung / 'phral du shog gsung pas de 'phral phyin/ khyod kyi ma bsdad kyang tshab byas te/ rtse gcig tu sku rim la 'phungs 'tshub drag chen
po byung 'dug ste mal yang ma spos 'dug pa sgor ma nas legs tshogs kyi dpe thub pa byung 'dug gsung / sku'i na bza' bzhes 'phro de 'phral gnang / dgyes dgyes kyi zhal ta
mang po dang lhan cig sbags nas stsal bas blo bde phugs su phyug pa'i sprang po skyid do/ /de nas rang lo bzhi bcu pa stag lo zhabs drung dpon slob dpal zha lu gser khang
la thegs song / bdag la bka' lung khyod rang khams la 'gro dgos pa 'dug pas khams gsum dbang du sdud pa'i phyir dpal tshogs kyi bdag po'i bsnyen pa byed dgos pa de bzhin
gyis gsungs nas zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bco brgyad la rgyal phur byung ba dang bstun nas mtshams bsdams/ spyir khams gsum dbang du sdud pa'i dmigs pa lhag par gang
dbang du bya ba'i gdul bya'i tshogs dbang du byed pa'i dmigs pa 'di ltar mdzod gsung bslab bya thun mong ma yin pa rnams mthar phyin par gnang / bka' lung bzlog tu ni ma
bde khams la 'gro 'dod pa'i zhe blo rtsa ba nas

ma byung / dbang sdud kyi dmigs pa khams dang gzhan zhig 'phos te byas pas/ gang bsams de nyid 'phral du sngon du gyur pa zhig byung ba 'og tu 'chad/ thog mar bsnyen pa'i lha
bde mchog nas gsungs pa'i dpal phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed kyi hUM bzhi pa la zla ba bzhi mtshams byas/ mtshams nang de nyid du zhabs drung phebs byung / yang
rgyal dang phur bu 'dzom pa'i nyin phyag bris mdzad nas tshogs bdag gi sku thang gong gsham zla gam zhal sprod kyi dkyil 'khor gtor ma bshom lugs kyi dpe chung dang phyag
nas tshun grub pa mdzad nas gnang / de nub nas gza' skar dang bstun tshogs bdag la bsnyen pa zhag nyer gcig byas gegs med du mthar phyin/ thun mong ma yin pa'i bris skus
gtsos pa'i rten rdzas de rnams phyis su rje btsun dbon rin po che'i phyag tu rten 'brel bsgrig pa'i phyir du phul/ de bzhin legs tshogs gong 'phel du song / lar bsnyen
pa gang byas kyang gegs kyi rnam pa gang yang 'ong ma myong ba dang / lhag par 'gab 'dre gnon pa sogs kyang ma byas/ gang ltar nged rang tsho'i brgyud pa 'di la brgyud 'dzin
thun mong ma yin pa bdun tshun la tshogs bdag gi bsnyen pa byed na 'gab 'dre gnon mi dgos pa'i zhal bzhes rdo ring rin po ches mdzad 'dug pas 'di gcig pu'i sku drin la
khyer ba'i thabs ma mchis so/ /brgya phrag 'tsho ba'i lus blangs dpag med kyi/ /dus kun lus srog 'byor tshogs ma lus kun/ /grangs med gcig tu bsdoms nas phul na yang /
/drin la khyer thabs bral lo mkhyen brtse'i dbang / /lugs gnyis 'dod

dgu'i drin gyis dus kun bskyangs/ /phyi nang rten 'brel ma lus khyod kyis bsgrigs/ /khams gsum srid zhi'i rgyal srid mi zad pa/ /'phral dang yun gyi dge mtshan du ma kun/ /nam
mkha'i mdzod bdag glang chen gdong pa can/ /bcu gnyis phyag gi dpal 'byor rgyas par spel/ /bden gnyis don mtshon zhabs 'og ne'u le/ /nor bu'i 'phreng ba ma chad rtag
tu skyongs/ /de lo rje btsun rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bco lnga la chos dbyings su phebs/ bdag cag ltos bcas kyi dpon slob rnams kyis gsol
'debs la yongs/ bdag gis rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye ba'i slob dpon gyi tshul byas/ zhabs drung tshogs chen gyi dbu la phebs/ bstan pa la rten 'brel bsgrig
pa'i phyir legs tshogs 'gran pa'i khungs byas kyang bstan pa nyams 'gro ba'i rtags kyis don rnams ma 'grig pa zhig byung / de nas rang lo zhe gcig pa yos lo grang chen
nas zhabs drung du 'dod chos zhu mi rje btsun bla ma'i bu slob dge ba'i bshes gnyen kha yar byon pa rnams la mgon po che chung gi phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'khrid dbang
lung rjes gnang dang bcas pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs 'khrid tshul gnyis dang des mtshon pa'i zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu'i zla ba dang
po'i nang du dpal grang mo che nas bshes gnyen mang po sku gzhogs la byon 'dug pa rnams la chos 'dod kyi dbul ba bsal ba dang / lhag par dge slong 'od zer ba dang bdag
nyid la thun mong ma yin pa'i zab gnad kyi gsung gi bdud rtsi du ma zhig gnang / de nas zla ba lnga pa'i

nyer gcig la rje btsun thugs rje can de nyid chos dbyings su phebs/ las ngan can gyi dmu rgod ma rungs pa bdag cag sogs ltos bcas rnams mya ngan gyi khang bur smre sngags kyi
cho nges 'bod cing shul du lus/ de nas sde pa bstan pa'i drung gi zla ba de ga'i nyer gsum la zhal ngo tshang ma bsags nas 'jig rten gyi phyi mo'i zhal ta la/ slar mchod
pa rnams dang mchog gsum la bsod nams kyi tshogs gsog tshul/ dpon po'i zhal 'dzin/ g.yog gi skyong lugs dgra 'dul lugs/ gnyen skyong lugs/ mnyam po'i 'grogs lugs sogs
mdzad pa'i zhal bkod dpyis phyin par gnang nas sku mtshams kyi rnam pas bsnyel ba'i tshul bstan nyer dgu la zhabs drung de nyid kyi phyags phyir 'di snang gi phun tshogs
kun bor nas 'bral med du phebs/ de lta bu'i mchod yon ni ma bzhugs/ rang yang 'cham yams shig byung nas 'chi la thug ste/ de phyin nga rang yang gdul bya'i zhing khams shin
tu zhal mthong gsung gi bdud rtsi thos skal ba can zhig a yong da lam shi na legs snyam bdog pa'i dngos po gang yod dge 'dun gyi phyag tu phul/ 'chi ba la blos blangs
nas gsol ba 'debs pa'i khungs byas gzims khang byang na sdod pa'i skabs su bla ma drag po phyag bco brgyad pa'i bskyed rim gyi rnam pa byas sngags shig 'debs pa'i skabs la
sdug gnyid kyi rnam pas nyin cung zad cig gnyid la srib tsam song ba'i rmi lam na/ sde pa a bstan drung gi gzims chung gi zur 'phyong na spre'u thog tshad gcig 'gyur tsam
gyi gzugs byas pa/ spu rtse la 'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba rgyan du mas

brgyan pa'i gzi brjid lta bar mi bzod pa lta bu zhig 'dug pa de bdag gi rtsar rgyangs te mchongs byung bas/ bred dngangs shin tu che ba zhig gi ngang la lag na sngags 'dren
pa'i 'phreng ba raksha 'jigs su rung ba de 'phyar nas skyon pas/ mdun gyi zhal ba la cag sgra dang bcas pas phog byung bas gnyid kyi rnam pa de had de sang byung ba nas/
spre'u ni mthong sa na mi 'dug /zhabs drung de lta bu ni ma bzhugs/ rmi lam yang de 'dra ba las gang yong 'khrul pa rgya 'byams pas lan mod/ gang ltar rgya 'dre ma rungs
pa drag shul can zhig ni yin pa 'dug /da snga yan du 'dre gdon gyi gtses pa yong ye ma myong zhing / ltos bcas kyi skye 'gro gang de la nged rang gi srung ba'i sbyor ba
byas pa kun la gnod pa mi yong zhing / bgegs gang yin de las 'phral du grol ba ni kun gyi mig sngar phebs pa 'di lags/ lar 'dzam gling chos kyi nyi ma de nyid bde skyid kyi
dpal 'phrog pa'i phyir du zhing 'di nyid mun pa'i gling du byas nas chos sku'i dbyings su phebs/ rtag 'dzin can gyi zhen pa bzlog pa'i phyir du me tog gi char nyin mtshan
sbrel nas kha ba babs pa ltar mdzad nas gshegs/ rje btsun nyid kyi ye shes kyi gzigs pa dam pa rgyun mi 'chad mnga' ba los yod/ las ngan can bdag cag rnams tshogs gcig
tu 'dus pa'i dus 'dir khyed kyi thugs rjes gtong ba phod pa snyam dran med du brgyal/ yang dran pa gsos tsa na bsam bzhin mchi ma ni ri gzar gyi chu ltar du 'bab/ lag pa'i
thal mo ni mgar ba'i lcags tho ltar brang la 'thab/ kye hud khyod sku mthong ba dang

khyod gsung thos pa'i dus dang ni bral/ khyod kyi thugs rjes mi gtong ba zhig mkhyen snyam re zhig sems kyi 'gyu ba 'gags par gyur/ lar khyed kyi thugs rjes bslus pa ma yin
mod/ las ngan can bdag la mos gus kyi yu ba med pas lan gda'/ spyir bstan pa'i nyi ma khyed nub pas sems can gyi bde skyid nub par gor ma chag /da skyid po yod pa'i bya
ba ni gang yang mi 'dug /cung zad 'chi ma thub na rgyal khams su snang zos gang bder lus ngag yid gsum 'chi ba la phan pa'i chos gdengs thob cig byed snyam pa'i zhe bcad
byas/ rin thang med pa'i sku gdung nyid ni bdag lta bu ni bsod nams dman pas phyags phyi ma grub/ 'on kyang mchod sprin rgya mtsho'i dbus su bzhugs su gsol nas/ gsol ba 'debs
pa'i dkyil 'khor bde kye gsang gsum/ gshin rje dmar nag /kun rig /mi 'khrugs pa/ sman bla/ nA rag dong sprug sogs dkyil 'khor du ma zhal phye nas gnang gin 'dug /bdag
nyid bsod nams kyi mthu dang bral bas ma thub kyang / lus ngag yid gsum rtse gcig tu byas nas gsol ba btab/ de nas ma shi tsam nad kyis grol nas sde pa'i bka' lung dngos
yin gyi khungs byas/ blos longs pa ni skad cig kyang ma byung / zhal ngo rnams ni bkra shis sgang la phebs song / bdag gis bla brang dkar por bsdad/ sbrul lo zla ba bcu
gcig pa'i rang lo zhe gsum pa ma rnam 'tsho por zhabs drung rig 'dzin chen po'i drung du gsung chos zab mo mang dag 'dod chos bka' drin bskyangs/ zhabs drung sku mtshams
gnang ba'i phyag g.yog byas zla phyed mtshams

shig byas/ de bar la A tsarYa zer ba'i phyag g.yog ngan pa dam pa nyid la yang log sgrub dang skur zhus kho na byed pa zhig bdog pas/ kho rang gis mchor yab 'dra mo zhig byas
kha ngan gyi dgra g.yabs/ gnas gsar nas kyi sku gsung thugs la phog pa'i rnam pas/ kho ni rang srog rang gis bcad de tshe'i dus byas/ de 'drar brten pa'i nga yang gnas
gsar ba'i mi ngor song ba nas gnas tshul ngan pa de'i rkyen gyis bdag gis kyang myug la log pha rgod sku drin can de'i sku gdung zhugs la 'bul ba sogs kyi zhabs tog byas/
shing skam rtse 'dzegs grogs ngan shugs kyis spun/ /gnas dang dam pa grogs bzang drung nas phyung / /rang yul bdud kyi btson rar yud tsam bsdad/ /dug gsum kha rlangs 'byung
bzhi lus nyid la/ /ma rungs bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad kyi mtha'/ /dran pas gso ba 'joms pa'i rgyu las grol/ /snyigs dus bskal ngan 'tshogs pa'i zhing khams 'dir/ /chos
kyi nyi mas mun rum kho nar byas/ /kye hud snyigs dus bstan pa nyams pa dang / /'gro kun skyabs dang bral bas sems nyid 'phyo/ /e ma chos kun sgyu mar ston pa'i 'jigs
gzugs la/ /'khrul pa'i snang bas gdon du mnar ba de/ /bltas na rang sems chos skur ston pa'i gda'/ /yin par ngo shes skad cig de nyid la/ /bgegs dpung dpung chen phyi rol
grags pa'i gzugs/ /gzugs stong stong par ston pa 'brel ba'i lam/ /lam mchog mchog gi skyabs su khyod kyis bstan/ /bstan pa'i mod la la mor mkha' spyod gshegs/ /de nas rang
lo zhe bzhi pa rta lo bo dong la yong dgos gsungs nas rta

bsu phyag dam nan chags dang bcas phebs byung bas phyin/ sleb 'phral byang gter gyi spyan ras gzigs nyon mongs rang grol gyi sgo nas skye bdun sgrub pa byed dgos gsung / de
ltar zhag bdun tshul bzhin du bsgrubs pas sgrub gzhung nas bshad pa'i 'phel rgyas dang / bla ma dam pa'i thugs rje'i rtags rab 'bring cha tshang tsam byung / mkhan bslab
gsum nas kyi dbu mdzad pa'i der 'dus pa'i tshogs la sgrub dbang rgyas par phul/ de lo mkhan po'i 'os rigs 'ga' re yod pa 'dug kyang / zhal ngo 'ga' zhig gi thugs bzhed du
song / bslab gsum nas la mnga' gsol mdzad/ bdag nyid ni rgyal khams su snang ba gang bde byas 'dir snang gi dgon pa dang / dpon la brten pa'i bya ba las rje btsun thugs
rje can de nyid la snying nas gsol ba 'debs pa la dga' snyam pa'i zhe bcad thun mong ma yin pa byas/ dgon gzhis kyi re ba blo las 'das kyang sngon du mtshams shig byas pa'i
dus khams kyi gdul bya'i zhing khams dang / 'dzin dka' la phan thogs chung ba'i stag ste nyid go 'phos byas pas lan pa 'dra/ zhal ngo rnams kyi bka' lung tsha drag bzlog
tu cung ma spobs 'jam dbyangs 'khon gyi gdan sa stag ste bla brang byed dgos pa byung / gang ltar de nas bzung lo brgyad tsam bdag bzung byas/ bya lo rje btsun thugs
rje can de'i dgon rnying phra bo la zhig gsos byas/ gnas der sde pa'i sku rim la mtshams byed dgos byung / bla ma drag po'i mtshams lo gcig byas mkhan drung gsung ngag cig
gnang gin 'dug pas

de la bar chad byung dogs yin pa 'dra/ gang ltar dgon chung sdod yul skyid la dge sbyor 'phel ba nyer 'tshe dang bral ba zhig bdog pas stag ste byed rin byin po dgon pa der
bsdad/ rang lo lnga bcu pa byi lo gling log yun ring la dos drag pa byung / gnas gsar nas kyang bo dong dang 'bral la nye bar 'dug /de la brten bdag gis kyang nyin mtshan
ngo mi shes par byang pa'i sgar la phyin pa'i 'bras bu bo dong ni ma byung / bkra shis sgang gi ston bzhes gang yod dang phyag rdzas sogs rgyu dngos phyi nang kun la zegs
'thor ye med par phyag tu phyin/ de nas sde pa'i zhabs rjes 'breng ba la ni stag ste ma 'phrod pa nas grol cha zhus/ de skor gyi gtam yi mug la bya ba'i thebs bral ba
mang dag yod kyang dgos pa'i don dang bral bas ma spros so/ /yi mug brjod tshig gtam nyid mang na yang / /don 'di phyogs la dgos med rgyab tu bor/ /lugs gnyis 'brel ba'i
dbon dang de ring bral/ /rgyab dpung blo gros 'dzom yang bslu bar nges/ /gnas bzang dam pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i sa/ /phyi nang 'tshe ba'i bdud las rgyal ba der/ /rtse gcig
bla ma sgrub la gzhol ba po/ /phyi ma don gnyer rnal 'byor ku sA li/ /de bas rtsis dgon pa de yang ring du spangs/ /de nas nga gcig pa glang lo sde srid bkra shis stobs
rgyas drung gis shog phebs pa nas ngam ring la phyin/ zla skor tsam 'dir snang gi gnas tshul la ma chags par rtse gcig tu thun bzhi'i dge sbyor 'chag med rnams gong 'phel
byas bsdad/ sde srid la chos lung byang rtser tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa zhig sku rim la gnang dgos

zhus pas ma grol de ltar byed na theg mchog gling du sdod gsung ba la/ bdag spun gnyis kyi chas sogs sgor ma nas dka' ba'i gnas su 'dug pas mi nus tshig sbyangs zhus/ de rting
slar yang gong ltar zhus pas nga sde srid cig gis mi gnyis kyi lto gos rang 'byor yong gsung bka' drin stsal kyang / don la nu bo de lugs gnyis gang la'ang rtsi med blang
dor dang bral ba zhig 'dug pas/ phugs su rang yang byed dkar song dogs nan grol zhus/ de skabs lha sa nas phebs 'dug pas tsha zhang bka' gros mdzad/ lha sa dgon pa byed
dgos tshul phebs kyang snyigs dus kyi bla gzugs kyis dmyal ba'i rgyu sgrub pa las mi 'dug pas/ de phyin lto phyi gang phyid byas snang zos gang bde dga' snyam gnang ba
zhus pas ma grol/ 'on kyang dpon khang du sdod pa las gang yang drag bsam khas blangs/ lha sa nas bsu mi gnang byung bas phyin/ sde srid bka' lung dang / lha sa nas rnam
dpyod 'jam dbyangs la 'gran brdo ba'i dgongs pas phyi nang gi legs tshogs spel ba'i slad du zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes bcu gcig la rgyal dang phur bu 'dzom pa'i nyin par g.yag
mi pham bla ma'i gdan sa nor bu chos lung gi khri la bkod/ mang ja dang khri ston sogs bzabs ma gnang / gzhan yang skya ser kun gyi khrod ni dpal 'byor legs tshogs rgyas
par spel ba sogs yang dag byung / lha sa nas kyi sde srid 'jigs bral dkon mchog rgyal mtshan bzhugs pa dang mjal/ nyon mongs rang grol la sogs pa'i gsung gi bdud rtsi
mang dag

bka' drin bskyangs/ btsun khral zhig gnang 'dug pas dam pa de nyid kyi mkhan po dang / bdag gis las slob byas te zhag grangs nyi shu bgrangs pa la bar ma dge tshul gyi sdom
pa phog /bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas pa'i smon pa rgya cher sgrub cing dar rgyas kyi 'go btsugs pa yin no/ /de nas nga gnyis pa stag lo chos lung du kye rdor gyi
dbang dang mgon po'i phyi nang gi rjes gnang thun mong ba sogs 'dod chos zhu ba mang po'i re ba bskang / sde pa'i ban tshang pa zhes skad kyi 'byon pa ku ru dang mnyam pa
rtags su bkod pa la rngam sems me ltar 'bar ba chu nang gi rdo bzhin du gnas pa rnams kyi khrod du/ sde pa'i sku rim la mi mthun bzhin du mgon po'i gtor bzlog cig byas/
'di'i gtor bzlog gi gzhung dang bla ma mkhas pa mtshan nyid dang ldan pa rnams kyi zhal shes brgyud ldan rnams kyi phyag bzhes mthong brgyud dang bcas pa la/ zor gtor zur
gsum par byas te de mthun skyed chog sogs zangs gri can la byed la/ de rnams mi ldan pa'i phyir phyag len gya tshom dang rol mo'i 'ur sgra gang che dang skad yod pa gtso
bor byas pa'i rgyu mtshan mdzad pa rnams dang stabs cig tu byas te pu tra'i rtag gtor de nyid 'phangs pas/ skyes pa rtsal chen gyis mda' 'phangs pa ltar mig gis mthong
tsam du song / /de nas kyang me dpung ri klung kun gsal ba lta bu'i 'od dang bcas nas song bas/ der yod pa rnams 'di lta bu ni nges par mgon po 'grub pa'i rtags zhing bcu
sgrol ba la gcig tu dpa' ba yin pa 'dug zer bdag la yang da snga ci yang mi shes shing ro za ba dang

chos brgyad slob dpon man pa med kyang / de nas cung drag tu song mod/ 'on kyang de phyogs na chos 'dod kyi gang zag ni nyin mo'i skar ma tsam du zad do/ /de nas byang chub
sems dpa' zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi dgon pa sa bzang du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dmar 'khrid tshem bu lugs zla ba tsam bskyangs/ der btsun ma kha re la 'khrid kyi skabs
bsnyen rtags byung ba yang mang po dang / lhag par byis pa lo bcu gcig 'gro ba zhig 'dug pa de nyin re bzhin chos rar yong gin 'dug /ngo sprod kyi skabs na mar la sleb
pa'i dus su sems kyi kha dog dang 'gro 'ong gnas tshul dris pas 'khrid pa rnams la smra ba'i yul dang bral nas mi 'dug /byis pa kho na re sems ni kha dog dkar po'o zer/
gang na gnas byas pas res 'ga' ni pha ma'i rtsar sleb 'a mo 'di ru sdod kyin 'dug /sdod lugs ji ltar byed kyin 'dug byas pas/ bla ma rang zer ba ltar had de chod de sdod
kyin 'dug zer bzhad gad theg pa byung / gang ltar byis pa de nyid la nyams rtogs mang po byung 'dug pas ya mtshan che ste lam 'di la skye ba sngon nas sbyangs pa'i las 'phro
can zhig yin pa 'dug pas skye ba 'di nyid sngon las phran bu ma zad pas blangs 'dug /de nas yun du ma song bar rus pa la 'ja' dkar po dang bcas po ta lar bzhud do/ /sgrub
sde der nyon mongs rang grol gyi sgrub mchod kyi dge rgyun btsugs da lta'i bar du'ang rgyun ma nub par yod/ de nas rje btsun padma rgyal po dbus nas ngam ring la phebs
laM lha sar spyan 'dren zhu ba gnang / bdag gis kyang yang tig

gces sgron gyi 'khrid thugs sgrub 'bring po'i dbang sogs gsung gi bdud rtsi ji snyed dang / dger gyi brtag gnyis dang mtshan brjod snga 'gyur gyi lung sogs 'dod zhus mang po
bka' drin bskyang / de nas phebs dus bka' lung la 'dir snang gi bya ba thams cad chu shing gi snying po ltar nges par mdzod/ dge sbyor gang 'phel dang bstan pa la gang
phan sems can gyi don ci nus gyis/ dang yang sngon gyi smon lam gyi dbang gi bkra shis stobs rgyas pa la phung po 'di sprod dgos pa yod pas 'chi ba la 'gro gsung / bka' lung
yang la brjed pa med pa 'ga' zhig phebs byung bas bdag gis phyag btsal te de lta bu'i bka' lung mi phebs pa dgos/ bstan pa nyams dma' ba dang sems can sdug pa'i dus bstan
'dzin gyi skyes bu rnams bstan dang skye 'gro'i don la dgongs nas zhabs pad brtan dgos zhus pas/ khyod blo ma 'chi da lo ci la thug kyang 'gro gsung gsol ba ma thebs/
sde srid la yang legs nyes kyi lung bstan mang po gnang gin 'dug lhag par lha sa nas la khyod kyi dbon po 'di la rang gi rnam shes la rang dbang 'dus pa zhig mi 'dug pas/
lugs gnyis sgor ma nas khyod rang yang byed lugs mdzod gsung phyi mo'i zhal ta mang po phebs/ ngam ring du zla ba brgyad pa'i nyer gsum la ayon mkha' 'gro'i gling du byon/
u dum wA ra ltar dkon pa'i sku gdung rin po che de nyid sde srid la bzhag /thugs rje'i gzigs pa rgyun mi chad du yod pas gsol ba snying nas btab/ lar bod 'bangs sdug
bsngal gyi nyen dus dam pa de lta bu ma bzhugs pas sems can

gyi bde skyid nub par gor ma chag ste las ngan can bdag nyid kyang bskal pa'i yang mtha' 'dir skyes/ dam pa nyid kyi gsung gi bdud rtsi ni chad/ khyod sku mthong ba'i dus dang
ni bral nam zhig khyed nyid bzhugs pa'i zhing khams su gdul bya'i tha mar skye ba'i gsol ba khor mor 'debs pa 'di lags/ de nas rang lo nga gsum pa yos bu la 'dar grang
mo che nas sngon gyi zhabs drung du mched po 'dras gtsos pa'i kha re byon byung bas rgya dang mon gyi dpes/ bshes gnyen de rnams la so sor thugs bzhed dang bstun pa'i rwa
khrid nA ro mkha' spyod sogs zab chos mang po phul/ zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga la rje btsun rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sku gdung rin po che la mjal du yongs
spyi sgos kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam yid ches par btab/ mched po blo gsal bkra shis pa'i gra khang du zhag lnga bsdad/ rtse nas gzhis len sogs brtse skyong zab
mo gnang / de skabs khro bo bcu'i rjes gnang dbang tshar gsum byas/ rje dbon blo gros legs bzang pas grwa khang du snod ldan kha re la mkha' 'gro lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang
byas pa'i tshe/ de snga yan chad shin tu dkon pa la ye shes phab pa dang mnyam du char pa'i rgyun yid ches nges babs/ zang zing gi bsnyen bkur yang mang po byung / rje
bla ma'i bstan pa rgyas pa'i 'go btsugs/ slar lha sar log rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi nyer gcig mchod pa rgyas par bsgrubs/ yang zla ba drug pa'i nang du grang chen
pa 'ga' zhig phebs byung ba rnams la rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi smin grol cha lag dang bcas

pa phul/ de nas sde srid sku mched thugs bzhed so sor gyes/ lha sa nas kyang rta brgyugs me tog yar ba ltar song / rdzong dang phyag rdzas bu rta kun dbang med bzhi mdo'i rtswa
bzhin dor nas bzhud/ skya ser gyi khul nas pho rus kyi gzhung 'then mkhan mang dag 'dug kyang ri bong gi cal dang mtshungs pa'o/ /zhag bdun gyi bar la rdzong du bsdad/
na bza' mchod rdzas dngos po drag pa'i rigs rags pa phyag tu 'bul mi rdzong bda' byas/ rang ngos nas phyi nang gi rgyu dngos la bslab pa'i rtsa ba ngos zin par byas nas
skyon gyur gyi rtog pa ye med/ dpal ldan rtse pa sku drung zhes mi lus la rngam sems me ltar 'bar ba'i srin po'i gzugs de nyid sde pa la rdzong sogs 'jags gnas zhu bar
gtsang la gnang ba don de nyid phyi nang log tu sgrub nas byon byung sde pa ma bzhugs phyin mchod khang 'di khyed bla ma yin pas rtsis bzhes gsung pa la/ bdag ni btsun par
khas blangs pa yin pas ma byin pa'i dngos po se ba tsam yang mi dgos byas pas 'o na de tsug yin zer nas mchod khang gi gtsos dngos po drag pa phal che ba bsdus song ngo
/ /gtsang nas mi sna sprel po byon rdzong chen phyi nang thams cad rtsis sprad/ dngos po'i rigs thams cad ni de 'phral sprin tshogs rlung gis bdas pa ltar dengs song / de
nas slar yang mi sna bskyar ma byung bas/ bdag dang cha zhabs skya ser kun la dpon chen gyi rdzong 'di lta bu'i phyi nang gi rgyu dngos thams cad khyed rang g.yog rigs
gros byas kyis bzas pa yin zer ba sgyur sgyang mang po byung / gzhan ni gleng mi cang mi 'dug /bdag gi lugs gnyis

gang gi khrims 'phrad mdzad kyang bdag skya ser rnams la 'khri ba rtsa ba nas med/ sngar byon pa'i mi sna tsho la rtsis 'bul mi bdag yin/ dngos po'i rigs 'di 'dra byas tshul
rim pas bsnyad pas dngas/ bka' 'gyur gser ma de nyid gtsang la khur ba sogs mi 'dod pa du mas mnar ba nas mi ser thams cad sdug thug /dka' bzhi pa zer ba'i sde pa'i nang
blon khrel gzhung nam mkha'i glog pas thung ba de nyid tho thal btang / de la brten pa'i bya ba ngan pas gzhi byas skya ser mi chags par thug pas/ gzhan ma 'go yod ni mi
'dug snying rje'i yul du gyur pa rang 'di rnams su 'dug pa snyam dka' ba dang du blangs/ yul dang yul gru thams cad bde na snyam pa dang 'jig rten bde zhing zhes smon pa'i
rtsis na dngos su lag len byed pa la ngal dub dang bgyid lug med par rang don spangs pa'i bya ba nyin mtshan ngo mi shes par byas pas thams cad rang gnas su 'drongs pa
zhig byung / de ltar lus ngag longs spyod sogs kun gyi ngal ba khyad du bsad pas don la sems can gyi don chen po dngos su bgyis pas rgyal ba dgyes pa'i thabs las gzhan
ma mchis so/ /de skor gyi gnas tshul mang dag cig 'dug mod/ yi ger bkod pa la don dang bral bas dgos pa med/ gang ltar lha sa pa skya ser bde ba'i go skabs thob pa'i khungs
byas/ bdag gis 'dar stod bla ma'i gdan sar yongs/ zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nyer gcig la sngar gyi grwa khang nyid du zla ba phyed gsum gyi bar la drug cu thor pa la rdo rje
nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i phyi 'khrid phyi nang

gsang gsum yongs rdzogs phul/ de grol 'phral don du gnyer ba kha yar la gsang 'khrid thun mong ma yin pa zla ba lhag tsam phul/ de gnyis car la rjes gnang lung sogs zung 'jug
tu byas/ brgyud pa 'di pa'i bgros la 'khrid grol ba dang sgrub skor sogs yi ge'i lung rdzogs pa mnyam du mdzad pas de ltar byas pas gegs med du grol/ tshogs kyi 'khor
lo rgyas par spel zang zing gi ster sbyin yang phul du phyin pa byung / sngon gyi smon lam gyi dbang dang lhag par dpal sbug tu gsung ngag gnang skabs yab sras lhan du lung
bstan la/ nged rang tsho'i brgyud pa 'di la chos rje karma pa 'di pas/ chos rje 'bru pa 'di phan thogs che ba yong 'dug gsung pa lung bstan ltar na rje bla ma'i bstan
pa la phan thogs e yong snyam gsung las ji ltar byon pa rnams gang zin lan sprod pa'i tshul du phul/ de nas chos lung du phyin/ rang lo nga bzhi pa 'brug lo lha sa rdzong
byang pa'i phyag tu byung / skya ser kun gyi mgo bcun byas phyag 'bul la phyin/ dgon pa rtsis bzhes gnang dgos nan zhus phul kyang len du ma bde bar ma gnang / dbyar thog
chos lung du chos ldan gyi bya ba gong 'phel byas bsdad/ de'i ston ka zla ba bcu pa la 'dar la yongs/ dpal ye shes mgon po phyag drug pa'i nye bar brten pa'i gnas ri khrod
kun gyi yang rtse shing mangs dgon par zla ba gsum gyi bar dmar 'khrid tshem bu lugs/ rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud/ dmar po skor gsum sogs 'dod chos zhu mi mang
po'i re ba mthar phyin par bskyangs tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgyas par byas nas so so nas 'gur ma dang glu gar sogs yid tshim par

byas chos dang dge sbyor gong 'phel skyid pa'i rang ngo shes pa zhig byung ba yin no/ /de nas chos lung du phyin/ sbrul lo nga lnga pa dpyid ka zla ba dang po la rdo rje brag
rdzong ma'i 'khrid khams pa'i slob ma 'dras gtsos pa rnams la byed skabs sku gsung thugs mi 'gyur ba'i 'khrid rdzogs mtshams su sde pa 'dar nas kyi rgyal po sku gzhon
pa cung zad bsnyel ba tsam 'dug pas yong dgos gsung 'bod mi gnang byung bas/ chos de yang mtshams shig tu slebs byung ba dang / phan thogs ji ltar yong kyang bka' nan ches
pa nas yongs rta khar slebs pa dang don grub dbang phyug zer ba khos phyag 'tshal byung bas nges par snyung ba la phan pa 'dug snyam blo bde ba'i tshad thub pa byas yongs/
slebs 'phral gzhi med du dngas pa zhig byung zhag nyer lnga rtser bsdad de nas bzung ste nyi zla ji srid gnas kyi bar du mchod yon zung 'brel byas pa 'di lags/ de nas
grang chen gtsug lag gi sgo mchor gyi gnas su zla ba gcig gi bar la sku rim la dmigs pa'i mtshams bcad rgya shin tu dam pa zhig byas/ de nas mang mkhar la byas skyid mo
gshongs su zhag gcig bsdad/ tshe dbang sogs kyi 'dod bzhed bsgrubs/ de nas rje btsun bla ma'i bsti gnas rmu gshongs dge ba'i tshal gyi bla brang mjal/ rim par phyin sprul
sku lhas sbyin pas gzhi len yang dag gnang tshe dbang gi thugs bzhed bsgrubs/ de nas gsang chen dam pa chos kyi za ma tog grub thob rim pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas mu
gu lung mjal/ zhag gcig rim gnyis gang yong gi

nyams len yid ches par byas/ 'di lta bu'i gnas su skye ba nas skye ba thams cad du lam zab mo'i nyams len khor yug tu byed pa'i rang dbang thob pa pha tshar chen yab sras lta
bu zhig nam yong ngam snyam pa'i lhag bsam phul du phyin pa byung / de nas rim par chu tshan la phyin/ shar bla ma thub bstan dge 'phel gyi lha khang mgon khang sogs mjal/
spyi sgos kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam rgyas par byas/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i phug chen bzhi'i nang nas nub kyi phug pa cha lung rdo rje'i brag rdzong mjal/ de nub
gnas 'brel byas bsdad/ de nas chos lung du phyin snang zos gang bde byas bsdad/ slar 'dar la shog gsungs nas yongs/ sde pa rgyal po rnams kyi bla ma byed dgos gsung /
de 'dra yong ba'i shes bya dang mthu stobs gang yang med/ sde pa tsho sngar phan yongs 'dzin gzhan dang mi 'dra ba'i grub thob slu med kyang gi zhal slob tu song ba dang
/ lhag par dus gsum rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs blo gsal rgya mtsho'i shul du bdag kha brdar la spu sud pa/ ser sna che ba lags gnyis gang nas kyang ci yang mi shes shing rang
gar 'gro med pas de 'dra yong ba'i na ma med zhus/ yang yang nan chags phul kyang ma gsan par byed dgos shar/ gang du'ang 'gro sa med pa 'di byas/ gang ltar sgrol dkar sogs
thugs bzhed phran bu phul/ chos lung la khor tsam phyin/ de nas dpal 'byor rab brtan tu rgyal po sku gzhon pas zla ba gcig mtshams bcad rgya shin tu dam par byas pa'i
bsnyen rgyab byas/ de bar la spyan ras gzigs kyi dmar 'khrid tshems bu lugs dpon sa chos mdzad ma nyid kyis

gtsos kha re la smin rgyas su phul/ de rnams gegs med du mthar phyin/ de nas rje btsun rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i ring bsrel phung po gser gdung rin po che'i zhal
bkod gnang / bdag la bar chad zhi phyir srung 'khor dang lhag par rgyu dang zangs bzo ba rnams la bgegs skrod dang bskyed chog byed dgos gsung / bla ma drag por langs nas
byas pas bar chad kyi mtshan mas glags blta bar ga la nus rgyang grags tshun la bkra shis mnga' gsol ma grub par la nyes pa'i go skabs bral/ lar bla ma dam pa'i thugs rje
las gnad du mi 'gro ba byung dogs med mod/ 'on kyang srung 'khor cher gtad nan bskyed de sgom pa dang nyin mtshan dal med drag sngags rgyun chad med par bzlas/ zla ba
drug gi khongs su yongs su rdzogs te rin po che'i gdung nyid mchod rten du spyan drangs pa'i ye shes phyir 'brang gi bgegs skrod 'jam dpal zhal dgu par langs te byas pas
bdud rigs kyi tshogs thams cad byer zhing der tshogs pa kun kyang spu zing byed pa mang dag byung 'dug mchod stegs su phebs pa dang mchod pa dang sku khrus 'bul ba sogs rgyas
par byas/ panytsa li ka snam char gyi grwa sbugs nas gnyis med kyi ye shes la kha dog med kyang bdud rtsi shel dkar gyi gong bu gcig tu byas pa tshul khrims kyi phung
po gong 'phel dang dri bsung phyogs bcur 'phro ba'i spos dkar gyi rdog ma bdag gi 'phang du gnang byung bas sgrib med ye shes kyi thugs rje rgyun 'chad mi mnga' ba lags
so/ /de ltar rgyu rin po che gser las grub pa'i gnod sbyin pho mo'i 'khor lo sgrub pa zla ba tsam byas rgyud

nas ji skad bshad pa ltar bzhugs su gsol/ mthar rab tu gnas pa rgyud sde nas gsungs pa ltar mtshan nyid tshang pa'i sgo nas zhag gsum sbrel zhig byas/ sgrub po sbyin bdag dang
bcas pa'i tshe dang bsod nams dpal 'byor gyi rgyun thams cad gong 'phel du 'gro ba'i phyir rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg thun mong ma yin pa'i phyag len gyis brgyan nas byas/
de skabs rje bla ma'i phyag bzhes min snyam pa'i skyon la brtag mkhan mkhas pa mang po 'dug kyang / ltag chu chad pa'i rdo bzhin du thang chad nas gzims/ gang ltar bkra
shis dge legs kyi rol pas dus kun 'tsho ba 'di yin/ de nas nga drug pa rta lo zla ba lnga pa'i nyer bdun la skal bzang gi slob bu brgyad cu tshun la nA ro mkha' spyod 'khrid
thun mong ma yin pa yongs rdzogs byas dus sngon 'gro rdor sems bsags sbyangs kyi skabs su chos lung la yud tsam phyin bsam gtan dpal ba zhes pa'i rgyu dngos phun sum
tshogs pa zhig bdog pa dus mthar sleb 'dir snang gi bdog pa thams cad bdag la sprad byung ba tshags byas kho rang gi rjes la ci 'gro byed bsam pa'i zhe bcad byas/ slar log
nas 'khrid nyid rgyas par bskyangs/ phyi nang gi mkha' 'gro thams cad kyi nyams chags bskang ba'i phyir tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgyas par byas/ de nas chos lung la phyin/ khong
ni pha rol tu 'phos tshar 'dug pas chos lung dang chos 'khor lhun por mang ja sbrel ma dang nas khal 'gyed khro zangs g.yu sogs rgyan rigs go khrab sogs kyi skam 'gyed
dge rgyun gyi zhing / mi dmangs la des mtshon pa'i 'gyed chas dang / lhag rnams

la lo dus kyi mchod stengs su bstan pa nam gnas bar du snying po kye rdo rje'i sgrub mchod btsugs rang don du ma 'khris par bstan pa dang sems can gyi don 'ba' zhig tu song
/ de nas sde pa a rin drung cung zad bsnyel ba'i sku rim la srung ma rnams la bskang bshags brgya rtsa dang thugs gso sogs rgyas par sgrub par yod/ slar yang chos lung du
chos ldan gyi bya ba gong 'phel byas bsdad/ de nas nga bdun pa lug lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer gnyis la byang nas lha sras drung gdan sar phebs pa'i lam bar du mjal phrad
yod tsam byas/ 'dar la gnam gshegs rin cen dpal bzang po'i gsol 'debs kyi tshogs dbu la yongs bsngo ba smon lam ci shes kyis rgyas btab/ de nas cho 'phrul chen po'i tshes
bco lnga la tshar chen bla ma nyid ayon bla ma dang mjal ba'i gnas cha lung rdo rje'i brag rdzong gi rje btsun grags pa'i sgrub phug nang du zla ba lhag tsam gyi bar
la bla ma drag po'i mtshams bcad rgya shin tu dam par rang zhig byas pa'i zhag nyi shu rtsa gcig song ba'i tho rengs kyi dus su thun gyi skabs la gnyid du song ba'i rmi
lam na/ cha lung gi brag sogs 'di thams cad zangs zhun ma ltar ram padma rA ga ltar dmar ding nge ba'i dbus na ri smug po mchong 'dra ba rtse gnam la snyog pa lta bu zhig
'dug /de'i rtse nas bltas pas gnam sa thams cad 'ja' tshon du khra shig shig 'dug /ri de'i rtse na gu ru rdo rje gro lod yin zer ba'i khro bo smug nag mi bzad pa 'jigs su
rung ba ni nam mkha'i khams la gzhal ba zhig byas 'dug /res 'ga' ni ri de

yang lha der 'gro/ res 'ga' lha de yang rir 'gro ba snyam byed pa yang sngar ltar 'dug pa res 'ga' nga rang ri 'di yin zer de yang bdag la thim pa snyam byed pa dang / yang
ri de'i rtse nas bltas pas rigs drug gi gnas kyi dbyibs mang po 'dug pa 'ga' zhig nyi zla ltar gsal ba'i mdangs 'dug /'ga' zhig ni mun khrod kyi gseb na mar me lta bu'i
'od phran bu dang / 'ga' zhig ni na bun gyi gseb na bun long long byed pa dang / 'ga' zhig ni phyogs bcur shig shig 'gro ba zhig 'dug pa dang / lha de dang ri de la kha dog
sna tshogs kyi 'ja' bun bun 'phro ba zhig 'dug pas/ e ma sangs rgyas kun 'dus ayon bla ma'i thugs rje sems can gyi don la rgyun chad med par gzigs par 'dug /bdag kyang
ayon bla ma'i rjes 'jug 'khor ba spong 'dod yin pas bdag dang bdag la ltos pa'i mthong thos dran reg thams cad zangs mdog dpal rir tshe gcig la ayon nyid kyi zhal mthong
gsung thos par skye bar shog snyam pa'i smon lam rgyas par btab/ yus kyi brnangs pa lta bu byas gnyid sad byung bas bar chad dam dngos grub gang yin kyang dgod bro 'khrul
pa rgya 'byams pa'i rmi lam la gang yang 'char gyin gda'o/ /gang ltar bla ma yi dam 'di nyid la zla ba tsam gyi bsnyen pa dang zhag bdun sogs bcad pa'i bsnyen pa dang /
lo tsam gyi bsnyen pa dang des mtshon pa'i dge sbyor thun bzhi 'di da lta yan la ma chag pa byas 'di'i gsang sngags bye ba gcig dang 'bum phrag phyogs kyis bsgyur ba tsam
song yang bza' btung 'di nyid ro zas kho na la longs spyod byas

pas g.yang sa chen po gda'o/ /de nas don du gnyer ba kha cig la rdo rje nag po chen po'i gsang 'khrid thun mong ma yin pa smin rgyas su byas/ de'i 'khrid kyi rgyab rten mkha'
'gro lha dgu'i rjes gnang byas dus/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams pas ye shes dbab pa'i tshe slob ma rnams g.yo 'gul med pa dang / gang de'i lha tshogs thams cad kyi
thugs ka nas 'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba dang / de rnams 'ja' tshon me long gi gzugs ltar rgyun ring yod pa'i zil byung / gang ltar de grol nas rdo rje phag mo'i rnam
sprul yin zhu ba'i cha lung sgrub chen ma dang mjal/ ne gu dang phyag chen sogs kyi gleng mo rgyas po byung / 'dar nas mi dbang sku mched kyang khor pa byon byung bas lugs
gnyis kyi dpal 'byor rgyas par spel/ rtser yong dgos kyi bka' dang bstun tshe dbang sogs kyi thugs bzhed bsgrubs/ shar lam don grub gling du phyin dpon sa sras mo de nyid
cung zad bsnyel gyin 'dug pas tshe dbang rjes gnang sogs gang shes thugs bzhed bsgrubs kyang dad pa nam mkha'i mtha' las ring ba zhig 'dug pas phan thogs yong ba ni dka'
snyam pa byung bas de ga thog tu babs song / gang ltar gzhis len sogs bzabs ma gnang / de nas rim pas chos lung du sleb/ zla skor tsam bsdad slar 'dar stod pho brang du
yongs/ zla ba bzhi tsam gyi bar la mi dbang sku mched kyis gtsos pa'i skal pa bzang po mang dag la/ rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud dbang lung / mgon po'i phyi nang
gsang gsum gyi 'khrid/ rjes gnang lung dmar po

skor gsum gyi rjes gnang lung sogs thugs bzhed gang nus bsgrubs/ snyan brgyud kyi bdag por mnga' gsol chos dang 'jig rten gyi 'dod rgu gya nom pa byung ba lags so/ /sngar chos
lung du gsung ngag rin po che zhig 'chad snyam dam tshig gso ba sogs bsnyen pa zla ba tsam byas/ de nang du rmi lam na rje bla ma tshar chen nyid sngon du gsung ngag
rin po che gnang ba'i dus su lam zab gnang ba'i skabs kyi sku gzi brjid dang zhal 'dzum pa dang na bza' sogs ji lta ba mdzad nas/ khyod kyis bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba
lhur blangs nas snyan brgyud thun mong ma yin pa bstan pa yongs rdzogs kyi zab chos 'di nyid rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i gnas su 'chad par gyis shig gsung byung ba dang gnyid
sad byung bas/ de lta bu'i bla ma dang mjal gsung gi bdud rtsi zab mo thos pa'i dus kyang byas snyam mchi ma mang du shor/ tshe rabs kun tu gdul bya'i zhing khams su skye
ba dang skye ba de nas kyang rjes su 'dzin pa zhig snyam pa'i gsol ba phur btsugs su btab/ rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i gnas ni/ chos ldan gyi rgyal pos bde bar sa skyong
ba phyi nang gi 'tshe ba dang bral ba'i gnas su bsam gtan gyi bya ba rtsoms gsung 'dug pas/ gnas de lta bu gzhan ma ni gang na'ang med 'dug /phun sum tshogs pa'i gnas de
kun lugs gnyis kyi khrims kyi kha lo ba nged rang kha'u brag rdzong pa'i bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa'i sbyin bdag chos rgyal pho brang 'dar rnam par rgyal ba'i rtse
mor tshang ba nas der 'chad snyam pa'i zhe bcad byas/ gdong dga' chos sder rje btsun kun dga' mchog ldan

zhabs drung du lam dbang sogs kyi 'dod chos phran bu zhus/ rtse nas gzhis len phran bu byung / rgyus med kyi chos skad chal chol gyi dri ba 'dra mdzad kyin 'dug /de nas gzhung
pa smad tsho'i yul par spyi dbang dang kha 'bar ma'i bzlog pas rim gro bsgrubs/ de nas gsung ngag gi cha rkyen gang yod khyer nas yongs/ rang lo nga brgyad pa sprel lo
zla ba dang po'i tshes lnga la gsung ngag btsugs pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgyas pa nged rang gis bsgrubs/ rgyal po gnyis kyis dbu mdzad 'bangs brgyad cu tsam gyi skal pa
can rnams zla ba drug gi bar la gsung ngag rin po che slob bshad gsung las ji ltar thos pa sba bsri med par smin rgyas su bskyangs/ brda ston gsal ba sogs kyi zur bka'
thor bu byas/ de skabs zla ba gsum tsam song ba'i bskyed rim gyi mngal 'byin pa'i dmigs pa gal gnad shin tu che ba zhig gi dus su/ the tshom cung zad yod pa zhig byung ba
de de nub tho rangs kha'i dus su rmi lam na/ zhabs drung rje'i zhu sna mdzad rje btsun tshar chen dang sngon gyi gzhi bsnyen skabs su phebs pa'i bla ma yab sras rnams zhal
'dzum lta bar mi bzod pa lta bu'i dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur ji snyed gnang / de nas sngon gyi bla ma nyid kyis skad cig la spyan nam mkhar khrir gzigs pa dang dpa' bo dang
mkha' 'gro yin zhu bas char sprin lhags pa ltar 'ja' tshon khra lam me ba zhig byas song / de nas bdag gi dogs pa phran bu 'di sel ba zhig zhu snyam pas/ e ma legs pa'i
lam la legs so zhes/ /de ga yin pas bka' stsal mi dgos te/ /logs su yod pa'i

'bras bu til tsam med/ /blo gros ldan pa khyod la ci zhig dgos/ /gsung ba zhig gnyid khong du zin de nas me long la has btab pa ltar yal ba dang gnyid sad/ e ma ngas 'di lta
bu'i lam tshang la ma nor ba thos nas lan sprad pa lta bu la'ang thugs dges dges gnang ba ni bstan pa nyams dma' bar 'dug snyam pa'i blo la 'khu 'phrig chen po dang dad
pa'i dpal 'bar ba'i dga' spro dang snying chu mig sngar 'bab pa lhan cig byung / bsams tsa na nga rang skal ba bzang snyam pa'i blo bde phugs su tshud ltos bcas kun kyang
lugs gnyis bya ba phra rags gang la'ang bgegs kyi mtshan ma mi 'byung ba zhig lags/ rdzogs rim gyi skabs lha sa nas yongs pa'i btsun pa zhig la stod du hags pa'i rnam pa
yod tsam byung ba la gegs sel gyi rnam pa mang dag yod mod/ gsung ngag brgyud pa'i bla ma'i mtshan nas thos te rkang pa mgo bo la bsnun pas 'phral du dwangs pa zhig byung
/ gegs med du mthar phyin te tshogs gtor dang longs spyod kyi 'dod rgu ni lha'i dpal 'byor la 'gran bdo ba tsam byung / gang ltar sde 'khrug mi bzad pa zhig byung ba nas
chos lung la phyin/ ser ma nas don grub rdo rje sde srid bkra shis stobs rgyas drung spyan drangs/ thog ma ni byus 'gro bla na med kyi grabs 'dug pas dpon g.yog gdong
dga' ba la bka' skyon gyi rnam par phebs dus/ phyag 'bul la phyin dges dges kyi zhal ta kha re phebs/ bdag rkyen bla med gnang / rting ma khong tsho'i byus ni nam mkha'i
glog ltar yal/ lha sa gzhung pa sogs go nang la gtad/ chos lung de

nyid byang nas zhal ngo rags rim gyis spyi mchod rang tshugs thub nges su bzhag 'dug pa dang / lhag par 'dar nas la blo gtad bcol chos lung la gzhung pa rnams kyi rgyud dngos
gang 'dug bskyas/ byang dpung gdong du dgon par dar 'dzugs dang srung ba la yong dgos zhus pas spyi mchod kyi phyag dam rnams ston long med par bcom pa la blo rtse gtad/
lhag par grogs byed pa dang blo gtad bcol ba'i 'dar nas kyi blon pos phyi ma nang byas te/ dgon pa'i thad nas gus bsub thes med pa mi sngon du mi thegs pa rang yang srog
thar ba la rgya chags pa zhig byung ste/ kun gyis mthong zhing myong ba de ga ma gtogs yi ger bkod pas zag pa 'phel ba las mi 'dug go /de phyogs kyi gnas tshul ni de ltar
du mchis so/ /'phrang bu brgyud nas mang mkhar phu bskor te nged rang 'dar du sleb tsam byung / de nas gzhung sa skya ser tsho'i gseb nas ngo log byed mi yin zer ba'i
mi kha yar thang ror btang / de la brten pa'i byang la khor tsam phyin lugs gnyis kyi khrel gzhung dam tshig thams cad rgyab tu bor ba'i dpon zhen pa'i zhu ba la/ gong nas
snyan grol ba'i gshis tshul phran bu byung kyang bden rdzun ni go ngal ba'i rgyu las med snyam ma bris/ tshur log 'dar du rang gi bsam gtan khang bur bsdad/ chos rgyal
chen po lha rtser phebs pa dang mjal phrad la phyin/ lugs gnyis kyi gnang skyong phul du phyin pa gnang / 'dod pa'i don ma lus pa stsal ba zhig byung ba yin no/ /de'i ston
gzhug zhing gshegs rin po che dpal bzang po'i phyi rten gyi zhal bkod

dpon sa a mdzes rgyal mos gnang ba'i rmang lding ba mdzad pa'i 'og tu 'di lta bu byed dgos phebs pas/ bstan pa rin po che spyi sgos la bsam pa dang / lhag par bod 'bangs spyi
dang sbyin pa'i bdag po'i sku rim la dmigs nas/ 'gong po spun dgu dam sri spun dgu/ bsen mo spun dgu sogs bod 'bangs phung bar byed ba'i mi min thams cad dus gcig tu mnan
pa'i phyir/ ri khrod dgon pa nyid du sgrub pa zhag bdun byas/ zhag bzhi song ba'i dgongs thun gyi dgug gzhug byas pas/ de dag kun gyi ngo bor gyur pa'i phug ron guu ma
zhig khras bdas te de nyid du lhags byung bas yang yang bstim nas yid ches par byas/ bsnyen pa'i sgrub pa'i rtags mngon sum du grub ste grol ba dang / mnan pa'i mtshams
su sleb byung bas rim pas de nub skyed mos tshal du phyin/ de nyin rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po tshar pa chos rje'i chos kyi khri la mkhas btsun yongs kyi gtsug rgyan dpal
mang du thos pa klu sgrub rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas mngon par mtho ba'i khri la bkod pa gnang / de nub de rnams kyi bar chad zhi phyir dang lhag par bod kyi yul gru thams
cad dang sbyin pos gtsos pa'i sa phyogs 'di nyid du chos dang 'jig rten gyi dar rgyas 'byor ba la bar du gcod pa thams cad lhan cig tu mnan pas/ chos byed kyi tshul rab
'byams gnad du 'gro ba dang / 'jig rten pa kun kyang rdzogs ldan gyi bskal pa ltar bde bar rgyu ba 'di yin no/ /sang snga bar bla brang du phyag 'bul dang bstan pa rgyas
pa'i dga' ston spel phyir mkhan zhabs drung du sleb/ lugs gnyis kyi

brtse skyong dges dges ci yang gnang / snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas pa'i legs tshogs mang dag bsgrig pa gnang 'dug pas sems la dga' spro nyi ma shar
ba lta bu'i gsal cha thob pa zhig byung / de nas rang lo nga dgu pa bya la ri khrod kun gyi mthar thug pho brang nyid dang khad nye ba'i sa/ dgon pa spe'u zhes bsam gtan
gyi nyams rtogs gong 'phel du 'gro ba zhig bdog pa der gsung ngag rin po che'i lam phyi ma rnams kyi 'khrid zla ba lhag tsam gyi bar la snod ldan gyi slob bu kha yar la
smin rgyas su bskyangs/ tshe 'di'i mdun 'jug sogs kyi g.yeng ba med pas ci byas chos su 'gro ba zhig yod pas skyid pa'i mthar thug byung lags so/ /de nas rtser bsdad pho
brang gi ltag tu mchod rten khang bu brtsegs pa zhig brtsig pa gnang / de'i rmang gi 'og tu yul phyogs 'di nyid kyi bde skyid dpal 'byor la glags lta ba thams cad ji lta
bu'i gzugs 'gros la bstim pa'i sgrub pa dang mnan pa sogs yid ches pa zhig byas pas de dang de 'dra'i rtags ngo mtshar ba du ma yod kyang spro ba'i 'os min pas gsal bar ma
mngon no/ /de'i ston kha lha rtser khor tsam phyin de nas dgun chos steng du gdong dga' ba dang bzlos pa'i rtsod par phyin/ thog ma ni nor dang mkhas phyug kho na'i dbang
du song nas rgyal po'i khrims nyid kyang gzhong ba'i nang du chu khur ba ltar byed pa zhig 'dug /slar bdag btsun pa'i khungs su song bas don med kyi bya ba sgrub pa kho
nar 'dug kyang / rdzun gyi 'gro sar dang sbubs kyi 'khyogs 'gros gnang na mi rung / bden

rdzun 'byed pa rgyal po'i khrims sa yin pas srog la ltos pa med bden na dang ma bden na byas dmod dmod yang cung zad btsugs pas khong rnams go gnad la gtad 'dug /nam mkha'i
mtha' la bskrad snyam pa byung / yang nged rang gi lha mo 'di nyid ma mnyes pa'i rtags du ma zhig 'dug pa dang / khong rnams kyi pho lhar mches nas khams kyang bde rgyu
med pa'i bsreb se ba zhig byung bas/ lag na ci yod thams cad chos sde nyid du spungs/ khrims de'ang de tshul du go bas su la'ang ltos pa med par log yongs bas khams kyang
bde mus su dwangs/ de nas rdzong nyid du ci bder bsdad pa'i skabs su bsam grub dgon gsar byed dgos gsung pa'i bka' dang kho rang tsho'i skya ser rgan pa 'dra dang bcas nan
chags byung kyang nan grol zhus/ de snga yang zhabs drung mkhan drung du zhu bya phul 'dug pa slar yang de ka nan phul mdzod/ bdag lta bu'i khyer nus kyis dgon pa 'dzin
skyong byed pa'i blo gros can zhig ye man zhus pas ma bzlog par khas blangs/ chos lung la khor pa tsam zhig phyin/ slar rtser khams pa 'dra dang zhag ngo 'bangs du ma la
chos 'dod kyi re ba thams cad mthar phyin par bskang ba dang / zhal ngo rnams la dpal padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i 'chi med tshe'i rdzong chung gi tshe dbang
phul bas dngos gzhir sleb tsam na tshe chang de chil le lud byung bas sde pa che sa nas kyis lud pa tshad ma bzhes song bas sku tshe'i bar chad zhi zhing gong 'phel du byung
ba yin no/ /de nas drug cu pa khyi lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes lnga la dgon gsar bde ba can zhes

grub mchog thang stong rgyal po'i zhal slob rje btsun blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi zhabs khri la bkod/ mi dbang sku mched gnyis kyang phebs/ bkod ja dang gnang sbyin sogs kyi
legs tshogs mang dag gnang / gzhan yang grang chen spyi sa nas bzung mchod yon gyi khul nas rten 'brel gyi legs lam mdzad mkhan ji snyed pa dang / ja bzang gi btung ba dbyar
mtsho ltar chal chil du gnas pa la longs spyod cing zhag lnga bsdad/ skya ser gyi khrod nas de snga yan ston ser gyi dus rgan gzhon dar babs kyi tshe 'dir gnas gzhis
'dzin pa la gces 'dzin gyi mi 'dra dang / chos pa'i khungs nas kyang de mtshungs glang 'thabs sam pho gzer gyis rkyen byas te/ 'phral du 'chi bdag grong du rings par 'gro
ba zhig 'dug pas de la phan pa dag kyang srid snyam pa dang / lhag par phyi nang gi mchod yon gyi legs tshogs gong 'phel du rgyas pa'i phyir/ mi dmangs la tshe rta bcas
pa'i dbang rgyas pa byas/ de phyin nas bzung da lta'i bar du gong smos pa'i 'phral rkyen de'i rgyun chad nas ma byung bas dgod bro snyam pa byung / des mtshon yul phyogs
der phan pa rgya cher byung ba mang dag yod mod/ thams cad bris na mang bas 'jigs nas ma spros/ chos sde nyid na rje shes rab bkra shis pa'i lo dus kyi mchod pa'i rgyun dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo'i mchod pa yang dag mdzad pa dang thug pas mang ja sogs kyi bsnyen bkur phran pa byas/ slar rtser bsdad nas khams pa kha re dang chos 'dod kyi don gnyer
mang po la nyin mtshan dal med byas re ba bskang / sde pa'i sku rim dang

sems can gyi don rab 'byams ci nus byas/ ri khrod nyid dang dgon gsar chos lung sogs su lo gnyis tsam bsdad/ mdor na chos ldan gyi bya ba gang yod ma gtogs 'jig rten gyi re
ba med pas skyid pa'i rang ngo shes pa zhig byung / de nas glang lo re gsum pa la rgyal ba gnyis pa rje btsun rdo rje 'chang bka' drin mnyam med mkhyen brtse'i drung gi
sku'i dpon dang chos kyi bur gyur pa'i dbon rin po che phebs/ chos 'di 'dra dgos gsung pa rgya mon gyi gnas tshul yin pas 'bul nus pa'i na ma med zhus pas ma gsan/ 'on kyang
rje btsun nyid kyi gzigs pa la khrel ba byung na mi rung snyam len sprod pa la dang len byas/ zla ba gsum pa la dbon nyid dgon gsar du bzhugs/ bdag gis mtsho sgo rnam
rgyal gling la phyin/ sde par thugs bzhed yod pa'i dbang rjes gnang sogs ci grub byas/ sku rim la gshin rje gshed kyi las tshogs bzhi yod pa'i nang nas gtor ma'i las tshogs
drug cu rtsa bzhi'i gtor bzlog cig byas skabs/ phyag len rnams la ngor pa'i dkyus ma rnams dang cung mi 'dra ba snyan brgyud zhal shes kyis brgyan nas byas pas skyon
'dzin 'dod pa'i rang mthong can mang po gda' ste khong brgyud chad pa'i pi wang ltar gyur to/ /de nas mgyogs bskor byas dgon gsar du sleb/ tshur lam mtsho bar brgyud nas
'ongs pas ma rung rkyen ngan du mas gar byed pa'i gangs dbar glang gling gi stongs la srung ma'i dbang po gur mgon nyid kyi sprul pa'i pho nya ru 'dren dang bcas pas mngon
sum lta bur bsu ba byung zhing / gsol ja pa g.yu rgyal sogs

skyel mi mang dag yod pa kun gyis bya nag zung sprel gyi lding skor gshog sgyur byed pa skad kyi rnam pa mang dag byed pa sogs bdag la dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur byed pa mthong bas
khong rnams mgrin gcig tu bgros pa la mgon po'i phebs bsu yin pa 'dug zer ba yang byung / gang ltar de nas bzung dbon drung la zla ba brgyad kyi bar la 'jig rten gyi zhabs
tog lhod med dang / phyag g.yog rnams la'ang 'dod rgu gang 'byor byas kyang re 'dod khengs pa zhig ma byung / gang ltar chos kyi thugs bzhed nyin mtshan dal med phul
bas thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa'i ngang la mdzad/ lhag par phebs pa'i dus sku tshe'i rten 'brel legs tshogs spel ba'i phyir 'chi med lcags kyi sdong po'i tshe dbang zhig
phul bas/ lo rgyus dang dngos gzhi'i mtshams su sleb pa tsam nas tshe chang nyid chil li lud byung bas byin mangs bzhes song / byin la ril bu byas phyag tu yod pas sku tshe'i
bar chad thams cad zhi zhing gong 'phel du 'gro ba'i rten 'brel mang dag 'grig song / de nas dpon slob rnams shar la thegs/ rang yang snang zos ci bder bsdad/ de nas
re bzhi pa stag lor ri khrod du bsam gtan gong 'phel byas bsdad skabs sa bdag klu nyid khros pa'i rims mi zad pa 'brum pa de 'gom thor ba 'dug /bsam 'grub mthong smon pa
zhes pa'i byis pa zhig la byung bas/ yul dang sde pa nas spyugs pa'i dgongs pa gnang ba la/ thog mar byung ba 'di shin tu yang ba zhig kyang yong / lhag par cha zhabs su
byung ba la ming bkra yang shis pa 'dug bas ma

spyugs pa dga'a'am zhus pas/ mi ser rgan pa 'dras phugs byas nas spyugs song bas rting ma bya thabs med pa la ya nga ba zhig byung song / mtsho sgo nas rnam dpyod kyi bum pa
mkha' la 'gran pa sbyin bdag cig la drin che ba dpon sa khye'u 'dren byas/ 'brum bu 'di la phos na dga'a'am ma 'dzems par sngos bsdad na dga'/ brtag pa byas pa'i gsal dgos
phebs pas/ lar yang thog mar byung ba 'di dga' ba dang / ched don brtag pa'i 'bras bu sngos par dga' bas dgongs spyod mdzod zhus pas/ de ga dang len mdzad song bas skyon
med du dwangs 'dug /rtser sku rim la car mar bsdad/ dge sbyor gang 'phel dang srung 'khor sogs rim pas gang nus bsgrubs/ yos bu re lnga pa zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes
bco lnga la shing mang dgon par zhal ngo tshang ma 'brum 'bros gnang / de'i sku rim sogs la bdag gis kyang phyin/ zla ba bzhi tsam rtse gcig tu drag sngags rgyun bzlas dang
rgyang grags tshun la srung ba'i sbyor ba byas pas gnyen 'brum klu nad kyis nye ma nus par bde bar thar pa yin no/ /de nas dpon sa yum chen cung zad bsnyel bas de'i phyag
phyir rtser yong 'phral rkyen de yang rim pas dwangs/ bdag gis dgon gsar du sleb/ mtsho sgo nas yongs dgos nan chags byung bas zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes gsum la phyin/
de nub grang so gzim mkhar du bsdad/ drung chen des gzhis len phran bu byas/ sang snga bar phyin bsu ba sogs gzabs ma dang bcas sleb zla ba drug tsam bsdad/ sde pa dang dge
bshes mang dag la rA 'khrid sogs smin

rgyas su phul/ gzhan dbang rjes gnang ji snyed pas thugs bzhed bskang / de skabs rang nyid la mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa'i skal pa can dge ba'i thugs stobs sngon rabs kyi
rgyal po rnams dang mtshungs pa rgyal ba dgyes pa'i thabs ma gyur 'gro ba'i don la gcig tu dpa' ba dbyangs can lha mo'i rnam par 'phrul pa dpon sa khye'u 'dren gyis bskul
nas rgyu rkyen phun sum tshogs pa spungs pa la brten/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po nyon mongs rang grol gyi steng nas skye bdun sgrub pa zhag bdun byas/ skal pa bzang po'i
dpon slob lha grangs dang mnyam pa bcu gcig gis thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor la brtson pa dang / gzungs thag 'dzin pa dang / gzhan yang gzungs rgyun 'dzin pa dang / skor ba
byed pa'i mi brgyad cus gzungs dang bcas te sgrub khog nas bshad pa'i sgrub bzhi ma tshang ba med par byas nas zla ba drug pa'i tshes bdun la btsugs te tshes bcu'i mchod
pa rgyas par bsgrubs/ thog mar ril bu 'go 'dzugs tsam la rang nyid khams cung zad nyog pa zhig byung bas 'byung po mi ma yin rnams kyis bar chad kyis glags lta bar go /de
la dmigs bla ma drag po'i bskyed rim bzung ste gdon rigs tshar gcod pa'i sdig pa nag po'i zas skal du sprad pas dus de nyid du zhi ba zhig dang / dam sri mnan pa'i skabs
su 'jig rten phung byed thams cad gnon pa'i dong gru gsum de la rgya bcus gdab pa'i skabs su bro brdung pas rkang pa g.yas kyi mthe bong la cung zad kyi gnod pa byung ba
mtshon cha sna lnga'i rtse la skyon nas gtubs/

gnyis med ye shes kyi 'ob tu gnod byed thams cad bcug pas rang dwangs su song / zhag gsum song ba'i dgong thun gyi dus de snga yan char shin tu dkon pa sa bon rnams kyang skams
par thug pa tsam dang mi rnams nyam thag pa'i skabs kyis skyo bar 'dug pas/ bdag gis 'phags mchog spyan ras gzigs dbang la ra mda' bos te/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
rgyas kyi rgyud las/ mtha' bzhi gangs kyis bskor ba'i rwa ba ru/ /sbas pa'i rnal 'byor me long 'dzin pa 'byung / /zhes pa'i gu ru rin po che chos kyi dbang phyug gi
mgur gyi bum pa las byung ba'i gdangs kyi yi ge drug pa'i ra mda' sgrub po thams cad lag sbrel nas dkyil 'khor khang pa la bskor bzhin pas bos pas dus de nyid du/ 'phags
pa'i spyan gyis 'dzam gling klu rnams bskul bas thugs rje'i byin rlabs kyi char rgyun de nas bzung nyin zhag sbrel nas babs pas skye 'gro thams cad bde ba'i go skabs thob
pa zhig byung bas/ lha mi thams cad dga' ba'i rtags su de nub rmi lam na bu mo gzhon nu mdzes shing brjid pa gsum gyis dgyes pa'i 'dzum dang bcas nas lha'i me tog dkar po
dang / ras dkar po dang spos dkar po dang / dkar gangs shel dkar ltar dwangs pa dang dung dkar g.yas su 'khyil ba zhig rnams sbyin/ bdag la mgo bo btsugs nas bsdad pa dang
gnyid sad/ ci yin nam snyam pas sang snga thun gyi steng du dpon sa nyid kyis ja bzang gi btung ba dang bcas char pa'i byin rlabs bka' drin che zhes rmi lam na byung
ba'i 'bul ba rnam grangs gsum tsam dang bcas pa byung bas/ dur khrod ma gsum de

yang dgyes pa'i rtags su nges/ gang ltar zhag bzhi song nas dri bzang gis rdzong chen gang ba dang / zhag lnga song nas srod la gzungs rgyun sgra cher mi 'dug pas yid kyi bskor
ba dang gzungs rgyun nan cher bgrangs pas rig pa mi non pa tsam zil bun ne ba 'dug pas dkyil 'khor khang pa la dbang gi ma bdun nyid kyis bskor ba dang gnyan chen po
thang lha de nyid bar chad kyi bdud 'dul ba la dpa' ba byas 'dug /sgrub grogs rnams kyang 'ur langs nas gzungs sgra cher byed pa byung / gang ltar sgrub dbang rgyas par
phul/ mtshan ma rdzas kyi rdul tshon rnams chags kyang sa la dkyil 'khor gyi bkrag ma nyams par yod cing gegs med du grol/ grub rtags gzhung nas bshad pa'i 'phel rgyas thog
ma byung ba dang / ril bu de nyid myong bas grol ba'i mtshan ma thob pa yin no/ /da lta'i bar du yang byin rlabs thum bu rnams la 'phel rgyas yong nges dang / sangs rgyas
kyi 'phel gdung rgyun ma chad pas ril bu rgyun la ring bsrel mthong bas grol ba dang bcas pa yod do/ /zla ba bcu pa'i nang du dgon gsar du sleb/ zhag kha yar ngal gsos
te/ de nas chos lung la khor tsam phyin/ de lo phyi mar 'gro ba'i rmi lam ngan pa 'dra dang ltas log pa phran bu 'dug pas dgon gzhis kyi gnyer ba rnams bzhag /bsgrubs kyang
mi 'grub pa'i dgon gzhis chos byed kyi gang zag gsha' ma med pa'i gnas bor nas/ re drug pa 'brug lo rang nyid dben pa'i ri khrod du 'chi ba mi bsgug na khyod la byed
rgyu ci 'dug ma Ni bsnyen mtshams bcad rgya

dam po byas bsdad/ bdog pa'i dngos po thams cad dam pa dge 'dun gyi phyag tu phul ba 'og tu 'chad/ de nas rje btsun dbon drung dang / chos rje byams pa shAkya blo gros/ chos
rje ngag dbang pa/ chos rje dkon mchog legs 'dzin sogs kyis dbu mdzad khams pa'i slob bu gsum tsam dang bcas pa'i chos 'dod thams cad so sor tshim par byas/ skabs 'gar
rtser yang phyin/ yi dam 'ga' re'i dkyil 'khor du sgrub mchod bdag 'jug brgya tshar sogs mang po byas kyang gong du brjod zin/ re bdun pa sbrul lo yang de skabs dang mtshungs
pa'i dge sbyor 'phel la bla ma dgyes pa'i thabs la yid ches thon pa zhig byung / 'on kyang dgon gsar na rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi nyer gcig gi sgrub mchod skabs
mtsho sgo nas dpon sa shin tu bsnyel ba yod pas yong dgos zhes nan tar dang / yum chen drung gis 'gro dgos nan chags byung bas sgrub mchod kyang bor/ mgyogs bshad rang
phyin/ de nub gzims mkhar du bsdad/ 'jam dpal zhal dgu'i rgyud sogs kyi be bum bskur nas de 'phral go chod kyi mi btang / de dang lhan cig tu bstan srung rgya mtsho'i gtso
bo 'chi bdag gshin rje gshed de yang rgyud kyi rjes 'brengs nas be bum sleb 'phral dngos su bar chad kyi mtshan ma thams cad skad cig la zhi nas bde khyad yod nges byung
'dug /sman pa dang kho rang tsho'i mchod 'os rnams kyis mi mi yong bar thag bcad 'dug mod/ bdag sleb nas snyung ba ni srung ma dang be bum gyi byin rlabs kyis grol 'dug
/rkang pas dbu la bzhag pa tsam byas zhag gsum song nas sor chud/ sman pa sogs cung

zad bskyengs pa lta bus dad gus tshad med mdzad pa byung / de nas dpon sa/ sde pa chos rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa dang bshes gnyen dad gus mang po la nA ro mkha' spyod
kyi zab chos ma lus par phul/ dpon sa'i drung gis gser sogs dngos po'i gnang ba dpag med byung / de lo dpon sa nyid der mi bzhugs pa'i gnas tshul lcag bskul sogs gong nas
'di ltar mdzad na mi legs mang dag cig car nas labs pas shin tu ma mnyes/ 'o na ji ltar 'os mkhyen pas gzigs byas/ kha 'jug spangs/ mdzad tshul 'jig rten phyi mo'i dper
gnod pa zhig dang ngos rang la skyon 'gyur cung zad byung song / gang ltar tshur lam bong chu gtsang po zhes chu bo chen po de la bye 'dam shin tu che ba yod pa dang / lhag
par yul de'i gnas bdag thams cad rjes la 'brang dogs mang po 'dug pa khros pa'i tshul gyis chu bo'i 'jing du sleb pa na bdag gi rta de nyid bye mar cung zad bying ba
dang chu de yang rba rlabs dang bcas nye ba na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi nga rgyal bzung chu bo de 'o ma'i bdud rtsir byin gyis brlabs nas gnod byed rnams la byin pas
nged rang la gnod pa lta ci 'khor bcas tshu rol du skyon med du sleb/ de nub sri sham zhes pa'i ne gsing bde mo skyid skyid 'dra ba der bsdad/ dgong thun la zhugs pa tsam
nas char pa'i rgyun yang cher babs/ de nub rmi lam na bud med sngo sangs rgyan sna tshogs kyis spras pa zung zhig ras dkar chu 'dzin gsar pa'i phung po ched du byas pa
lta bu zhig phyag dang bcas phul/ nged la byin rlabs zhu zer bdag la mgo bo btsugs nas cung zad nongs

pa tsam byas nas 'dug /gleng mo zhig byed snyam yod pas zla bo 'dras skad ngan gyis gnyid sad/ mtsho mo baiDUrYa'i mdog ltar gnas pa'i gnas bdag de nyid nged la dga' ba'i rnam
pas rjes la 'brang zhing brtse na'ang gzhan la khros pa'i rnam pa zhig 'dug pas phyis su 'phrin las mi zad pa yong bar go /de nas kyang pher pher gyi mi rigs kha re'i
zhon rta nyal ba sogs gzhi bdag 'brangs pa'i rtags du ma gda'/ de nub rma bya rdzong du bsdad sngar 'dris kyi nang so rgyal ba'i drung gis gzhi len yang dag bka' drin bskyabs/
de nas chos lung gi mchod gzhis gra ma ri snar tsha ba byas/ chang dbon pa zer bas gus pa'i sna len bla med byas/ de nas 'byung bo'i bya ltar rgyu ba'i ma rungs pa'i
skye bo rnams kyi 'dus gro sngon la mal byas yongs pas/ rgyud sde'i bang mdzod bsrung ba'i gnyer kha'o rdo rje legs pa de mtsho sgo na brten bzhin 'dug pas/ de nyid ma
mnyes pa'i rdzu 'phrul sprul pa'i spre'u mi bzad pa zhig rang gi rta gsar de nyid sga stong pa yod pas de la zhon spang thang de la mig gis chod pa tshun la skad cig la
bskor ba kun gyis mthong bas ci bya brtol med du gyur/ bdag gis cho 'phrul de ltar du go /rnam 'phrul mi zad pa du ma zhig gda'/ de nas re brgyad pa rta lo sde pa nas bka'
lung yang yang phebs pa dang dgon pa rang gis kyang nan chags byung bas slar yang dgon gsar byed par byas/ lugs gnyis dam tshig khrel gzhung rgyab tu bor ba kha cig la
gong nas dran 'dzin gyi zhal bkod phran bu gnang / chos sde nyid du bla ma gong ma rnams kyi sgrigs

bca' ba ltar gzhir bcas kyi bca' yig dam khas mnan pa zhig kyang gnang 'dug /sngar nas yod pa'i bla ma so so'i dus chen sogs kyi sgrub mchod rnams la skyabs 'gro nas bkra shis
bar shar sbyangs dang gong 'phel kho na byung / lo dus kyi sa ga zla ba'i smyung gnas gtong ba dang de steng dbang mo che la las slar ma song ba'i tshe rta bcas pa'i
dbang rjes gnang rgyas pa re dang / ston dus dbang mo che re la yang de mtshungs rgyas par byas sems can gyi tshe nyams pa phal che ba gsos par gyur to/ /gzhan yang nged
rang sleb nas dgon pa'i ltag na sngar chu cung zad byung ba'i shul gyi sa der rkang pas phran bu brad pas chu thon nas da lta'i bar du'ang rgyun ma nub par yod/ tshe thar
gyi sems can phran bu bsags pa dgon par rten 'brel ma 'grig /de tsho bzhes spro byed mi rnams la'ang rtags mtshan mngon du gyur pa byung / nged rang rtser bsdad pa'i skabs
shig sngar gyi khams pa de log 'gro ba la blo gtad tshe dbang byed pa'i khungs byas skabs su babs pa dang 'bod mi btang bas lam bar du na nas 'chi la thug /tshe dbang
bzhag 'gro dgos byung bas bdag la ngo sbas se byas 'dug /bla ma'i bskyed rim gsal po zhig bsgoms/ drag sngags kyi mchil ma btab pas 'ding ba dgos pa'i brda byed/ de sprad
pas mgo bo gtums nas cang mi zer ba 'dug /zla bo de sangs pas nga ngo mi shes pa lags sam/ khyed sgyid pa ma skyur bstan pa la gang phan mdzod zer/ khyod su yin/ gang nas
yongs/ 'phrin las gang yin/ yid la ci 'dod bris pas/

he he dam can stong gi sde dpon ayon padma'i bka' sgrub pa'i ma sang rdo rje legs pa drag po mgar ba nag po lags/ gang nas kyang 'ongs/ gang du 'ang 'gro/ bstan pa dang ayon
bla ma'i bka' skyong ma rung dgra bo'i gshed ma bstan dgra sgrol ba'i dmag dpon sa 'dzin chos la dkar ba'i dgra lha/ 'dzam gling chos nor gyi bang mdzod thams cad kyi gnyer
kha'o/ /dam ldan stong gi 'phrin las sgrub pa'i pho nya/ khams gsum skye 'gro'i srog len yin/ yid la ayon gyi bka' ltar sgrub pa'i bshes gnyen ni dkon/ nged bstan srung
rnams la gtor ma ster mkhan ni med/ sems can rnams ni dmyal ba'i rgyu sgrub pa kho na 'dug snyam snying mi dga' zer/ gtor ma ster ba 'phrin las 'chol ba po 'di 'dra yod
byas pas/ de tsho ni ngal ba'i rgyu ma gtogs ci yang med/ da lta sa paN gyi rnam 'phrul ngor pa dkon mchog lhun grub rgya nag ri bo rtse lnga na skyes yod/ khong gis sbyin
