pa nas phran bu bza' ba yod/ kha'u brag rdzong sogs kyi gtor gzhi nas bza' rgyu mi yong pa 'dug pa e yin byas pas de tsho nas kyang med zer/ rje tshar chen dang mkhyen
brtse'i drung gang na bzhugs e mthong byas pas/ bla ma tshar chen ni ma mthong / mkhyen brtse ni zangs mdog dpal ri na bzhugs/ bod la 'byon 'dod 'dug kyang ayon gyis mi
gnang zer/ gzhan yang dgon pa 'di sogs kyi rtsis sprod zer ba'i par pir mang dag 'dug mod/ gang ltar de nas bzung khong gis 'phrin las bsgrub pa dang / bdag gis gtor ma
ster ba'i dam bcas pa sogs mtha' yas pa zhig byung / tshang ma bris kyang ngal ba'i rgyur

zad do/ /de nas re dgu pa lug lo zla ba bcu gcig pa la snga dar gyi gtsug lag khang sras bcas rgyal bas brten pa'i ru lag rgyang gi lha khang la grub pa mchog gi 'khor lo sgyur
ba thang stong rgyal po'i dbon rje ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa'i drung gis zhig gsos gnang zhing grub pa'i rten rnams la rab gnas mnga' gsol la yong dgos gsungs nas
phyin/ tshes bcu'i mchod pa dang bstun cho ga yang bsam yas su ayon nyid kyis mdzad pa ltar rgyal ba mchog dbyangs la gnang / de nyid kyi skye mtha' sprul sku tshe brtan
rgyal mtshan gyi mon chu sbug gi mkha' 'gro lA se gar byed pa 'dra ba'i gsang gnas nas spyan drangs pa'i bde legs lhun grub kyi steng nas tshul bzhin du byas/ zhi khro yongs
rdzogs kyi mnga' dbul grub 'phral nged rang rig pa mi non pa'i zil bun ne byas pa zhig byung bas rig pa mnan pas ayon bla ma mkhyen no snyam pa byas pas rten gtso'i
gtsug nas 'od kyi rnam pa khra bun ne ba zhig byung / me tog rgyas par gtor/ spyi sgos kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam rgya cher btab/ nged rang gis rab ston rgya cher bsgrubs/
de nas slar ri khrod du ci bder gnas skabs nas zhal ngo rnams la dbang rjes gnang sku srungs kyi 'khor lo sogs rgyas par bsgrubs/ sprel lo bdun cu pa zla ba gnyis
pa la mtsho sgo la khor tsam phyin mgyogs skor byas ri khrod du sleb/ rje btsun mkhan drung sku khams shin tu bsnyel ba zhig 'dug zer/ de thos nas sems la bde ba'i go skabs
ma byung ba dang / lhag par dam pa nyid mi bzhugs pa'i ltas du ma

'dug pa nas ji ltar drag snyam pa byung / gzhan ma ni bdag lta bu la gleng sa med/ cung zad smos kyang yid ches kyi gnas bral/ 'on kyang phran bu zhig 'jig rten gyi mes po
dam pa rje 'di nyid sogs la mi phyed pa'i dad pa can skyid mo gshongs pa dar chen pa la/ rje nyid kyi phyag na ci yod kyi rgyu dngos rnams phyed mar btang ba'i cha gcig chos
sde chen po sogs kun la gnang na bla ma rin po che zhing khams mi brje ba bdag gis khag theg /de ltar ma gnang na da lo mi bzhugs pa 'dug go byas pas/ rang nyid rgyal
ba'i bstan pa dang / bstan 'dzin gyi dam pa la lhag bsam dad pa ltar kun la yong ba dka' ba dang / rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang lhag par snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa dpal kha'u
brag rdzong pa'i bstan pa nyams pas kun kyang blun/ de nas 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi nyer gcig mchod kyi sgrub mchod la dgon gsar du phyin/ sgrub mchod kyi sta gon grol skabs/
sde pa lhun chen drung gis skyabs mgon dam pa zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i gshis tshul ngan pa'i phyag dam gsol 'debs kyi rten gnang srung 'khor ched gtad dgos tshul gyi
gtam sleb pa na snying mi dga'/ thos pa bas kyang ba spu ldang / e ma snyigs dus kyi bstan pa nyams pas sems can gyi bde skyid ma lus par rdzogs 'dug go /de 'phral sgrub
mchod pa rnams la thos mchod kyi mang ja ci yod sgrub/ sde par dam pa de nyid ma bzhugs phyin gsol 'debs la 'bung ba ma gtogs thugs ngal gyi rgyur 'gro ba spu tsam mi gnang
ba zhu/ lar yang mchod yul gong ma nyid ma bzhugs pa'i rjes la sbyin bdag gtso bo la ngan

pa zhig yong bzhin 'dug pas thugs rtog zhib lon zhu/ 'dir yang srung 'khor rgyun dang khyad par ci 'grub byed pa yong phul/ de grub nas ri khrod du ci bder bsdad/ zla ba drug
pa'i nang du gdong dga' bas khog zhugs kyi rnam pas rje bla ma kun dga'i drung du a gho ra nag pos nyi bar brten pa'i gnas sgron mo lung gi ri khrod du khor tsam phyin/
chos lung bcoms pa'i nus pa sngon du gyur pa nas/ khyod kyis bshags pa len dgos chos sder mang ja 'gyed sogs bsgrubs chog pa dgos gsungs nas bla ma'i bka' stsal byung ba
na/ srung ma rnams la gtor bsngo sogs kyi mjug tu bstan pa dang rnal 'byor la sdang ba rnams la 'phrin bcol yod pa tsam las dngos brgyud gang nas kyang gnod sems kyi 'khri
ba ci yang med pas mi nus tshig sbyangs zhus pas chog pa dgos zhus/ dmyal bar 'gro ba gnong gis 'gro zer ba rang bden pa 'dra/ gang ltar dam pa'i drung du dam bca' gnyan
po 'dra yod pa kho rang tshos rim pas bshig /lar yang mthu bu lon bzhin du gsher ba zhig 'dug pas/ zhing gi gnas tshang bas sbyor grol zhig dgos rgyur gda'o/ /de nas
zhal ngo rnams sa lud kyi chu tshan 'khor/ /rgyal bu snyan phran bu bsnyel bas rtser phyin 'phral dwangs/ de nas dpon sa'i drung tsho yang sku bde rgyu rang med pa zhig byung
bas srung ma rnams la bskang bshags brgya tshar sogs sku rim la bsdad/ gnam gang la drug cu pa'i bzlog pa zhig byas/ de skabs sde pa chos lhun drung sku khams shin tu
ma bde ba zhig 'dug par shog phebs

bzlog pa 'di dang yang thug sgor ma nas rtags dga' mo rang mi 'dug kyang khor pa phyir/ sngon 'gro rjes 'then gyi rnam pas rten 'brel ma 'grig song ba dang / gong du zhus pa
ltar dam pa nyid mi bzhugs pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis mi dbang de yang ma bzhugs pa zhig byung / de la brten rtser bcar sdod byas bde gshegs de nyid kyi gsol 'debs kyi tshogs
dbu la phyin/ bsngo ba ci shes dang smon lam rgya chen po gdab/ ngos kyi dpon g.yog gi nA ro mkha' spyod kyi tshes bcu'i mchod pa sindhu ra'i sgrub cing mchod pa brgya
tshar tsam dang bcas ci nus su bsgrubs/ de nas ri khrod du snying po yod pa'i bya ba ci yang mi 'dug 'chi ba la phan nges chos mi mtsher ba zhig byed snyam rtse gcig tu dge
sbyor la brtson pa byas/ slar rtser gsol ja zhu ba dang 'dul ba phran bus brgyan nas dbu lo rnams bkrus/ de nas ri khrod du rje ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa/ ngag gi dbang
phyug dga' ba'i bshes gnyen/ gong po rab 'byams pa zung dang bcas pa la spyan ras gzigs/ gur zhal sogs chos 'dod re ba so sor bskang / de grol rgyal po'i gla tshal khrod
du skyo bsang la zhag kha yar bsdad/ rje btsun bla ma'i gdan la dpal ldan grang mo che'i dgon pa byed dgos gsung / zhal ngo dang gra bgres rnams kyis lan cig ma yin
par phebs kyang / chos 'dod kyi skyes bu dam pa yod na ni sngar bstan pa bsams blo nus kyis gang yod byed/ gzhan ma gdan sa byas pa la dgos pa ci yang med/ lhag par sde pa
rang yang mdzad dka' cher 'gro ba min pa med/ nged rang mchod yon da lta'i 'di gas thus

ched du yang rje btsun tshar pa rje'i chos kyi khri la bdag lta bu'i blun po'i rkang pa bzhag pas mi yong bas dgongs pa gnang dgos rtse gcig tu zhus/ na so rgas pa dang dgon
pa la lugs gnyis nas phan pa med nan chags byas kyang ma bzlog bar khas blangs/ pha bla ma'i bstan pa nyams pa'i rtags su nga lta bus bla ma'i gdan sa byed dgos pa bsams
sems skyo ba'i tshad thub pa byung / 'on kyang sngon gyi lung bstan dran pas sems thang chad ba cung zad gsos/ de nas chu tshan la phyin/ tshur lam dgon gsar du zhag kha
re bsdad/ zla ba bcu pa'i tshes lnga la rgyal dang phur bu 'dzom pa'i dus sbyor la/ gsang sngags zab mo'i chos gra rgyun mi 'chad sgrog pa'i gnas mchog bshes gnyen bye
ba chos bzhin spyod bzhin pa'i yang dben dpal grang mo che la chas nas yongs/ grog yod du sde pa khu dbon dpon g.yog du ma phebs bsu bzabs mar bcas nas byon/ bkra shis kha
btags kyi rten gnang gi phyi nang legs tshogs bsgrigs pa gnang / rim pas skyid mo gshongs su sleb/ ja bzang gi btung bas dbang po'i rgyud tshim pa dang bkras dar sogs kyi
rten 'brel mang dag bsgrig pa gnang / dar 'phyar dang ser sbrengs kyi bsu ba bzabs sprod dang bcas/ khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po blo gsal rgya mtsho grags pa rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po'i mngon par mtho ba'i chos kyi khri la bkod/ sde pa che sa nas kyis bkra shis kha btags kyis thog drangs pa'i phun sum tshogs pa'i rten 'brel ma lus pa
rang 'grig tu byung / gong nas bkod ja dang gnang sbyin gyi legs tshogs spyi sa nyid nas

mang ja dang / dngos po'i gnang sbyin mnga' 'bangs kyi chos sde so so la/ rgyal phran so so nas mang ja/ dngos po'i tshogs mtha' yas pa zhig dang / gzhan yang grong dpon so
so sogs grwa rigs rnams dang char gtogs pa thams cad kyi rten 'brel gyi dpal rgyun 'chad med par spel nas mnga' gsol gyi me tog char ltar du phab/ nged rang gis mang ja
dang lha rdzas kyi 'gyed bcas bcu phrag re la kha gru re dang bcas pa bsgrubs/ rje bla ma'i drung chen bzang po'i drung gis snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa rgyas pa'i ched yin
gsung rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi be bum bla ma'i phyag dpe yongs rdzogs gnang sbyin mang po byung / sang snga bar mchod yon tshang mar gsol 'debs phran bu bsgrubs/ sde pa nas
dkar spro'i gnang sbyin dang ngar ngad 'dzom pa'i rgya ja bzang po'i btung ba sogs dpal 'byor gyi rgyun 'phral dang yun gyi dge mtshan phul du phyin pa gnang / de nas rim
par phu'i dgon pa rje btsun bla ma'i zhabs khri dang po dge 'phel ri bo'i spo nyid la phyin/ ser sprengs sogs du ma legs tshogs kyi dpe mthar thug pa byung / mi mangs skya
ser kun la tshe rta'i dbang rjes gnang rgyas par byas skabs pha bla ma tshar pa chos rje'i tshe dbang 'dra mo byung zer mi kha yar byung / de nas mgyogs skor byas/ don
gcig pa bya lor rwa 'khrid/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ gur zhal phyi nang gi 'khrid sogs mdor na snyan brgyud kyi sbas don ma lus pa don gyi gdul bya mtha' yas pa'i re ba so sor
bskang / chos sde nyid kyi sgrub mchod sogs kun la shar sbyangs byas dus steng gtong dgos rnams kyang gong 'phel kho na

byas/ mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams sprin bzhin du 'du ba'i gnas ru mtshon gyi rten rnams cung zad rnyings pa'i skyon 'dug pa rnams la ji ltar 'os pa'i rten rnams rgya cher
gsar du spos nas gtsugs pas chos srung dam can tshogs kyang mnyes pa'i dge mtshan du ma snang / rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi dus mchod la pha rgyud kun gyi yang snying
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub mchod kyi rgyun btsugs pa'i cha rkyen du rgyu dngos gang yod de steng du spungs nas mchod pa'i rgyun mi nub par btsugs/ de nas don gnyis pa
khyi lo dge sbyor gang 'phel skabs gzhan phan gyi ban ling kho na'i dus zla ba dang po la rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rwa 'khrid nyid rgyas par 'chad skabs/ gdams pa 'di'i spyod
yul du ma gyur pa'i gang zag skal dman kha re 'dug pa la/ lam 'di'i bdag po snying nye la bka' nyan pa chos kyi rgyal po de nyid cung zad khros pa'i nyams kyis/ rang nyid
la bzlog pa'i rnam pas khams shin tu nyog pa kha bdar ba'i skyon gyis mgrin pa yang 'gags pa'i tshul gyis go skabs dog pa tsam byung bas grol ba rigs 'dra zhes pa'i nye
gtam byed mi mang po byung / de 'dra ma zer chos srung 'di ma mnyes pa'i rtags su 'dug /lar chos byed mkhan yin pa la shi na yang legs pa yin/ mi tshe chos la bskyal ba'i
don de ga yin mod byas/ 'tsho byed nyid kyis phul du ma phyin pa'i 'bras bu nad ngo de yang cher mi zin pa zhig 'dug pa dang / lhag par chos srung de dang lha mo nyid
kyis rmi lam du khyed rang 'o brgyal mgyogs par blo la yod pa'i 'tsho

byed 'bod pa zhu/ nged kyis 'phrin las ci nus sgrub zhes pa'i za zi la gnyid kyi rnam pa dwangs/ nged rang gi blo gtad bcol ba'i sman pa de nyid 'phral du spyan drangs pa'i
nus pa dang / mkha' 'gro chos srung gi byin rlabs kyis da bar gnas pa lags/ de dus kyang 'gro dgos pa'i ltas log pa byung yang bgegs de nyid dgyes pa'i 'byor pa thams cad
med par byas pas don thams cad de gas tshim song / chos de yang gegs med du grol chos srung rnams la bskang bshags kyi btang rag brgya tshar gyis mnyes par byas/ de nas
sgrub thabs brgya rtsa sgrol ma nyer gcig sogs kyi rjes gnang gis don gnyer thams cad so sor tshim par phul/ zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes brgyad la chos kyi rgyal po sku mched
kyis mthun rkyen phul du phyin pa'i mthun sbyor gnang / lhag par ayon bla ma'i bstan pa la 'jam dpal nyid ched du mi'i gzugs 'dzin pa khri srong lde'u btsan gyi brtul
zhugs 'dzin pa dgra 'dul drung gis sgrub pa chen po bka' brgyad kyi rtsa sgrub sogs rnying ma'i bstan pa gsal bar byed dgos zhes ched du bskul nas sgrub pa chen po'i steng
nas sman sgrub ril bu sil ma dang gong bu sogs yong gin 'dug kyang / gong bu'i sgrub pa zla ba lhag tsam bde gshegs bdun brgya nyi shu'i bsnyen pa dang lhan du bsgrubs
pas/ zhag bcu gnyis tsam song ba na dri bzang gis sgrub khang kun gang ba dang / dam rdzas kyi sman rag gtor gsum rnams kyang dri ro phun sum tshogs pa dang mar me'i rgyun
gcig gis nyin mtshan lnga tsam thub pa dang / gzhan yang zhag nyi shu song ba'i nyi ma snga phyed tsam la gnyid

kyi rnam pa yod tsam gyi rmi lam na nam mkha'i khyon thams cad la li khri'i mdog ltar byas pa'i dbus na bum pa gser btso ma ltar gsal zhing dwangs pa chen po zhig 'dug /de'i
dbus na padma sna tshogs kyi 'dab ma brgyad kyi 'dab ma re re na gu ru padma'i sku'i dbyibs thams cad padma rgyal po'i tshul ji ltar byas pa 'od sna tshogs lta bar mi bzod
pa zhig 'dug pa dang gnyid sad/ e ma ayon bla ma'i thugs rjes nam yang bslu ba mi 'dug snyam nyi ma shar ba ltar gyi dang ba shar/ ril bu rnams kyi 'phel rgyas cung zad
dang yid bzhin nor bu ltar rdzi la gang nas ltas kyang yid kyi re ba khengs pa zhig byung / de nas rgyal po'i gdung brgyud rnams dang / bka' 'bangs kyi don gnyer mang
po dang snyigs dus kyi sngags pa'i gzugs brnyan du ma dang bcas pa'i tshogs la rtsa ba'i dbang nyid rgyas par dbang tshar kha yar byas pas rgyal po'i dgongs bzhed ltar ayon
bla ma'i bstan pa ches cher rgyas par byas/ de nas lha lcam padma gsal gyi skyes mtha' padma bho Tas bum thang sku rjes brag nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma drag po'i gtor
bzlog byed dgos phebs/ dmigs yul de yang tshul ltos ru thag 'dzin pa la ched du bdos pa'i stod 'brog rnams la gtad/ bskul btsugs gtor ma cung zad phyir bsgyur bas gtor
snod nas rgyangs tsam thon dgra phyogs la rings par chas pa kun gyis mthong ba dang / 'phen pa'i skabs su slebs pa na rlung gi rgyu phyogs 'phral du 'gyur ba dang / zor rnams
lag nas 'phen 'gro ba tsam dang / gnam lcags kyi 'phang gtor de yang tsheg sgra dang bcas nas

song bas rtags mngon du gyur pa zhig byung ngo / des mtshon pa'i bzlog pa 'di nyid snga phyir lan kha re byas pas/ res 'ga' gtor ma sa la thim pa dang / res 'ga' zor skam rlon
la me med pa'i du ba 'phyur ba sogs byung mod/ thams cad ma spros/ gong sman sgrub skabs khams nas chos rgyal mtshan gyi ja gsigs sogs kyi skyel ma dang mi 'di la chos
mang po gnang dgos zer ba sleb/ mtshams 'di ma grol bar phrad mi thub pa 'dug /de nas gang yong byed byas pas/ yus kyis brgyal ba'i da lta dgos ja yang 'bul zer ba la da
lam yi dam dang ja brje bo mi yong byas/ phyis su blos ma long ba dang bcas byung bas chos phran bu ma gtogs rten 'brel ma 'grig song / de nas don gsum pa phag lo mtshams
me byas pa'i khong nas chos 'dod phran pa la chos sbyin ci nus dang / nyer gcig mchod kyi sgrub mchod dge rgyun la dmigs nas chos sde 'di nyid kyi mdun ngos su spyi khang
chen po zhig 'debs rtsis byas/ gong nas kyang dge ba'i rgyun la dgongs mthun rkyen legs lam phun sum tshogs pa gnang / der sdod kyi pho mo rnams la khral rigs kyi rgyun
spangs nas sbyor stod gnang yongs su rdzogs par mthar phyin/ zla ba bzhi pa'i nang du mtsho sgor khor tsam phyin/ phar lam dge 'phel du padma dbang chen gyi dbang nyid
rgyas par byas/ rwa 'khrid sogs chos kyi thugs bzhed ci nus sgrub/ mgyogs skor byas yongs/ lha rgod gangs kyi rwa ba'i nub kyi lcags mtsho sngon mo'i 'gram du phan tshun
gyi mi dbang zhal ngo rnams kyi skyel bsu 'dzom pa dang lus sems dub pa rnams

cung zad ngal gsos/ de nas phu pa skya ser rnams kyis bsu ba bzabs sprod dang bcas dge 'phel du bsdad/ chu tshan la khor ba phyin rim pas gdan sa chen por sleb/ yar klungs
bkra shis rtse nas rje btsun bla ma tshar pa rje'i zhal snga nas kyi gsung las skyes pa'i mkhan chen yol pa de nyid chos dbyings su gzims pa'i gnas tshul dang / gser gdung
drung du mar me rgyun spar dang / lha rdzas kyi brnyan dar mchod rdzas kyi gsung snyan sogs dang / dge 'dun tshogs par nag rtse bden ja'i mang ja zung dang 'gyed chas/
'dir yang bsngo ba'i rten dpag med dang bcas mkhan nyid kyi gsung las byon pa'i bshes gnyen bcu phrag tsam dang bcas 'byor byung bas gsol 'debs bsngo ba'i smon pa rgya cher
bsgrubs/ khong rnams la dpal kha'u brag rdzong ba'i snyan brgyud kyi bdud rtsi 'dod pa'i re ba mthar phyin par byas/ dam tshig pa'i bu la gdams pa'i ye shes kyi rgyas
btab ste bstan pa phyogs mthar rgyas par byas/ yar klung chos sde nyid na dam pa des gnang ba'i chos skyong rnams kyi sku brnyan sogs kyi bar chad bsrung ba'i ched du bla
ma'i thugs dam ye shes kyi rdo rje dgos zer ba ltar bstan pa bsams nas thugs bzhin bsgrubs ngos la yang rje bla ma dang de'i bstan pa bsam yong dgos gsungs kyang / na so
smin pa dang sa khad 'gyangs pa la brten phan thogs yong ba dka'/ de bas bstan pa'i nyi ma ayon gnyis pa'i dbon drung mkhyen rab gdul bya'i mkha' la byin rlabs kyi 'od zer
'bum phrag 'gyed par nus pa'i sngags 'chang dbang phyug

rab brtan spyan 'dren par 'os so zhes pa phul/ de ltar dngas len mdzad song bas de phyogs kyi re 'dod thams cad 'grub par go bas blo bde/ de nas don bzhi pa byi lo dge sbyor
dang chos 'chad ci nus skabs nas rtse sogs kher ma byas bsdad/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa de 'dzin gyi skyes chen rnams la lhag bsam gyi thugs mdun gzhal du med pa/ gzur gnas
kyi mkhas pa thams cad dga' ba bskyed par nus pa'i dpa' bo/ rnam dpyod kyi mkhyen rab nam mkha'i khyon ltar yangs pa/ mthu stobs kyi 'gran la sngon rabs kyi rgyal brgyud
bskyangs par mdzad pa'i chos skyong ba'i rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan gyi rnam par 'phrul pa dgra 'dul drung gis ched du bskul/ bang mdzod thams cad kha phye nas kun tu
bzang po'i mchod sprin ltar phyogs gcig tu mdzad/ mkha' mnyam 'gro ba'i don du thar pa'i rgyur 'gro ba'i bag chags kyi sa bon bzang po 'debs pa'i skye ba bdun pa'i sha
la brten pa'i ril bu sgrub pa'i sgrub pa zhig gnang dgos phebs/ de ltar ci gsung dang len byas/ rten de'i steng du rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung / shA ri'i bu sogs
nyan thos rnams kyi gdung / ayon bla ma'i byang sems kunda dkar po/ /mkha' 'gro 'bum gyi gtso mo ye shes 'tsho rgyal gyi pad rag /chos rgyal gsung gi skye ba chos dbang
gi sku sha /sna nam pa'i skyes mtha' rgod ldem pa'i sku sha /lho byang gi gter kha so so'i chos sman phye ma/ rgya gar gyi lo paN so so'i gdung shangs mtshal dbu lo na
bza' sogs dang / rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud gong ma rnams kyi gdung shangs mtshal dbu lo na bza'/ rje btsun

sa paN gyi 'phel gdung / theg chen rin po che'i sku sha /gong ma so so'i bdud rtsi ril bu/ rje btsun kun dga' bzang po'i dbu lo sogs dang / grub thob chen po'i dbu lo na bza'/
tshe sgrub ril bu sogs mdor na rgya bod kyi skyes chen tshad mas grub pa thams cad kyi byin rlabs/ rtsa ba dang brgyud pa'i skyes bu mtshan nyid tshang ba kun gyi byin
rlabs yid ches rnyed pa rnams kyis gzhi byas/ de dag la brten pa'i rgyu rin po che sna tshogs tshad/ sman rin po che tshogs tshad/ 'bru rin po che tshogs tshad / de sogs
ji ltar dgos pa'i yo byad sgrub khog gzhung nas bshad pa ltar ma tshang ba med par byas/ mtshan nyid de ldan gyi ril bu sgril ba rnams kyang gzhung dang mthun par mi dbang
nyid kyis sta gon gnang / dus la babs pa'i tshe zla ba drug pa'i nyer lnga la phun sum tshogs pa kun tshang ba'i gnas kyi gtsug lag khang chen por 'phags pa thugs rje
chen po'i las gzhung gi steng nas sgrub cing tshes bcu'i mchod pa rgyas par bsgrubs/ gzungs thag 'dzin pa'i sgrub po bcu gcig /'phrin las gyer ba'i sgrub po bcu phrag gsum
tsam dang / gzhan yang gzungs rgyun mi 'chad par sgrog pa'i skye bo brgya phrag dang bcas sgrub pa zhag gsum song ba'i snga thun gyi thog mar brgyud pa rin po che la rtse
gcig tu gsol ba phur btsugs su btab pas/ po ta la sogs sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams rnams na bzhugs pa'i dkar phyogs kyi lha rnams dgyes pa'i me tog gi char nyi ma sbrel
nas 'bab pa dang / zhag bzhi song ba'i dgongs thun gyi 'dzab kyi skabs su nged rang mchod yon kun

dkyil 'khor khang pa la skor ba byed pa'i grogs mdzad de/ 'phags pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bka' nyan lhag bdud kyi pho nya/ lha chen/ klu chen/ gza' chen/ rgyal chen/ ha ri ka /paN
tsi ka sogs kyi srung ma thams cad dang / gtsug lag khang gi gnas bdag gnyug mar gnas pa'i dam can mgar ba nag po/ /bdud mo tha chung re ma ti sogs dkar phyogs skyong
ba thams cad yol ba gsum rim gyis nang na skor ba dang gzungs rgyun cher sgrog pa'i nyams 'ur lang la khad pa byung / zhag lnga song ba'i snga thun gyi bar la gnyid kyi
rnam pa thung tsam byung ba'i rmi lam na rje btsun sprul sku chen po padma rgyal po'i sku nyid myug rgyal khang du skye bdun sgrub pa'i skabs kyi sku'i mdangs ji lta ba dang
/ g.yas na 'khrul zhig chos skyong bsod nams yin zer ba'i sku gzi brjid che ba zhig dang / g.yon na tshar chen yab sras dang bcas dgyes pa'i zhal 'dzum gyi mdangs yal
ba byas pa zhig rmi/ gnyid dwangs pa na e ma ho nga yang bsod nams che de lta bu'i bslu med kyi bla ma rnams dang mjal snyam pa dang / da snying po bdag dang bdag la ltos
pa thams cad ayon bla ma'i drung du skye nges kyi smon pa yid ches nges shig btab/ de nas bzung dri bzang gi ngad pa 'thul bzhin pa dang bcas 'phrin las kyi mchod pa brgyad
brgya kha 'thor tsam song / de yang bstan pa dang de 'dzin gyi skyes chen thams cad yun du gnas pa dang / 'phrin las 'gag med du dar ba la dmigs nas sum brgya/ sbyin
po nyid dang gdung rabs kyi mnga' thang thams cad gong 'phel du rgyas pa dang / rkyen gyi bdud rigs thams cad

dpa' gzhom pa la dmigs nas nyis brgya 'thor ba/ sgrub po bdag sogs mtha' yas pa'i sems can thams cad kyi sgrib gnyis bag chags ngan pa sbyangs te 'khor ba rgyun gcod pa la
dmigs nas sum brgya dang bcas pa bsgrubs/ de bar la bza' ba dang btung ba'i bye brag gnang ba po ni nam mkha'i mdzod la longs spyod pa ltar nyin mtshan khor yug tu byung
/ de sbyor ba po thams cad po ta la sogs phyir mi zlog pa'i zhing du skye nges kyi nges 'drongs byung ba yin/ 'phags pa'i g.yon gyi 'og ma'i padma la de kun gnas pa 'dug
pas 'khor ba'i skyon gyis ma gos par go /dkyil 'khor de nyid du rtsa ba'i dbang dang / des smin pa'i skal ba bzang po'i rgyal 'bangs ji snyed la sgrub dbang shin tu rgyas
pa ril bu'i dbang dang bcas pa bsgrubs/ ril bu la 'phel rgyas sgrub gzhung gi thog ma byung ba dang / mthong bas yid 'phrog pa dri bzang gis gzhung stod du ma khengs pa
dang / des mtshon pa'i dge mtshan dpag par dka' ba dang / 'di nyid myong bas grol ba'i rtags mtshan du ma dang / ring bsrel gyi tshogs kyang mthong bas grol ba yod do/ /de
nas zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nang du dbon rin po che khor pa phebs byung bas thugs bzhed kyi don ma lus par blo nus kyi rig pa rtsal dang bcas pas bsgrubs/ 'di tshor rten 'brel
bsgrig pa yin pas sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi gtso bo kun rig rnam snang gi dbang ji ltar 'os pa'i gdul bya 'di rnams la stsal ba dgos zhus pa ltar bka' drin bskyangs/
de nas nged rang shul du bor shar phyogs la thegs song bsam pa'i re ba 'di'i phyogs nas

ma rdzogs pa zhig yod do/ /de nas don lnga pa glang gi lo dge sbyor nyin mtshan dal med byed skabs bsam pa'i blo la 'khu 'khrig 'di ltar shar/ sngar nas chos bshad pa thams
cad kyi bstan pa la phan thogs yod pa dum pa tsam las mi 'dug /bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bur nges pa kun kyang dpon po'i ngo gang zin dang 'du 'dzi su che gtso bor 'don/ de
la brten sems can gyi bde skyid rnams kyang je lod 'gro bar 'dug /ri la gnas pa'i sgom chen pa rnams kyang 'ga' zhig ni 'tsho bas 'phongs 'ga' zhig ni ri khrod mi 'dzin par
grong yul khyi ltar bskor/ 'ga' zhig ni g.yo rgyu dang zog gi 'khor lo rgyun mar bskor nas sems can mang po bslu/ e ma bla ma yab sras rnams ni ma bzhugs/ 'di 'dra'i dus
ngan zhig snyam lus sems ngal zhing sgyid lug la yi mug pa zhig byung / 'on kyang sngon gyi dam pa rnams kyis 'gro ba'i bde skyid la dgongs/ yul dang yul gru thams cad
du gtsug lag khang mchod pa'i rten dang bcas pa bzhengs 'dug nga rang la yang pha bla ma rdo rje 'chang blo gsal rgya mtsho'i bstan pa 'di la dar rgyas shig kyang e yong
snyam pa dang yul phyogs 'dis gtso byas yangs pa'i rgyal khams su 'gro ba'i bde skyid la phan la re ba'i lhag bsam skyes nas/ gtsug lag khang rten dang bcas pa'i phyogs
su lus dang longs spyod thams cad spungs nas bzhengs pa ni zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gnyis la rgyal phur dang bstun rmang 'ding ba nas bkra shis mnga' gsol man chad zla ba phyed
lnga'i khongs su yongs su rdzogs par grub pa sogs rgyas par 'og tu bkod/ de skabs mi ngan kha re dang phrad pas lan

pa yin nam/ zhabs drung mkhyen brtse'i drung cung zad ma mnyes pa'i rtags mang po byung / ma babs ro zas 'di dang ma bral bas yin pa 'dug /gang ltar lus srog bdog pa thams
cad dang / phyi nang ma lus pa bran du phul nas ci mdzad legs nyes thams cad khyed rang shes snyam thugs rje la re ba 'di yin no/ /zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes bcu'i snga
dro gnyid kyi rnam pa thungs pa byung ba'i rmi lam na ayon bla ma da lta bris yod pa 'di lta bu'i sku'i cha lugs byas pa bar snang 'ja' tshon gyi rnam pa khra shig ge ba'i
khrod nas mi tshad gsum 'gyur tsam byas pa zhig gi mdun na/ rje bla ma mkhyen brtse nyid sngon gyi sku'i tshul la pad zhwa phod ka bzhes pa zhig 'dug pa'i zhal nas/ mchod
pa'i dge tshogs dpag med mchis na yang / ayon rje la 'dud pa'i mchod pa de/ /ji srid mchog la ma reg bar dag tu/ /gus pas dngas len rab tu 'bad pa gces/ /gsung ba lhang
lhang byung ba dang gnyid sad/ sngar nas kyang grogs kyi ram bu 'degs pa ni med kyang / rang gis ji ltar nus pa gsol ba btab pa'i 'bras bu 'dug /da dung grogs dam tshig
pa phran bu byung na lus ngag yid gsum rtse gcig tu gsol ba 'debs pa dang / lhag par tshes bcu'i mchod pa ma chag pa rgyas par byed pa'i zhe bcad byas/ de nas stag lo don
drug pa la rten bzhengs kyi mjug bsdus zla ba bdun pa'i dus mchod rgyas par byas rjes zla skor rtser bsdad/ bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu gnyis la lha chen nag po zhal bzhi'i
gsang 'khrid lus pa med par phul/ de nas dgon gsar chos rje ngag gi dbang

phyug sogs la dpal gur gyi mgon po'i dbang rnams yongs su rdzogs pa phul rjes ci bder gnas/ don bdun pa yos bu la lus ngag gi tshe 'di'i spyod pa thams cad rgyang rings spangs
nas ci nus su byang chub sgrub pa la rtse gcig tu gzhol/ de skabs rnam dpyod kyi blo gros gzhal du med pa stag na nas chos kyi rje kun dga' blo gros bzang po la gcig
brgyud du gsung ngag rin po che yongs rdzogs phul/ mdor na dmigs pa med pa'i sems can rnams kyi don du/ bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha tshogs la khor yug tu dal med gsol ba 'debs
pa la brtson pa 'di lags so/ /bzhi pa sgo gsum gyi las don yod par bya ba'i phyir rtag tu bsam gtan gyi kha ton 'chag med byed tshul la/ skyabs bslu med gcig chog rgyal
po mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi mtshan spel yod pa mtshan bstod shlo ka gnyis brgya rtse ra/ rnam thar bstod thung shlo ka bcu gcig yod pa nyer gcig re/ dran pas srid
zhi'i rgud pa sel ba blo gsal rgya mtsho'i mtshan bstod shlo ka gcig brgya rtsa re/ kye rdo rje'i bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis rtsa sngags brgya phrag lnga re dang / nA ro mkha'
spyod kyi bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis yi ge so gnyis stong phrag re/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis rtsa sngags brgya phrag re dang / snying po nye snying
stong phrag re/ rdo rje nag po chen po'i bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis bod pa stong phrag re/ rbod rbad bsad gsum dril ba'i shA sa na brgya phrag re/ bla ma drag po dmar po
dbu dgu pa'i bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis drag sngags yig 'bru zhe bdun pa khri tsho gnyis re/ drag po mthing kha'i bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis

yang snying 'bru gcig khri tsho re/ 'phags pa thugs rje chen po'i bskyed rdzogs thun gnyis yang snying 'bru drug stong phrag re/ phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po'i bskyed
rdzogs/ dpal mgon ma ning gi bskyed rdzogs/ lha chen nag po zhal bzhi'i bskyed rdzogs/ rje btsun yid bzhin 'khor lo'i bskyed rdzogs/ tshe dpag med kun gyi yang snying lcags
sdong ma'i nyams len rta mchog rol pa gsang sgrub kyi bskyed rdzogs/ las kyi gshin rje gshed rang gi bran po chos kyi rgyal po'i bskyed rdzogs/ de rnams thun re re gsang
sngags rnams kyang brgya phrag la nyung mtha' byas pa re/ gzhan yang yi dam chos skyong rnams kyi dbang thob gsang sngags bdun bdun zla ba mang po yod/ thob tshad kyi
gsang sngags bzlas pa ma byung mod/ de kun gyi nyams chags gso ba la dmigs yi ge brgya ba brgya phrag re/ yi dam chos srung de rnams kyi gtor bsngo rgyas pa tshar re sogs
nyog la mang ba mtha' yas bdog ste thams cad ma spros/ drag po bla ma dang legs nyes kun lung ston pa'i 'dod khams lha mo re ma ti dang / bran po las kyi gshin rje rnams
kyi thugs dam bskang ba dang bshags pa rnams dus dang khyad par ba brgya rtsa re dang bcas pa song zhing / mdor na chos ldan gyi bya bas g.yengs na ma gtogs spyod lam drug
po'i gnas skabs ci byed dal bar skad cig kyang sdod ma myong / de snga yan la 'chag med khri tsho gnyis 'dren pa rnams dung bzhi la nye ba dang / khri tsho re 'dren pa
rnams dung gnyis la nye ba dang / stong phrag 'dren pa rnams bye ba gnyis re lhag thor song ba dang /

gzhan yang snying po nye snying rtsa sngags dang 'khor gyi lha sogs kyi gsang sngags sa ya dang / 'bum tsho dang / khri tsho stong tsho la mtha' ma byas pa mang po yod mod/
thams cad 'dri bar ma ldang / sgrub cing mchod pa dang / 'jug cing dbang blang ba dang / skabs su ci babs kyi las bzhi so so'i sbyin sreg rnams stong tsho drug nas brgya
phrag bdun tshun la nyung mtha' byas pa song 'dug kyang / sems gzhan g.yeng bas byas pas 'bras bu ma mchis so/ /'khrul pa spangs pa'i rgyud ldan gangs ri las/ /legs bshad
snyan brgyud bdud rtsi rnyog bral bas/ /nyams myong bde ba chen po'i bcud kyis myos/ /skyon med 'bras bu ye shes mngon du gyur/ /bslu med 'khrul zad yab sras sa skya pa'i/
/zhal 'od bskyed rdzogs drod ldan sgom pa po/ /zol zog dri mas dben pa'i ku sA li/ /rnam gsum 'dren pas skyong ba'i sngags smyon mkhan/ /blun po bsod nams chos 'phel
e ma ho/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi rdzu 'phrul gcig bsdus pa/ /bod khams ma rung 'phung byed 'dul ba'i gtso/ /padma ka ra zhal bcud 'thung ba bo/ /'dre 'jigs ro nyal mkhan po
'bru pa nga / /gzugs can mi rnams ya ga sgrog pa'i gnas/ /ltos bcas tshogs rnams don ldan nyams dgar mdzod/ /mkhas kun dga' ba'i glu dbyangs 'tsher bas gzur gnas snying la
bde ba ster/ /brtson 'grus ldan pa'i rkang drug tshogs rnams theg rim lam la myur du 'god/ /bzang 'dod grags smon med kyang rgyang na gnas pa'i pad tshal lo/ /lnga pa 'gro
ba lha mir bcas pa'i phyag dang mchod pa'i smon lam gyi

rten du gyur pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs tshul la rnam grangs du mar 'dug ste nyung ngu'i tshul gyis brjod na/ bo dong byang chub chen po'i mchod rten rmang 'ding
ba nas rab gnas ma grub bar gyi bkod pa byas nas/ srog shing rgyud sde nas ji skad byon pa'i gzungs kyi rim pas ma tshang ba med pa theg rim gyi bzhugs tshul dang / drag
dmar/ thugs sgrub/ bka' brgyad/ bde kye/ 'jigs byed/ tshe dpag med/ nor rgyun ma/ rgyal chen bzhi rnams kyi gzungs 'bum phrag re lhag pa dang / gzhan yang rgyud sde bzhi
dang 'brel ba'i lha tshogs rnams kyi gzungs du ma dang bcas pa dang / drag dmar gyi gzungs dang ye dhar 'ba' zhig bzhugs pa'i tsha tsha'i tshogs du ma dang bcas pas yongs
su gtams pa'i chos sku'i mchod rten/ longs sprul gyi sku brnyan dang bcas pa'i grangs las 'das pa zhig bzhugs shing mdor na ding sang gi sa rdo gar blugs kyi bzhengs blo
tsho dang cung mi 'dra ba zhig yod/ gzungs chen sde lnga'i par sogs du ma zhig bzhengs da lta bo dong dbu rtse na bzhugs/ gsol 'debs kyi rten du bla chen rnam gnyis kyi
bris sku la gsung ngag brgyud pa dang 'jigs byed brgyud pas bskor ba chos skyong sogs 'dod lha'i tshogs dang / 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i sku rmi lam du byung ba la 'dod lha
rnams kyis bskor ba/ de nyid kyi mtshar sku la drin che ba'i bla ma 'dod lha dang bcas pas bskor ba'i bris sku/ thugs rje chen po'i sku brnyan brgya rtsa/ sbrul lo lha sa
rdzong du kye rdor/ gur lcam dral/ bla ma'i sku/ dud sol lha mo/ zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi sku brnyan dang bcas pa mus nas dpal chen drung gis bzheng ba gnang / thog mar
bdag la cang mi gsung bar mkhyen rab kyi sgo nas bzhengs kyang / byings rnams la skya bris thengs

tsam byas/ zhal khra yongs rdzogs de nyid la skya bris brtsams pa na bar chad kyi rnam pa rlung la rten de lha bris pa rnams la zhugs nas/ zhi drag gi thabs ci byas kyang phan
pa zhig ma byung 'dug /mthar ri mo ba tsho sems dran pas mi zin par spyod pa sna tshogs byed pa zhig 'dug pas/ bdag la byin rlabs dang bgegs skrod dang zhal gyi rjes
gnang thun mong ma yin pa zhu zer/ de ltar mi nus thun mong ba tsam byas chog lar 'di lta bu'i sku brnyan bzhengs pa ni dal 'byor gyi dper mtshon par gda'/ da lam dngas phyin
skyon mi mnga' byas/ rjes gnang gi ye shes babs pa na ri mo ba la ye shes dngos su phebs nas tsha ba tsam lus g.yo 'gul med par gnas pa byung / de nas gzungs rten rnams
gegs med du phyin/ rab gnas kyang bdag nyid kyis byas da lta ni sbyin po de'i lag na yod mod/ de 'dra'i 'tshub lta bu yin nam de lo lha sa rdzong ni thang mar btang nas
bar chad kyi gtso bo dbon zhes pa dga' ba'i glu blangs so/ /de skor mang po yod kyang ma spros/ gzhan yang 'dar stod grang mo che'i chos gra zhes/ chos 'khor yang rtse'i
gtsug lag khang gi gnas su/ glang gi lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes gnyis la rgyal phur dang bstun gtsug lag khang gi rmang bting / zla ba brgyad pa'i mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus
nyer dgu la phyag tshad ldan pa'i bzo bo byin gyis brlabs te 'go btsugs/ de yang rgyu rin po che gang las bzhengs snyam na/ 'jim pa la rtsi tshon gyis byugs nas mdzes
mdzes lta bur byas pas sa rdo'i gong bu la rgyan du che bar byas pa ma yin/ gang zhe na gser g.yus

gtsos pa'i rin po che'i tshogs mtha' yas pa/ ga bur gyis gtsos pa'i sman tshogs tshang / tsan dan la sogs pa'i dri bzang dpag med/ a ru ra la sogs pa'i shing 'bras duu ma/
spang rgyan la sogs pa'i me tog sna tshogs nas gro la sogs pa'i 'bru tshogs grangs med/ bsam yas kyis gtsos pa'i mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi gnas na bzhugs pa'i rten rnams kyi
rdul/ skyi rong gi 'phags pas gtsos pa'i 'byung ba kha gnon la bzhugs pa'i jo bo rnams kyi rten dang shing kun gyis gtsos pa'i bal yul na bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag rnams kyi
rten dang / dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang gi bse 'bag gis gtsos pa'i rten grangs dpag med rnams dang / kha'u brag rdzong sogs me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi'i
gnas na bzhugs pa'i srung ma rnams kyi/ e waM chos ldan la sogs pa'i bod yul gyi mdo sngags so so'i chos grwa'i gtsug lag na bzhugs pa'i rten dang / mnga' ris rdzong dkar
la sogs pa'i rgyal po'i pho brang thams cad na bzhugs pa'i rten sogs de thams cad kyi zhabs rdul gtsug lag de rnams dang / gnas brgyad kyi mchod rten gyi sa sna/ bkra shis
pa'i lung pa mang po'i sa sna dang chu sna/ ri bkra legs pa pho gsum mo gsum gyi sa sna sogs dang / ka shi ka'i ras sogs dang / kha dog sna tshogs pa'i lha rdzas kyi dar
bzang mang po dang / de rnams tshogs gcig tu byas shing 'jim pa cung zad dang bcas pa'i phung po la rab gnas mtshan nyid tshang ba byas/ de yang brgyud pa thun mong ma
yin pa 'di pa'i bgros la/ chos skyong gi sku

brnyan bris 'bur ci bzhengs kyang thog mar gzungs kyi bya ba yongs su rdzogs par byas nas/ thun mong gi sku dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sku rnams yod pa las/ phyi ma 'bad pas
sgrub pa la/ de yang dregs pa pho rgyud kyi ngo bo gri snying 'khor lo/ dregs pa mo rgyud kyi ngo bo nal bu'i gri snying 'khor lo/ gnyis med kyi ngo bo ye shes kyi rdo
rje gzugs dang bcas pa/ theg pa che chung gi bla ma brgyud pa dang / rgyud sde phyi nang gi bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan rim 'dod gsol dang bcas pa brgya phrag gnyis re dang
/ rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i yi dam chos skyong nor lha bstan srung dang bcas pa'i mchog thun sgrub pa'i lha rnams kyi gsang sngags brgya phrag gsum re dang bcas pa
ru shing so so la theg rim gyi dkri tshul so sor byas te lha rdzas dpag med kyi na bza' dang bcas pa bzhugs yod la/ de ltar chos skyong gi sku brnyan de yang bzhengs pa'i
dus/ phyi nang gsang ba'i rten 'brel ma lus par tshang dgos pa yin te/ de lo glang lo zla ba dpyid zla ra ba/ tshes nyer dgu/ gza' mig dmar skar ma mgo /skyes pa stag lo
pa grir shi ba'i snying khrag sar ma lhung ba/ de nyid kyi gri rkang / mgon po 'di nyid la bsnyen sgrub las gsum gyi sgo nas mtshan ma thob nges kyi bla ma dam pa'i srin
lag gi khrag dang / shangs mtshal/ skyes pho mo lo bcu gnyis 'gro ba'i rang byung gi khams dkar dmar dang bcas pa 'di rnams 'dzom na nged rang dpal ldan sa skya pa'i snyan
brgyud 'dzin pa rnams kyi bzhed pas ye shes pa dngos su zhugs pa yin pas/ zla ba tsam ma 'grig mod/ gzhan

yang tshang ma rang 'grig tu byung nas/ phyag tshad ldan pa'i bzo bos rdo rje dang padma'i lag pas dus de nyid la 'go btsugs/ de la yang phyi nang gi nye ring kun bar chad
yong zer mda' skur mang dag 'dug kyang / khyed de ltar bsam pa'i don rnams la kha thal bas bcad do byas/ don la sngon du bla ma chos skyong dang bcas pas mtshan ma bzang
po byung ba dang nye bar gnas pas grogs bgyis te rkang blangs/ blos 'char tshul mi dbang rnams la'ang zhe nas phul/ dgongs par ji ltar bzhugs pa'i zhal bkod da lta gnang
ba skabs su babs/ phyis su de dang de 'dra byung na bzod par gsol byas/ gang ltar bar chad mi 'byung ba'i 'phrin bcol gyi mchod gtor bzang po phul/ nam zla cung zad dgun
la sbyar ba nas rdul gyi nyes pa las skyob pa'i 'phrin las rlung lha sha gzugs 'od kyi rnam pas ma grub par la mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang gnas srung dkar phyogs skyong ba
rnams dang / rgyal chen bzhi sogs kyis rtse gcig tu sgrub pa'i grogs kyi 'phrin las yang dag byas/ de rnams la mchod gtor bzang po yang yang du phul dus dang rgyun gyi sa
lam bar chad srung ba'i gsol ba drag tu btab ste/ dam tshig gi sku brnyan mkha' 'gro lha brgyad/ gnya' mnan pa'i phyir 'byung po 'dul byed/ rigs bdag cod pan 'bral ba med
pa'i phyir phrag dpung g.yas g.yon du rje btsun rdo rje 'chang rnam pa gnyis kyi sku brnyan/ phyi nang gi las mgon gsum dang bcas pa/ bram ze'i gzugs 'dzin zhing skyong
chen po yum bzhir bcas pa'i sku brnyan/ de

nyid kyi gsang ba'i las mgon shu tra nag po'am sangs rgyas kyi gcung por grags pa/ dpal padma dbang chen yang gsang khros pa'i thugs kyi sprul pa dbang gi skyes bu bshan pa
nyer gcig gi gtso 'khor gsum gyi sku brnyan/ spyir 'dzam gling bod yul gyi gnas bdag /ayon bla ma'i bsha' sgrub/ sgos rje btsun tshar pa rje'i dam chos phyi nang gi ltos
pa thams cad bang mdzod kyi gnyer kha'o/ /nged rang la gnas 'di nyid rtsis sprod dang yul byes kun tu chos dang thun mong gi dpal 'byor rgyas par spel ba'i 'phrin las mdzad
pa po gnas kyi dkor srung dam can mgar ba nag po nyid dang / 'dzam gling kha ba can gyi yul bdag bstan srung bstan ma bcu gnyis kyi bdud mo bzhi'i tha chung khyung lung
re ma ti dang bcas pa'i srung ma rnams kyi sku brnyan dang / de'i steng du pha rgyud kun gyi yang snying rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa 'khrid mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi brgyud
pa rin po che yongs rdzogs dang / gdan sa chen po 'di nyid kyi mkhan rabs kyi sku brnyan dang bcas pa bzhugs yod cing / de rnams kyi steng du gos dar zhe gcig pa'i bla
bre na bza' snyan dar dbu snyel bzhugs gdan dang / steng du snyan brgyud zhal shes las 'ongs pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i ru mtshon rtse lnga pa dang bcas pa tshun legs par
bsgrubs so/ /de yang rten gtso'i sku brnyan 'di bzhugs tshul chos kyi dbyings la 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir chos skyong 'di nyid bris 'bur gang bzhengs kyang g.yon du 'gying
ba dang bcas pa yod bzhin 'dug pa ltar bzhengs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi phyag nas dngos bzhugs

bod du bse 'bag tu byas pa'i sku 'bag nyid g.yas 'gying du yod pa/ zhal gnam sa lta bu gdangs pa yod pa ltar du rang grub tu byung ba ni bzo bo'i rig byed sogs der gnas pa
kun gyis mthong ba de yin/ da lta'i bar du yang cung zad g.yas la 'gying ba dang bcas pa yod do/ /de la yang rab gnas rgyas par sgrub pa'i ston mo sde pa che sa nas dgra
'dul drung gis bka' drin bskyangs/ rim pas mtshon rdzogs kyi mthar sku gsum gyi spyan 'byed par brtsams zla ba dgu pa'i tshes lnga la rgyal phur gyi 'phrod dang bstun/ tshogs
kyi ston mo bzang po dang bcas mtshon gyis dbye bar brtsams pa na/ rnam snang mtsho'i thugs ka'i bde ba chen po'i ye shes kyi spyan de nyid dngos su sems can gyi don
du sku brnyan 'di nyid kyi spyan gsum la bkra lam shar ba nas mtshan ma rdzas kyi mtshon dang lha bzo ba la ltos pa med par kun gyi mig sngar 'byor ba dang bcas pa yod cing
/ de lta bu'i sku brnyan spyan 'dren par brtsams nged rang gi yi dam lha'i bskyed rim brtan po spos kyi dri bzang phyogs kun khyab pa dang bcas g.yabs pa na/ gnyug mar
gnas pa'i skor srung rnams dang rgyal chen bzhi/ phyogs skyong bcu sogs kyi rnam 'phrul 'od gzugs kyi rnam pas spyan 'dren pa'i gsal snang chen po byung / de ltar rten
gyi bya ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs nas gong du brjod pa ltar gzungs bzhugs kyi steng du sku brnyan re re la sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung re re dang / gser zangs las grub
pa'i gnod sbyin 'khor lo tshul bzhin bsgrubs pa re re dang bcas pa

bzhugs yod la/ mthar rab tu gnas par sleb pa na/ gong nas mi dbang rnams nor bu'i 'phreng ba la sogs pas brgyan pa dang / zab ber la sogs pa'i rgyal po'i chas thams cad kyis
brgyan nas bdag nyid bsu ba dang bcas ji ltar rab tu gnas bya'i khang par sleb/ 'og tu rab gnas khyad par ba kun dang thun mong ma yin pa zhag bdun du byas pa'i ye shes
bstim pa/ rje ngag gi dbang phyug gis mdzad pa dang / rgyud dang rgya gzhung nas gsungs pa ltar la zhal shes kyis brgyan nas zhag gsum du byas pa'i mnga' gsol rgyas par
stag lo zla ba drug pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dus tshes bco lnga la grub pa dang / 'di nyid kyi 'gram 'ding ba nas rab gnas kyi mnga' gsol tshun la zla ba bzhi dang zhag nyi shu'i
khongs su gegs med du yongs su rdzogs par mthar phyin te/ bkra shis dang dge legs kyi rol pas dus kun 'tsho ba 'di lags/ gzhan yang lha khang 'dir sangs rgyas byang
sems kyi li ma dang / zangs sku ji snyed dang / lag na ci yod kyi mchod rdzas thams cad dang / gong nas mi'i dbang phyug rnams kyi 'byor pa'i dngos kun ma lus pa zhum pa
med par lan cig min par 'bul ba dang bcas lhan cig tu mchod sprin rgya mtsho lta bur dmigs nas phul ba dang / 'bangs thams cad kyi phyogs phyogs nas ji ltar nus pas bkur
bas nam mkha' mdzod la 'gran bdo ba tsam byung / rang nyid kyi tshe 'di'i phun tshogs thams cad kyang zhing mchog dam pa dge 'dun gyi sde dang / bzo ba'i rig pa 'chang ba
nyer gnyis dang bcas pa la rnam thos kyi bu'i 'byor pa ltar 'phongs pa med pa ltar lan gnyis

su phul ba dang / rab ston gyi dpal 'byor ni lha 'dre mi gsum mthong bas tshim pa dang bdud rtsi'i rgyun ni ganggA'i rlabs ltar chal chil du longs spyod cing / so so nas glu
dbyangs gar sogs kyi rdzogs ldan ltar byas pa byung / srung ma'i dbang po de dag gi drung gi dam rdzas mchod pa zag med ye shes kyi bdud rtsi ro brgya ldan pa ri bo la
'gran pa tsam btsugs nas dus dang rgyun gyi mchod pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du yod pa dang / de ltar sku gsung thugs phyi nang gsang ba ste drug ldan rten gzhan yang mi lpags
kyi g.yang gzhi dang / gos nag gi 'phan dang / steng du gsang ba'i rnga thug sogs dpag med cig bzhugs yod do/ /rdo rje 'jigs byed la med du mi rung ba'i snyan brgyud zhal
shes kyis brgyan nas dbang chog /gtor bzlog /sbyin sreg dang bcas pa/ sgrol dkar gyi rgyun gyi nyams len/ bsngo ba'i yi ge chung ngu / gsar rnying gi bla ma brgyud rim
kha yar gyi mtshan sngags/ de mtshungs yid dam chos skyong kha yar gyi gzugs sngags rnams kyi par dang / gzhan yang chu chen por zam pa dang / lam 'dus che sar mgron khang
dang / 'jigs pa'i gangs srag tu 'jigs skyob dang / phu chus cung zad 'phong sa'i lung par rdzing bu 'bru ba dang / lam 'phreng gi g.yang sa 'chos pa sogs mdor na sems
can gyi bde skyid mi nyams shing gong 'phel gyi thabs la skad cig kyang g.yel ba med par byas kyang / dus kyis mkhyogs bas lan pa yin nam tig tig mi gda'/ gang ltar lus
srog 'byor pa thams cad da dung rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang

'gro ba'i don du 'phongs pa med par byed pa 'di yin zhing / rang nyid zhi ba don gnyer gyi blo ni nam mkha'i padmo ltar mtshungs so/ /drug pa mgon med srid mtshor 'khyams pa'i
nyam thag gi 'gro ba mtha' yas pa'i don rtse gcig tu byas tshul la/ 'gro drug gtso bo mi lus dang / skam rlon gyi rten la gnas pa'i sems can gyi don byas tshul sogs las/
bo dong dang lha sa rdzong du snying rje'i gnas su gyur pa'i sde phan tshun 'khon bzhi thams cad zhi ba'i tshul gyis 'jam la blangs te byams pa la gnas par byas/ so so
nas blo'i re ba phul du phyin pa byas btang snyoms kyi yul du gyur pas 'khrug gzhi bral rang dgar spyod pa'i bde ba la bkod pa dang / gzugs can mi rnams kyi 'dir snang
phun tshogs kyi bde ba la 'tshe bar rtsom pa'i gzugs med bgegs kyi gnod pa las bskyabs pa'i 'gro ba pho mo drag zhan bar pa khri dang nyis stong tsam/ tshe mthar mi gtong
ba'i bar chad 'chi bdag grong kha nas phyungs te bde bar mthar phyin pa dang / gzhan yang 'gro ba pho mo klu'i nad kyis btab pa mang po la phyag rdor me dbang dang bcas
pa/ nA ga rakSha/ seng ge sgra sogs kyi gnyen po'i rjes gnang / klu nyid nad las gsos pa'i thabs gdon grol gyi cho ga rgyas par sgrub pa sogs kyi mi dang klu nyid bde ba'i
go skabs thob pa dang / tshe 'di'i 'du byed rdzogs te nam zhig dus mthar gtugs pa'i 'gro ba pho mo grangs med pa la tshe dbang re byas pas de ring tsam mi gnas pa yang
lo zla zhag sbrel nas tshe bsrings te thub pa dang / chos byed kyi 'gro ba pho mo mtha' yas pa rnams la lam du mi 'gro ba'i bar chad

zhugs pa mang po la gegs sel bogs 'don gyi dmigs thun re'am/ rdo rje 'chang nas rtsa ba'i bla ma dam pa'i bar gyi mtshan nas brjod de bgegs la bka' bsgos pas de 'phral bgegs
las grol zhing gol sa las bzlog ste mthar phyin/ gzhan yang bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad dang / gdon nyis stong dang bcas pa'i sner ba la gnyen po gang la gang 'phrod kyi
dbang rjes gnang gtor ma sngags chu gsang chu byin rlabs bsrung ba sogs byas pas dngos de kun gyi bdud las grol ba'i 'tsho mdzad sman pa rkyang par bzhugs pa mang po byung
mod/ mdor na skyes thog 'di nyid mthong thos reg pa kun gyis mthong bas grol ba 'di ma gtogs yi ger bzhag pas dgos pa med/ da phyin snyigs ma'i dus su 'khrungs pa'i gdon
'di rnams kyi 'gro ba'i lus la ji ltar byas pa yong ngam snyam pa'i zhe mtsher tsam gda'/ gzhan yang 'gro drug gang gis lus rten 'jig pa'i 'phral rkyen de dang de la gnyen
po 'phrod pa byung na de dang de min na phyi mar phan pa'i gzhan rkyen stobs chen byas pa ni bgrang ba'i ra ba las 'das/ gnas gang du sdod kyang dus kun nye 'khor du
gnas pa'i ser gzugs rnams kyi spyod pa zhi drag ci byed kyang rang rang spyod tshul dang mthun pa'i legs nyes thams cad rang gnas su tshang bar byas te bde ba'i ngang du
lhod de bzhag /gzhan yang tshe 'di'i spun du gyur pa'i ming po de nyid lo nyer lnga pa la pha rol tu phyin/ bdag dang las kyi 'brel pa phran du ma rdzogs bar slar mi'i lus
rten zhig blangs/ smra shes tsam na ma de'i ya khud du gyur nas bzhi mdor bskyal/ de

bdag gi rtsar sleb snying nas mi bzod pa'i brtse bas mchi ma 'khrug /phyi nang kun gyi 'di 'dra la bdag rkyen byed pa zer/ nged kyis 'di tsug yin de 'dra ma zer snying rje'i
yul 'di ltar/ pha mas ni bor/ smra ni mi shes/ mgon skyabs byed mi ni med/ 'di lta bu la snying rje ma nus na theg chen gyi sems bskyed yang nyams 'gro/ lhag par bdag gis
ma skyabs na gzhan mgon skyabs byed mi su yang med byas/ don la yang de ga yin/ skam sar gnas pa'i bya ri dwags dud 'gro'i 'gro ba 'bu srin chur gnas pa'i nya lcong sbal
ba sogs sems can gyi lus rten grangs med pa'i srog skyabs sogs dngos su sems can gyi don la rang srog las gces par 'dzin pa'i blun po snying khams can zhig lags so/ /bdun
pa skam chags kyi rtag 'dzin mtha' dag bzlog pa dang / tshe sgrub kyi mchog gyur sbyin pa'i phar phyin bskyang tshul la/ sangs rgyas la skyabs su song ba'i thugs rjes
rang nyid lto gos ma 'phongs tsam 'di ga yin mod/ de yang rang nyid pho skyes gyi 'bras bu ni ma lags/ skyabs bslu med dkon mchog gsum gyi ngo bo mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug
gi sku drin kho na las gnas gang du sdod kyang 'byor pa'i phun tshogs gzhan smon med tsam gda' ste/ bsam bzhin du shes pa skyo/ 'ga' zhig ni dad pa'i khungs kyis mi phod
bzhin du sbyin pa dang / 'ga' zhig ni chos bshad nas nor 'dod pa med kyang kha khyad kyis phran bu sbyin pa dang / 'ga' zhig ni mchi ma can gyi me bzhin du btsal nas
sbyin pa'i nor dngos man pa med/ 'di lta bu'i zas gos btung bas 'tsho dgos pa'i

tha chad dang 'dra snyam snying gnas nas 'thon 'gro ba snyam yong gi 'dug /phyi ma ni bsams pas kyang snying rtsa 'gul/ phran bu bzas pa btung ba tsho yang rtags mtshan lo
zlar ma 'gyangs pa yong gin 'dug /'di 'dra'i rgyu dngos ni sus spyad kyang dmyal ba'i rgyu sgrub pa kho na bla ma lnga bcu pa las gsungs 'dug pas de phyin dag pa'i zhing
khams rab 'byams na bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba thams cad dus gcig tu mchod pa dang bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu thams cad yun du gnas pa dang / rab dkar las kyi 'phreng ba dri ma med
pa'i smon lam gyi srad bus brgyus pa'i dpal ldan bla ma dam pa mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi thugs dgongs sgrub pa'i phyir dang / ltos bcas kyi skye 'gro kun gyi bsam
pa'i re ba mthar phyin par bya ba'i don dang / re ltos dang bral ba'i dmigs yul mngon med thams cad myur du phyir mi ldog pa'i sa lam thob par smon pa dang / rang nyid skye
ba nas tshe rabs kun tu bde bar ma gyur kyang bla'i/ de thams cad kyi don du lo bcu gsum nas da lta yan gyi rang nyid gang brtse ba'i rgyu dngos kun bla ma la 'bul ba
dang / zas lhag rnams gzhi gang bzung gi chos sde mi sde rnams su mang ja 'gyed sogs dang / bstan pa rin po che nam gnas kyi bar du chos lung du cho 'phrul chen po'i dus
la thugs tshugs nas 'gyed dang bcas pa/ dgon gsar dang / dpal grang mo cher rje btsun bla ma'i nyer gcig mchod la rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub pa'i mchod pa dang / shing
mangs dang / rtse dkar dang / shar ri sbug rnams su yar ngo tshes bcu'i mchod par thugs rje chen po

nyon mongs rang grol gyi 'phrin las dang bcas pa'i mchod pa'i ji srid gnas kyi bar du yod pa dang / ngam rings chos sde chen po/ bzang ldan/ thub bstan rnam pa gnyis su mang
ja/ 'dren pa gong bzhugs la bsngo ba'i rten yang dag /gser mdog can/ dpal ldan sa skya/ kha'u skye lhas rnams su mang ja/ dge 'dun bcu phrag re la dar bzang kha gru'i 'gyed/
sprin dkar gyi phung po ched du gtibs pa lta bu'i ras bzang gi 'gyed/ dpal ldan bla ma'i tshogs la brgya 'bul gyi bsngo rten/ gnas de dag gi rten rnams la snyan dar
dang bcas pa lan cig ma yin par yang yang dang / gzhan yang gnas 'di nyid sogs dgon gzhis gang bzung gi chos sder mang ja/ bcu phrag re la dkar yol gyi 'gyed/ gsum gsum
la dar bzang gi 'gyed/ de sogs gos lag /ras kyi tshogs/ zangs/ lcags/ thab gdan spyad kyi 'gyed pa/ rje bla ma'i dus sam/ sangs rgyas kyi dus sam/ nyi zla gzas bzung ngam/
nyi ma log pa'i lo 'go'i dus dang bstun mang ja dngos po brab brab kyi 'gyed pa/ khro zangs sogs lugs su 'gyur ba rnams gshin po kun gyi don du dge 'dun gyi tshogs khro
dang kong bu sogs mchod rdzas dpag med bzhengs pa dang / gtsug lag 'di sogs su mar me'i 'phreng ba kho ra khor yug tu chu bo'i rgyun bzhin du btsugs pa dang / lha sde mi
sde kun gyi mgo rer 'bru'i 'gyed dang / dbul po'i bu phal che ba'i ma 'dres pa'i mdza' bshes byas zas gang 'phrod kyis re ba bskang ba dang / chos snying nas dran pa'i lto
gos kyis phongs pa kun la blo'i re ba phul du phyin pa sogs mdor na sbyin pa rnam pa

bzhi'i sgo nas rgyal po'i btson rar tshud pa'i skye bo'i don mi dang dud 'gror bcas pa'i srog skyabs/ chos kyi sbyin pas dmigs pa med pa'i sems can thams cad tshim pa dang
/ zang zing gi dngos pos phyi nang thams cad tshim par byas pa sogs kyi sgo nas/ ster sbyin byed po rnams dang dmigs yul ltos par bcas pa kun gyi don du bsags pa don yod
pa'i dgos pa de tsam mo/ /da lta ni rang nyid 'chi ba nam yong ngam snyam pa'i mi rtag pa'i lcag gis bskul/ ma gyur mkha' mnyam sems can gyi don du rtse gcig tu byang chub
sgrub pa la gzhol ba 'di lags so/ /brgyad pa bstan pa srid mthar rgyas pa'i slad du gsung las 'khrungs pa'i bshes gnyen gyi tshogs byon pa ni/ mdo sngags gsar rnying gi
rgyud sde mtha' dag la mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes pa snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa rgya mtsho lta bu'i mnga' bdag tshul khrims kyi phung pos rgyud yongs su mdzes shing shes
bya'i mkha' la mkhyen rab kyi gzi 'od 'bum phrag 'gyed pa'i sngags 'chang chen po rje btsun dbon rin po che dbang phyug rab brtan grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/
rje btsun mchog gi dbang po'i rgyal tshab dam pa mkhan bslab gsum dbang phyug /shes bya'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dag la bsnyengs pa mi mnga' ba lung dang rigs pa smra ba kun gyi
bdag nyid chen po rnam dpyod blo gros kyi bum pa gzhal du med pa kun dga' blo gros bzang po/ byang chub sems kyis dus kun 'tsho ba chos lung gi gdan sa pa dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan/ mdo rgyud rgya mtsho lta bu'i pha rol tu son zhing snyan brgyud

bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'phags nor bdun gyis phyug pa'i rje ngag gi dbang phyug /mkhas btsun du ma'i ral pa'i khri la zhabs kyi padma ngal 'tsho ba lung rigs rgya mtsho'i mnga'
bdag 'jam dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes gnyen/ rje btsun chos rje rin chen sgang drung rab pa/ grub mchog thang stong rgyal po'i gdung brgyud byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas
'gro kun thar lam du 'dren pa'i rje ngag dbang blo gsal bstan pa/ dul ba zhi ba nye bar zhi ba'i spyod pas mdzes pa rje ngag dbang nor bu/ grub chen de nyid kyi nyer gnas
kyi sras su bskrun pa'i rnam dpyod 'jam pa'i dbyangs la 'gran pa'i chos rje dkon mchog legs 'dzin/ gzhal du med pa'i yon tan rin po che la dbang 'byor pa'i byams pa shAkya
blo gros/ mdo rgyud ma lus pa'i mnga' bdag 'chi med rigs 'dzin brnyes pa'i mkhas btsun sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ de nyid kyi thugs las 'khrungs pa'i rgyud sde'i don la
blo gros kyi spobs pa brnyes pa/ shes bya'i don la blo gros kyi spobs pa gzhal du med pa gzhon nu dkon mchog grags pa/ sngags rnying ma'i theg pa nyi zla ltar gsal ba'i
nyi shar rdor gling gi slob dpon kun bzang dpal chen/ bka' gter dam chos kyi glegs bam gtsang stod grum pa yongs kyi sngags gcig rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mchog la gzhol ba
po dgon sdug legs ldan skyabs ma/ dgon chen/ phun tshogs sogs kyi sgrub chen rnams dang / gzhan yang dpal zha lu gser khang gi grang mo che'i slob dpon/ dpal 'khor chos sde
chen po'i gur pa slob dpon/ rtse gcig tu sgrub pa snying por mdzad pa'i pa

rnam dga' gdong gi slob dpon pa/ ngam ring bzhi sde'i jo gdan slob dpon rnams dang / 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ mgon po chos dbang / chos rgyal mtshan/ padma 'phel/ blo gros bzang
po sogs khams pa'i slob bu phran bu dang / gzhan yang bstan pa dang sems can gyi don nus nges kyi thun bzhi'i dge sbyor gong 'phel gyi sgrub po grangs las brgal ba dang
bcas pa yod do/ /gsum pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas ma gyur 'gro ba'i don rab 'byams byas tshul/ dngos dang brgyud nas grangs med pa'i sems can gyi don byas par rags
pa tsam du gong du brjod zin mod/ slad du yang 'khor ba ma stongs bar du lus srog thed du bor nas dmyal bar song yang gzhan don la skyo ngal med par byed pa 'di yin/ de
yang 'gro kun phan pa dang bde ba'i go skabs bla na med pa 'byung ba'i sgo ni dkon mchog gsum gyi dbu 'phang la rag pa 'dug pas/ de gsum mi nyams pa'i thabs la 'bad rtsol
dang khor yug tu dmigs pa med pa'i chos sbyin gyi bsam gtan la brtson pa 'di lags/ gang ltar bdag lta bu'i blun po la rnam thar dang bcas pa'i ngo mtshar gyi 'phreng ba
'chad rgyu ci yang med mod/ 'on kyang dad pa'i tshig gis bskul ba nan ches pas skyon thams cad gsangs nas yon tan cung zad yod pa thams cad bris pa yin/ de yang snyan dngags
sogs kyi legs legs mi shes pas tshig skyon mang po yod na gzur gnas mkhas pa rnams kyis gzigs na bzod par bzhes/ mthar thug don gyi 'bras bu gzhan nas btsal dgos pa
yang

med/ 'di nas gzhan du 'gre nyan pa yang med pas dag ma dag gi cha mchis ban rgan nga rang gi spyan sngar bshags so/ /de ltar bris pa la nongs pa'i tshogs mchis na chos srung
rgya mtsho'i spyan sngar bshags shing / dge ba'i 'bras bu sems can thams cad myur du sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob par gyur cig ces dus gsum gyi rgyal ba kun gyi ngo bo
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi zhabs rdul spyi bos len pa'i bka' 'bangs kyi tha chung rgyal khams kyi sprang po za nyal mkhan 'bru'i sngags 'chang dge slong
rdo rje 'dzin pa bsod nams chos 'phel gyi sngar byas kyi gleng mo thams cad yi ger bris pa 'di ni/ dad can gyi mi dbang mtsho sgo nas dar rgyas drung gis gser gyi maNDal
dang / chos gos rnam pa gsum sogs dngos po'i gnang sbyin dpag med bcas nan gyis bskul ba la brten/ skyag rdzun gyi gral mi 'grig bzhin du bsgrigs pa 'di ni 'dzin byed ces
bya ba chu mo yos bu'i lo zla ba bcu pa'i mkha' 'gro 'du ba'i dus tshes nyer gsum la dpal ldan grang mo che'i gtsug lag khang gi bla brang chos dbyings dkar po'i rang gi
bsam gtan khang bur sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni nye bar gnas pa dkon mchog rdo rjes bgyis pa dge bar gyur cig/ //!na maHshrI gu ru puNya dharma wardhA ya/ dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa rigs kun gyi bdag po grub pa'i 'khor lo sgyur ba'i bdag nyid chen po sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po bsod nams chos 'phel gyi ngo mtshar mdzad pa'i rnam par thar pa'am/
rtogs brjod rags pa tsam ni dam pa nyid rang gi zhal nas spel ba

de yin/ der ma bzhugs pa'i mjug rnams thung tsam brjod na/ dam pa gang gi sku'i 'phrin las gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ nam mkha'i gza' skar gyi tshogs grangs las ches
mang bar 'gro ba'i don la bkod pa du ma snang mod/ gcig gis mdzad pa'ang brjod par mi nus/ gsung gi 'phrin las gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ rab dga'i sar gnas rnams kyi
smon lam gyi mdo las/ lha yi skad dang klu dang gnod sbyin skad/ /grul bum dag dang mi yi skad rnams dang / /'gro ba kun gyi skad rnams ji tsam par/ /thams cad skad du
zhes pa ltar 'gro ba du ma'i skad du tshangs pa'i dbyangs kyi chos sgo brgyad khri bzhi stong tshig gis 'doms par gnang mod/ gsung zer phra mo'i don yang brjod par dka'/
thugs kyi 'phrin las gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ dbang chen rin po che'i sa gzhi lta bu'i skye gnas bzhi'am/ rigs drug gi 'gro ba mtha' dag gi rten dang dpung gnyen
du gyur pa yin mod/ 'dom gang tsam gyi yon tan kyang brjod par dka'/ yon tan gyi 'phrin las gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ nam mkha'i mtha'a'am rgya mtsho'i gting la gzhal
ba dang dpag par sus kyang nus par dka' mod/ bug pa chung ngu'i tshad la gzhal ba'am chu thigs tsam gyi cha shas kyang brjod par mi nus/ 'phrin las kyi 'phrin las gsang
ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ sa chen po'i rdul gyi grangs dang mnyam pa'i 'gro ba'i don rab 'byams la dus kun slu ba med par gang la gang 'dul gyis 'khor ba ma stongs bar
du mdzad mod/ rdul phran gcig tsam gyi don la brjod par ma nus so/

/'on kyang de lta bu'i rje btsun bla ma dam pa gang gi sku gsung thugs yon tan 'phrin las kyi mdzad pa rab 'byams bdag lta'i so skye rnams kyis bskal par lce brgyas 'bad kyang
brjod par nus pa ma yin no/ /'o na bla ma dam pa'i bka' drin snying la dran pa dang dam pa gang gi sku gsung thugs mtsho las 'khrungs pa'i dri bsung phyogs brgyar dgod
pa'i utpa la'i sdong po'i bsil grib la nyon mongs pa'i tsha gdung ngal gso ba'i ser gzugs za nyal 'chag gi blun po'i snying la/ lo 'dab 'bras bu'i khur gyi rnam par 'gying
ba'i yon tan rin po che bde ba chen po'i utpal gang gis/ byams pa chen po smon pa shes rab kyi gzhu mo la thabs snying rje chen po 'jug pa'i mda' mos yang yang du bsnun
pa la brten nas/ rang bzo dang sgro skur gyi dri ma ngan pa thams cad gsung gi bdud rtsi'i dwangs ma lhad ma zhugs par/ brjed ngas dang le lo'i mun pa dang thang la rig
pa'i sgron me sems kyi lcags gis bskul te/ dam pa'i gsung las byon pa ni 'di ltar/ de yang thams cad 'dul zhes pa me mo phag gi lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la gza'
phur bu dang skar ma bi rdzis rlung gi sbyor ba la 'khrungs pa nas sa mo yos bu'i lo zla ba bcu pa'i nyer gsum bar gyi thos bsam sgom sgrub 'chad nyan gyi mdzad pa rlabs
po che mtha' dag ni gong du smos pa ltar ro/ /de'i mjug rags pa ni/ da dad rdzas gshin rdzas kyi longs spyod la thab su bzang 'gran pa ni rang gzhan thams cad phung la
sbyor zhing ngan song rgyu sgrub pa 'di 'dra bor/ 'chi ba snying zug gi gnas

rang dbang 'dus pa zhig tu sdod dgos pa 'dug /khyod rlung gis khyer ba'i skabs nas/ gong du zhu ba phul nga la sdod gnas shig gsang ba'i tshul gyis 'chos gsung ba dang du blangs
so/ /de la rnam par sun 'byin pa'i dam pa'i thugs dkrugs pa la gcig tu dpa' ba gsang ba'i dgra bo 'dras zhi drag gi byed pa yod kyang zag 'phel bas bzhi mdo'i rtswa
ltar bor/ da shi na yang blo bde chos kyis gzugs kyi don thams cad ni grub/ sngar yod kyi kho bo'i lag tu phyin pa'i longs spyod thams cad ni don ldan du 'gyur ba de yin/
tshe mjug 'dir ltogs 'khyags nas shi na yang 'gyod pa bral/ ma shi bar bsdad kyang bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa ni 'byung bas gtugs nas mi 'dug /na so'ang dus mthar
sleb rten bzheng sogs phran bu de tsho yang grub/ mtsho sgo ba'i dar rgyas drung gi bzhed pa ltar/ sprang po'i bde sdug gi gtam rnams kyang thar thor zhig grub/ lkog zhal
spangs pa'i nye 'khor 'di pa'i byed lugs 'di tsho dang / gang la bsams kyang da lo sdod pa dka' gsung / de lta bu'i gsung mi phebs pa zhu/ bla ma dam pa bzhugs phyin bstan
pa dang sems can la phan pa de yin zhus/ gang ltar snyan brgyud kyi gdan sa 'di tshor bstan pa 'di la mdung chig 'dzin byed pa zhig e yong snyam pa'i lhag bsams byas
lan cig ma yin par blangs kyang thog tu mi 'gro ba 'di bstan pa 'di nyams 'gro ba'i rgyu ru 'dug /lar bstan pa 'dir dar rgud phran bu dang snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa 'di
la 'phel 'grib dum pa

'dug pa nas/ rten bzheng sogs dang smon lam yid kyi re ba gang gi skabs su/ dar rgud gang che sar de la nan tar mdzod gsung ba 'dug pas/ bla ma brgyud pa'i skabs su ched du
'bung ba gang lcogs byas mod/ gang ltar gshin rje'i sku 'di la las sbyor lan cig byas de rjes gshegs su gsol ba'am mi mngon par sbas na ched du 'di phan pa 'dug ste/ nga
ni rgas 'dug gzhan ni sngags par khas 'che yang 'di phyogs kyi lag len dang gdams ngag skor la bar do'i gnas su sleb pa dang 'dra gsung / de ltar yin na bstan pa rin po
che la dgongs nas gnang 'tshal/ rdzas sogs mthun rkyen bdag gis byed lags phul nas/ dpe la nan tar ltos bsnyen pa zhig kyang song bas da lo e 'grub lta ba yin no/ 'on kyang
'grub pa dka' gsung ba de'i thog tu song ngo / /babs sde pa 'dul lags 'di sa gnas kyi byang chub sems dpa' zhig yin pa 'dug pas rab tu byung na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa
la bya ba phul du phyin pa zhig yong ba 'dug ste da lam phan par ma gyur pas sems thang chad pa'i ngal gsos thabs mi gda'/ nyin mtshan med par chos bshad 'jig rten gyi
bzhed dgu'i gang phan byas kyang snyan brgyud kyi bstan pa 'di'i sgros ma nyams bar 'dzin pa'i slob bu ni nyin mo'i skar ma ltar dkon pa nas sgyid pa lug /zhabs drung yab
sras rnams kyi bu slob kyi khul nas nga las zhan pa med kyang 'chad nyan thebs ma chag tsam 'di byas pas snyan brgyud phyogs re tsam ma chad pa 'di yin/ khyod rang shes
rab ni a tho 'dug da tshod bzung nas sgrub pa

'dra byas na tshe mjug bstan pa la phan pa dag kyang srid de/ bstan pa 'dzin pa las bud med kyi sems 'dzin pa dga' gsung / thugs kyi khrel ba dpag med gnang byung bas nga 'dra
ba la 'di 'dra'i thugs kyi re ba snyam sems la sdug bsngal bzod glags med pa byung / de ltar na sgrub pa byed lags pas snyan brgyud kyi chos ma thob pa 'di tsho gnang
dgos zhus pas/ de ga byed de phyis gda' gsung / de nas zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes gcig la lo gsar byed gsung / ja nag rtse nas rang re kun la skol/ nga'i rtsar khyed rang
tshang ma shog gsung / bzhes spro'i rnam grangs du ma gnang ba la/ bdag gis da lam lo gsar gyi sa 'dul byas rting ma lo gsar chen mo mdzad dgos zhus pas/ de ga byed khyed
tsho zo a gsung / tshes bcu la spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub mchod 'di'ang byed dgos pa 'dug pas de lugs shoms shig des sgrub mchod 'di'i mjug byed do gsung ba dang / de nas
btsun pa byed mi zhig kyang byung bas da lta shog gsung khyod kyi ming la ci zer pha ma yod dam gsung ming mgon po rnam rgyal zer pha ma mi bdog lags zer bas/ de ga yin
'o cag 'dra ba 'dug pa khyod 'jig rten la skyo ba skyes nas btsun pa byas/ nga 'khor bas sun kyang da dung zhen pa ches 'dug /da nga'i rtsar btsun pa byed pa'i gzhug ma
khyod kyis bgyis gsung pas/ de ring bka' lung gang man rkyang pa'i mi gsung ba zhu lags phul bas/ a pho khyed tsho rtag tu sdod pa'i 'du shes 'di ga nga la mi 'dug /skyes
zin pa nas 'chi ba'i bya gtong

pa'i skad drag po 'di snying la lcags gzer btab pa tsam 'dug /khyod tsho la 'di 'dra'i tshul bsams mi dgos pa re dga' gsung ba dang da lo dgon pa 'di tsho'i 'khri ba 'di yang
bcad snyam kyang / rtsis mi sprod par gtan du 'dzin snyam pa'i ham can 'dra 'dug kyang 'dzin rgyu ma byung na ngo tsha yo gsung ba sogs thugs 'byung ba'i bka' yang yang
phebs pa zhig 'dug kyang mi srid snyam pa ma gtogs gor ma chag /gang ltar tshes bcu'i mchod pa rgyas par gnang spyan ras gzigs kyi bzlas pa'i dus su bod yul mun pa'i gling
'dir 'phags pa 'di nyid kyi smon lam gyi dbang gis gdul bya'i zhing yin pa dang gu ru chos dbang gis ayon la chos gsan pa'i rnam thar mnal lam mar/ gu ru dpal dbyangs
thugs rje chen po'i 'phrin las kho na snang ba la/ ji tsug lags zhus pas srin po sdig shas che bas yin rgyal ba gcig gi dkyil 'khor du rgyal ba kun gyi 'phrin las btang
bas chog /khyed bod rnams kyang sdig pa chung rgyu med pas de ltar byas na 'thad gsung ba ltar/ ngas sngar phan la 'phags mchog 'di'i dkyil 'khor bsgrubs shing mchod pa dang
'jug cing dbang blang ba khri khrag lnga kha ral song / de rjes 'jug 'dras byed mi byung na bod spyi 'di la phan pa dang rang rang sdig pas 'jigs pa mtha' dag las skyob
pa 'dug kyang byed mkhan mi 'dug /'di las lhag pa'i ba rdzi ma zhig sgrub snyam pa tsho nam mkha'i mtha' 'tshol ba snang ngo gsung / de nas tshes bcu bzhi la rje ngag
dbang drung ri khrod shing mang gi gdan sa bkod pa'i bka' lung phebs pas/ spyir

bla ma'i 'dod pa ye med pa dang lhag par skye ba mi mthun pa nas/ dgongs pas grol ba dgos zer ba la de ltar ma gsung / 'jig rten na bu dang chos la slob ma yin phyin rten 'brel
gyi cha yang yod gsung bas de ltar snang ngo / /phyi nang gi las mgon gyi rjes gnang sogs byed do gsung zhal bzhes gnang / de nas tshes bco lnga la rnam thar gyi ljags
lung gong nas zhal ngos dbu mdzad bu slob rags bsdus thog cig la gnang / de nyin gyis chos thun grol dgongs thun la phebs khar/ rnam thar gyi lung dgos zer ba nga gang
zer lta ba yin pa 'dra gsung / de 'dra ci yin lags zhus pas/ nga la rnangs med kyang gsar rnying gi rgya bod kyi bla ma brgyud pa ji snyed dang de dang mtshungs pa'i rgyud
sde bzhi'i yi dam zhi khro dam can rgya mtsho 'das pa dang 'jig rten pa'i srung ma mang po yod pas/ de rnams la nyams gso ba'i phyir dang / phyi nang gi rten 'brel gang
'grig byed dgos pa la ma byung song / nga rang gi byas na shes 'dod langs pa ltar yod snyam pa byung / gter sbyin 'di tsho las tshogs 'khor zhig byas na lo re lo gnyis
rten 'brel zhig bdog ste phaT gsung / 'o na sang nyin tshogs 'khor zhig dang bskang gso 'dra yang byas na yong lags sam zhus pas snga ma dgos pa rting ma byas pas ci la phan
da de ga yin mi byed gsung / ltas ji ltar bda' lags zhus pas/ go rgyu med labs kyang thang chad pa las mi 'dug 'chi ba'i rtags mang po 'dug gsung byung bas/ zhabs pad
brtan pa bka' drin che dgos brtan bzhugs zhig kyang 'bul zhus pas

ro mgo med pa la bcos thabs yod na de ga mdzod gsung / 'on kyang gsang la kha rog sdod gsung ba tsam byung kyang blo la bde ba'i go skabs ma byung / da sku rim 'dra mdzad dgos
pa 'dra zhus pas rim gro'i mtha' rdzogs nas med/ nga las gzhan phyug pa yod sbyin pa'i mtha' ma de yin/ nga la yid la yod pa gang yang lag tu ma blangs kha la ma byin
par zur 'then kho na byed pa zhig 'dug ste ltos a gsung thugs chad pa du ma gnang byung bas/ ci bya gtol med du gyur pa zhig byung ba sogs de skor mtha' yas pa'i bka' phebs
pa zhig 'dug kyang 'dir dgos med du zad pas ma spros/ gang ltar de grol nas sgrub pa chen po bka' brgyad kyi thugs dam zab skor gnang ba'i dus mdzad kyang slob ma rnams
gzhan dbang du shor nas ma byung ngo / /zla ba de nang gi tshes bco brgyad la babs sku 'khrugs kyi gzhi ma phran bu yod pa'i steng du sku grib la nyen pa'i sku khams nyog
tshad pa tsam byung ba'i ngang nas slar yang don du gnyer ba mang po la rnam thar gyi ljags lung tshar gcig gnang / sku khams kyang dngas mur byung skabs bzhugs yul gyi
'phro 'di tsho dang lha khang gi ldebs ris 'di rnams bsos 'phral byed dgos pa 'dra bas tshon rtsi 'dra rtsol grub byed dgos pa 'dra zhus pas/ khang pa ru ni su sdod pa
sdod nga sdod pa'i nges pa ni med ldebs ris rnams sus mdzad kyang stabs bde mod/ ngas ni grub pa'i lugs yin gsung mdor na phyogs du ma nas bka' lung phebs pa la snying khong
lcags la byas pa'i bred po khos gor ma chag go /

lar de lo mchod yon sdebs cig tu sku dog chen po 'dug pas/ gong du zhabs drung ma chen sku khams shin tu nyog pa zhig byung ba nas/ dam pa nyid la phebs bzhud kyi gdan 'dren
nan 'bul zhus pas/ bdag kyang khams bde mo mi 'dug ste shi na yang 'gro dgos/ sde pa 'di nyid sde pa sgar pa'i rnam 'phrul yin/ nga de'i dus rdo ring rin po che'i gra pa
zhig yin nged gnyis smon lam gyi dbang gis 'dir 'dus pa yin/ de'i skabs su sde pa de'i phun tshogs la glags lta ba'i rgya 'dre ma rungs pa de la rdo ring rin po ches skrad
gzir byas pa'i lan chags rnyog par 'dug /nga dam pa de'i gsung rgyun lhad ma zhugs pa 'chad mkhan yin pas lan chags 'jal par 'gro gsung / zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tshes
gcig la bla ma drag po'i bskyed rim gyi ting nge 'dzin la zhugs nas lha 'dre mi gsum tshang ma 'dar khril le ba'i ngang nas rtser phebs/ byin rlabs kyi zil ma bzod pa'am
'di ltar dam pa 'di nyid la 'o brgyal 'di 'dra'i dus kho na mdzad dgos bdag gis zhu ba snyam yus kyi rgyal ba'am skyengs pa lta bu'i tshul gyis zhabs drung nyid spyan chab
mang du sil ba la/ de tsug mdzad mi dgos thugs bde 'bol mdzod ngas khyed bsams nas lus srog thed du bor nas yong ba lags gsung / dbu la phyag gi byil byil gnang / nga las
skyid pa med snyam pa'i rbad kham mdzod gsung thugs dbyung gzengs bstod mdzad/ zhabs kyis dbu la bsnun brgyud pa'i bka' bsgo'i mthar 'di snang phun

tshogs la glags lta ba thams cad phyi'i rgyal mtsho'i mthar skrad pa dang / phyi ma byang chub kyi sa lam la bar du gcod pa thams cad zhi ba'i 'phrin bcol dang bcas pa rgyas
par gnang / rim pas sku nyid dngas pa'i 'go tshugs/ tshes gsum gyi nyin sku tshe'i bar chad thams cad zhi ba dang bsring ba'i phyir tshe dbang lcags sdong ma brgya tshar
gnang ba'i phyed tsam song ba na dam pa nyid thugs mi non pa lta bu'i bun ne ba zhig byung ba nas sku bser lta bu yin nam zhus 'jam phran bu tsam mdzad bka' dbang rdzogs
par gnang / da zhabs drung rang 'jig rten na bde ba gang yang mi 'dug mod 'on kyang nga nyid las lhag pa med snyam lhod de bzhugs/ cung zad yer ba'i grabs byung na thugs
dbang chen rin po che gser gyi sa gzhir phab la de'i ngang la zhig ge zhog mdzod gsung bslab ston gnang / thugs dam spros bcas rnams kyang spros med kho na'i ngang la yun
ring du har re bzhugs pa gnang / sku 'khor yong ba'i skya ser kun la/ kho de tsho 'jig rten 'di la snying po e 'dug /ma Ni re bgrongs dang gsung ba lan cig ma yin par
gnang / mdor na tshe 'di la zhen log gi bka' lung 'ba' zhig gnang ngo / bka' dbang phyed tsam song ba'i dus thugs la ji ltar bzhed pa byung lags zhus pas/ ri bo po ta la
nas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi gnang ba yin zer ba'i khye'u dkar po ral pa'i cod pan cung zad yod pa dar dmar po'i ang rag byas pa me tog dkar po'i se ral kha dang lag
na dung dkar po dang padma dkar po khyer ba

zhig gis/ nga la rgya phyag sdam nas tshe zan gyi bum pa'ang 'chor la nye ba phyung / kun mkhyen rong pos se sdong can khrid nas rgya nag la klog song ba gzigs lags sam zer
'dug /rgod bro sde pa 'di'i sku rim la mnan pa zhig med ka med 'dug kyang mi 'grub pa 'dug /da lam sku khams gzhi med du dngas pa yod pa 'dug pas blo bde/ khye'u de nyid
'phags pa'i snang ba ni e yin mi shes nga la khyod kyi gdul bya'i zhing khams yin zer lung pa thams cad nags rong 'ba' zhig byas pa 'dra dang chu bo kho nas bskor ba'i lung
pa mang po dang lung phran ji snyed ston par byed pa zhig byung / de bar la nga la rlung yin byas pa 'dra don la de ltad mo la yongs pa yin gsung / mi gzhan la ma zer
gsung pa tsam gnang mod/ bka' dbang de'i ring la brgya tshar cung ma song lags sam zhus kyang brgya tshar song / ngas grangs tig tig byas pa 'di lags gsung phyag 'phreng
ston pa gnang / don la yang song ba de gar gda'/ tshes lnga la gsung las byon pa'i sras kyi mchog gyur rje btsun ngag dbang drung ri khrod shing mang gi gdan sar phebs pa'i
bslab ston zhu bar phebs/ da lam shing mang la khor pa byon slar dgon par phebs nas phyi nang gi las mgon sogs chos gang yong byed pa yin no/ /lugs gnyis sbrel ba'i dpon
po 'di pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyab dpung mdzad pa'i dus zhig yong bas drag sngags kyi 'khor lo rgyun chad med par rtag tu bzla ba gal che/ bdag kyang khams bde rgyu rang

mi 'dug pas yun ring sdod du dka'/ thugs dam dang bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya cher mdzod/ 'am bu shi na yang kha chems mdzod/ ma shi na yang bslab ston gyi dngas
ma yin gsung lung bstan stsal/ mdor na mi bzhugs pa kho na'i dgongs pa mdzad gda'/ slar yang rje drung gis sku khams kyi tsho 'dzin sogs zhu cha 'dra 'bul gyin gda' bas
lan mi gsung par lta ba spros bral kho na la zim me 'jog pa gnang gda'/ de nub sa srib tsam la sku nyid gsang ba'i dus kho de sngar phan nga la sri ngan pa 'di 'dra ye yong
ma myong ste 'on kyang da lo a ma'i lo sri dang zhabs drung mkhyen brtse'i drung gi lo dus kyi sri dang sgor ma nas nga mi sdod pa 'dug /da sde par zhus na thugs khral
che bas ma zhu/ sang nyin dgon par 'gro zhus shog /lo mang ga nas sdong de ring sang mi 'chi ba'i nges pa mi 'dug gsung / mi tshe chos la bskyal ba'i khung yin pas rdzong
sogs khyim nang du shi na de 'dra las blun pa med gsung / sang dgon par phebs pa'i bslab ston rnams zhus/ tshes bdun la sde pa'i drung du bzhugs gral rgyas par mdzad gsol
'degs 'bul chas rnams ni lha'i dpal 'byor la 'gran zla bral ba 'dug /phebs kar zhabs dbang dang brgyud pa'i bka' bsgo rgyas par mdzad rjes/ sku tshe 'di nyid du nad gdon
bar du gcod pa thams cad zhi ba dang / tshe dang dpal 'byor thams cad rgyas pa dang / skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du thugs rje'i skyabs 'og chud pa'i 'phrin las bcol
ba drag tu mdzad/

'jig rten phyi ma'i bslab bya la/ zhabs drung rang da lam sku khams dga' mo yod gda'o/ /rgyal srid chos bzhin du skyongs/ thugs dam gong 'phel dang / g.yog po la byams brtse
dang ma bral ba'i skyong rdar mdzod/ 'am bu la thugs 'phreng mi dgos sku khams kyi 'tsho skyong gang yong mdzod gsung / don la 'bral mi phod pa tsam mdzad nas dgon par
phebs/ de nub ras phran bu zhig las 'dug pas 'di tsho dge 'dun la phul gtong gsung / ka shi ka'i ras 'ba' zhig gi dge 'dun re la kha re'i 'gyed/ bla ma yab sras so so'i gdung
dang sku 'dra la snyan dar sogs kyi zhal bkod gnang / tshes brgyad la mang ja 'gyed chas/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi brgyud pa rin po che'i lha khang du las kyi gshin rje
dang / dpal ldan lha mo nyid la snyan dar dang thugs dam gtor gzhi 'dzugs pa gnang / bskang gso brgya tshar re'ang mdzad pa'i phyed lhag tsam song ba na/ ngas gtor ma 'dzugs
pa dang bskang gso byed pa'i mtha' ma yin pas/ lha mchog khyed kyis byin gyis rlobs shig /sa lam gyi bar chad srung shig gsung byung bas/ bstan pa dang sems can gyi
don dang bdag sogs gdul bya'i tshogs la dgongs nas de ltar mi gsung ba zhu/ da lan tshes bco lnga la brtan bzhugs kyi gsol 'debs kyang byed rtsis yin lags zhus/ de ga mdzod
dang gdan gzhan na'ang bshams gda' gsung / de nas bskang gso'i mjug rdzogs pa dang nyi ma phyed

yol tsam la snyung ba'i tshul bstan/ de skabs bsam grub nas skya ser kun gyi khrod nas gcig gnyis la chags sdang gi gdon zhugs nas/ bla ma dpon po rgyu 'bras gsum khyad du
bsad pa'i rjes mang po sngar nas kyang 'dug pa dang / de'i mig ltos ngan pas mtshams sbyar nas da lan kyang kho rang rnams 'di phyi'i don thams cad rtsa ba nas brlag pa zhig
dang / nyams grib kyis rkyen byas dam pa nyid kyi zhing khams 'di nyid stong par gyur pa'i rgyu byas so/ /de nub na bza' sogs sku rim gyi lan grangs mang du mdzad/ tshes
dgu'i snga bar sde pa 'dul lags ngam ring du phebs dgos kyi zhabs dbang zhu ba dang / sku khams kyi 'tsho skyong zhu bar phebs skabs/ byin rlabs kyi gnang byin stobs
che ba dang bcas/ ngam ring la de ring byon rgyu lags sam/ de ga lags dpon po 'di tsho las skyag pa med pas byon mdzod/ sgor ma nas rtog pa zhib mo dang lus ngag yid gsum
thugs dam la dril mdzod/ snying po gang la'ang mi 'dug pa/ bdag kyang a tho yong ngam/ ma byung bar shi yang mi tshe mthar khyongs shul na 'phrang dgos pa ni ci yang med/
chos 'go thon pa'i khungs byas 'gyod pa med gsung ba la/ bstan pa nyag pa'i dus dang sems can sdug pa'i dus 'dir/ dam pa nyid bdag sogs gdul bya mtha' dag la dgongs nas
zhabs pad brtan pa gnang dgos zhu ba la/ de ga zhu thugs 'phrang 'phrang ma mdzad par byon myur du mjal yong gsung / de nas rim par phebs rtsis mdzad pas/ nyi ma phyed yol
tsam nas

dam pa nyid mi bzhugs pa'i grabs 'dug pas/ sde pa che sa ni snyung / gcig ngam ring la phebs na mi yong ba 'dra dgongs pa mdzad par 'dug /myur du mjal gsung ba ltar phebs 'grul
ni shol dgos shar/ sman pa rnams la 'phral legs tsam du/ nga ji ltar yong ba 'dug pa tsam phebs/ rdo rje'i sku lus la 'di yong gi tshod things pa'i gshis su mi 'dug
zer/ cung zad 'jigs par snang ngo / /phyi mo nas sde pas ngam ring la ma byon pa yin nam gsung / sku khams dub tu song ba nas 'gro ma nus byung lags zhus/ he he 'am bu shi
dogs med gsung thugs gso ba gnang / tshes bcu'i snga dro gtor ma dang mchod pa shoms tshes bcu rgyas par byed gsung / rje dkon cog grags pa la/ chos rje mi 'di tsho'i byed
khyer 'di dang bdag kyang 'chi ba la thug pa 'di gar 'dug /khyed rang sgrub pa snying po nyams su long / 'am bu la ma 'gran par 'chi tsa na mi mtsher tsam re mdzod gsung
pa la/ dam pa khyed ma bzhugs na bdag ltos bcas rnams su la re ba zhabs pad brtan pa gnang dgos zhu ba la/ 'jig rten ni dpon la re ltos 'chol/ chos phyogs ni'am bu bsams
la nyams len la 'bungs mdzod/ sems can la phan pa gang nus mdzod gsung / thugs dam gyi phyag phyi byed mi rnams ni tshes bcu'i mchod pa la 'di lta bu'i dus shar ro snyam
skad kyi sang thon par ngu ba dang / dam pa nyid kyi zhal 'dzum ltas pa'i mod la mchi ma'i rgyun ni yur chu'i rgyun ltar 'bab

cing / ci bya gtol med du gyur pa byung / 'on kyang dam pa nyid zhabs pad brtan pa dag kyang srid dam snyam pa dang / tshes bcu'ang chag na mi rung snyam lus sems tshugs mi
thub kyang byed pa'i rtsis byas/ tshogs 'khor gyi skabs su babs pa tshogs 'khor rgyas par byed nga la'ang zhus/ zhabs drung dang khyed tsho rang yang yid ches par zo gsung
tshogs 'khor rgyas par gnang / de nub zhabs drung lhun chen lags kyi sku 'dra rin po che kha re la phyag nas zhus gsung snyan dbang phul bas/ mtshan la rab gnas byung
dogs med sang snga bar byed pa yin no gsung / de nas tho rang gi dus nyid na sku lus drang por bzhugs nas/ skad cig yud tsam zhig la ma bzhugs pa zhig byung bas/ slar da
lam zhing khams ji 'dra zhig la gshegs zhus pas/ shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'am po ta la yi zhing du khor tsam 'gro bsam pa byung gsung don la'ang gshegs par gda'/ tshes
bcu gcig la slar yang zhal 'dzum dang bcas phebs nas/ khyed tshos nga shi ba'i khungs byas pa e yin gsung dbugs dbyung / de nas zhabs drung gi dam pa khyed lta bu skye
'chi la rang dbang thob pa yin pas/ bstan pa dang sems can gyi dpal du slar phebs par bka' drin che zhu ba'i rten dang / bdag sogs gdul bya'i zhing khams mi gtong bar bzhugs
pa gnang dgos zhu ba gnang bas/ de ga byed gsung ba dang / phyag yod kyi byin rlabs ci 'dug thams cad tshogs gcig tu mdzad pa dang / bdag cag rje 'bangs kun la 'gyod
pa gnang /

do nub nye khor cig tu rnga rdung mi zhig byung na yong ba 'dug ste gsung / sku rim la dmigs nas drag dmar gyi gtor bzlog cig byas na e yong lags zhus pas/ da lta rang rtsoms
gtor ma 'phang mkhan khyod rang gis byas pas chog /nga la phan par ma gyur kyang phyis su sbyin bdag gi rkyen ngan bar gcod thams cad mi 'byung bar nges pas/ dmigs pa
dgos pa rnams nga rang gis byed gsung pa ltar ci gsung kun lkog gyur lung bstan du song ngo / /de ring tshes bco lnga yin ang gsung / sku mdun du byin rlabs zhu bar phebs
pas/ rje btsun ngag dbang pa dang zhal ngo rnams dang / gzhan yang skya ser su byung yang sngar las zhan du ma song ba'i phyag dbang gnang ba zhal ras la 'gyur ba mi mnga'
ba 'dug go /snyung tshul mdzad pa'i gnas skabs thams cad du'ang thugs dam zab mo'i rim pa rnams dang gsang sngags bzlas brjod mdzad pa rnams rgyun chad med par smra dag
cing rang babs su gnang ba dang sku lus kyi zo mdog kyang sngar bas dngas pa tsam byung mod/ bsams na rdo rje'i sku lus la skye 'chi dang bgres rgud sogs pha rol gyi mtshan
ma ngan pa gang yang med par gda'o/ /gang gi tshe dpal rgyal ba sras dang bcas pa kun gyi yab/ grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po dkyil 'khor kun gyi rigs bdag /dpa' bo dang
mkha' 'gro thams cad kyi ded dpon/ bdag sogs gdul bya mtha' dag gi skyabs mgon gcig po/ zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang dang zhal mi gnyis pa'i dam pa nyid zhing 'di nas

gzhan du gshegs par gyur pa de'i tshe/ nam mkha'i khyon thams cad li khri'i mdangs ltar dmar zhing gsal ba'i mtha' dbus kun na 'ja' sna lnga'i 'od 'khyug pa dang / gzims chung
sogs phyogs thams cad na dri bzang pos khyab cing bskyed rim mngon du gyur pa'i rtags su thugs dam zab mo mdzad pa sgra dag cing gsal bar snang / bla ma dang dkyil 'khor
gyi lha tshogs rnams dang dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i lha tshogs thams cad kyis mngon sum du bsus/ rgyal chen bzhi dang phyogs skyong bcu sogs 'jig rten skyong ba thams
