cad kyis zhabs nas bteg /gnas gsum gyi dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro/ de dag gi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyi mi khyab pa dang bcas pa'i rig pa 'dzin pa rnams kyis mdun nas bdar
te/ bde ba can sogs mkha' la spyod pa'i gnas su gshegs par chas pa'i tshe bdag cag gis sku gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor gsol 'debs cung zad phul/ shul du lus pa'i ltos
bcas sde pa bsod nams lhun po/ sde pa dgra 'dul don grub/ sde pa bsod nams dpal 'byor sogs zhal ngo brgyud par bcas pa dang / bdag sogs gdul byar gyur pa thams cad skye
ba nas tshe rabs thams cad du rjes su 'dzin pa dang thugs rje'i skyabs 'og tu nam yang mi 'bral bar rjes su bzung du gsol/ de nas kyang dam pa khyed gang du bzhugs pa'i zhing
khams su 'khor gyi thog mar skyes nas gsung gi bdud rtsi 'thung bar shog /ces gsol ba btab pas zhal 'dzum pa dang spyan ras kyis gzigs pa dang

'ja' 'od rol mo'i sgra dang bcas/ tshes bcu gnyis kyi tho rangs nub phyogs bde ba can gyi zhing khams/ dpal ri padma 'od kyi gzhal yas su ayon mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyi sde dpon
la gshegs par gyur to/ /bdag sogs gdul bya'i zhing khams 'di nyid du rje btsun chos kyi nyi ma khyed ma bzhugs pas mun pa mun nag gi khrod na shul du lus pa'i las ngan
can bdag cag rnams/ 'ga' zhig ni gsol 'debs kyi sgra dir ba 'dug /'ga' zhig ni ci bya las 'das mig rtsa hrig hrig brang lag 'thab cing 'dug /'ga' zhig ni smre sngags kyi
cho nges gnam du 'bod cing 'dre ldog drag po dang bcas gnas par gyur to/ /kye hud/ phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i rgyal ba sras bcas rnams/ /skyabs bral bdag gi smre sngags 'di
dgongs dang / /gtsug gi nor dang bral ba'i dbul 'phongs bzhin/ /mig rtsa hrig hrig da dung yid ma ches/ /khong pa'i snying dang bral ba'i smyon pa bzhin/ /thom thom lus
ni ci byed thabs dang bral/ /gnas skabs chu dang bral ba'i nya mo bzhin/ /'dre ldog grangs med 'phar kyang mgon ma rnyed/ /bslu med mgon skyabs bor ba'i las ngan can/ /bdag
las sa steng 'di na gzhan ma mchis/ /bdag gi snying 'di da dung mi 'gas na/ /lcags sam khro chu'i rdo las byas par zad/ /khyod sku tsha zer gzi 'od stong 'phro de/ /blo
bur 'chi bdag sprin gyi de ring sgrib/ /gsal la dngas pa'i sku de da ga re/ /khyod gsung bdud rtsi 'o ma'i chu rgyun de/ /ma rung rkyen ngan sa la de ring thim/ /sgra
snyan tshangs pa'i gsung de da ga re/ /khyod sku bsil zer ston zla nya gang de/ /khrel

med 'chi bdag gza' yis de ring zin/ /brjid chags lhun grub sku mchog da ga re/ /khyod gsung chu 'dzin gsar pa'i chos char de/ /skal med lho phyogs rlung pos ga gshed brdas/
/blo yul 'bab pa'i gsung de da ga re/ /khyod thugs sgrib med ye shes rgya mtsho de/ /me long chu zla 'ja' tshon ltar gsal yang / /skal med bdag gis mthong dang thos gnas
bral/ /kye ma kyi hud rje btsun thugs rje chung / /zhes re zhig yid kyi dbang po dran med du song ngo / /de nas tshes bcu gsum gyi nyi ma dgong myur la nam mkha' mthing
zhun gyi mdog lta bu la nub phyogs nas 'ja' dkar po ba thag rkyang ba lta bu'i rtsa ba gcig la rtse mo gsum du byas/ de la je mang gyes nas nam mkha' kun 'jas ris des khyab
pa'i khrod nas/ me tog sna tshogs kyi char mngon sum du thul ba skye bo kun gyis mthun grub mthong ba byung / rin thang ma mchis gzhal du med pa'i sku gdung rin po che
nyid kyi zhabs tog ni/ bslab pa gsum gyi rgyud yongs su phyug cing dam tshig gi rgyan gyis rnam par mdzes pa dkon cog rgyal mtshan pas mdzad/ de'i phyag g.yog dgos pa bdag
gis byas nas/ sku gdung rin po che nyid yid bzhin nor bu ltar snum la brjid chags shing dri bzang gis yid kyi dbang po tshim pa dang 'od dang 'od zer gyi tshogs 'phro
bzhin pa dang bcas kun tu bzang po'i mchod sprin lta bu'i dbus su bzhugs su gsol/ de nas gsol 'debs kyi zhal bkod zhabs drung 'dul lags kyis mdzad de/ thog mar tshar chen
chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung yid bzhin nor bu'i drung du snyan dar dkar me/ 'jigs byed lha khang du rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gi sku 'dra la snyan dar dang mar me/ mgon
khang du

chos skyong gi spyan gzigs lha rdzas/ gzhan yang rje btsun mchog gi sprul sku kun dga' snying po dang / bstan 'dzin nyi ma bzang po dang / dbon dbang phyug rab brtan pa dang
/ rje btsun lha dbang pa rnams kyi drung du/ dam pa nyid zhing 'di nas rgya che ba'i zhing khams gzhan du phebs pa'i sa lam gyi bar chad thams cad zhi bar zhu ba'i smon
lam gyi rten mi zhan tsam dang bcas phul/ dpal chos 'khor yang rtse'i dge 'dun rnams la mang ja zung sbrel dang bcas gsol ba btab/ phyag rdzas kyi lhag phran bu yod pa'i
steng du/ sbyin bdag stobs ldan nyid kyi dam pa gang gi dgongs rdzogs la dgongs/ ngam ring chos sde chen po nyid du mang ja nas 'bo'i 'gyed bsngo rten dang bcas pa/ chab
srid kyis dge 'dun pa drug brgya tsam dang / sgrub pa mo brgya lhag dang bcas pas kye rdor dang / 'khor lo bde mchog dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed dang / rje btsun nA ro mkha'
spyod/ sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi nang nas kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug nyon mongs rang grol gyi dkyil 'khor rnams rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor kho na byas/ zhal phye nas gsol ba btab/ de yang rdo rje 'jigs byed pa'i tshogs dbu rje btsun ngag dbang drung gis mdzad/ kye rdor pa'i tshogs dbu tshar
chen chos kyi rgyal po'i nye gnas mi phyed pa'i dad pa can bzang po rgya mtshos mdzad/ bde mchog yab bka' yum bka' rnams la rang rang gi bsnyen song gi sgrub po res bum
'dzin dang / rje byams pa shAkya blo gros drung gis kun rig pa'i tshogs dbu dang / rje dkon cog grags pas tshogs dbu mdzad nas sgrub sde rnams kyi 'phags pa nyon mongs

rang grol gyi cho ga /de yang nyi ma re la sgrub cing mchod pa dang 'jug cing dbang bskur ba dang bcas pa tshar gnyis re'i gsol ba 'debs pa dang / zhag bdun nas sta gon skyar
ba sogs brgyud pa 'di pa'i sgros thun mong ma yin pa phyag len la lhad ma zhugs pa dang bcas dgung tshigs gnyis kyi bar du gsol ba btab pa'i bar la yang me tog gi char
thul ba 'bab pa kun gyis mthong bar byung ngo / /gzhan yang 'bangs mnga' 'og tu gtogs tshad der ma 'dus pa'i skya ser pho mo thams cad la rtsam 'bo'i sbyin btang dang /
der ma zad dge 'dun gyi sde dang sgrub sde so sor mang ja rtsam 'bo sbrel po'i bsnyen bskur dang / gzhan yang chos sde sgrub sde so so nas dus rgyun dang khyad par lo dus
kyi mchod pa'i cha rkyen sogs thams cad/ rje btsun bla ma dam pa gang gi ye shes kyi gzigs pa dam pa mtshon pa'am spyan lam du 'byung zhing rgyas pa'i phyir/ gang gi sku
gsung thugs mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo las bskrun pa'i rje btsun ngag dbang chos kyi rgyal po tshogs chen gyi dbu la gdan drangs te bsngo ba'i rten dang bcas pas mthar
yongs su rdzogs par mdzad do/ /zhes yongs 'dzin dam pa grub pa brnyes pa'i dbang po 'jam dpal khro bo mi'i gzugs kyis rnam par rol pa 'bru'i sngags 'chang chen po bsod nams
lhun grub chos 'phel grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi ngo mtshar gyi mdzad pa rin po che'i kha skongs su/ dam pa nyid gdul bya'i zhing khams rgya
che ba gzhan du dgongs nas chos dbyings su gzigs pa'i rnam thar chung ngu 'di ni/ yongs 'dzin dam pa nyid kyi sku gsung thugs las 'khrungs pa'i byang chub sems

dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ mkhas pa'i dbang po thams cad kyi pha rol tu son pa se'i gdung rigs las 'khrungs pa rig pa 'dzin pa chen po dbang po'i sde/ zhabs drung 'dul drung gis
'di ltar bsgrigs gsung rgyang ring po nas bka'i zur gnang sbyin dang bcas stsal ba la brten nas rje btsun dam pa de'i bka' drin dang yon tan rjes su dran nas mi shes bzhin
du/ dam pa de dag gi zhabs pad lo bcu phrag gnyis dang dbang po'i grangs tsam brten kyang yon tan gyi dri mas ma gos pa'i ser gzugs rdo rje'i ming gis me pho rta'i lo
dbyug pa zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la bris nas phul ba/ bla ma dang mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyis bzod par bzhes la rgyud la byin rlabs 'jug par shog /thugs rje'i zhags pas 'khor
ba'i gnas nas drongs/ /byams pa'i lcags kyus khyod bzhugs zhing du khug /thabs mkhas lcags kyi sgrog des phyir mi zlog /byang chub sems kyi dril bus dbyer med mdzod/
/ces kyang smras so// //mangga laM//
